Learning Objectives | 學習目標

  • Explain why IT Infrastructure qualification is required for GxP compliance
  • Distinguish between platform qualification and application validation
  • Describe the horizontal (platform-based) approach and its advantages over a vertical approach
  • Identify the three IT Infrastructure elements: Platforms, Processes, Personnel
  • Assign GAMP categories to platform components (networks, OS, servers, clients)
  • Map regulatory requirements (21 CFR Part 11, EU Annex 11) to IT Infrastructure controls

P

Preface | 序言

Purpose and legal context of the GAMP IT Infrastructure Guide · 指南目的與法律聲明

Original Text (English)

This document, the GAMP® Good Practice Guide: IT Infrastructure Control and Compliance, is intended as a supplement to the Guide for Validation of Automated Systems (GAMP® 4). It provides an approach to meeting current regulatory expectations for compliant IT Infrastructure platforms, including the need to identify, qualify, and control those aspects impacted by GxP.

This document has been designed so that it may be used in conjunction with guidance provided in GAMP® 4 and other ISPE publications, such as the ISPE Baseline® Guides.

Disclaimer

This Guide is meant to assist pharmaceutical companies in managing the validation of IT Infrastructure platforms. The GAMP Forum cannot ensure and does not warrant that a system managed in accordance with this Guide will be acceptable to regulatory authorities. This Guide does not replace the need for hiring professional engineers or technicians.

CDMO 實務解讀

這份指南是什麼？

GAMP IT基礎設施指南是GAMP 4的補充文件，專門聚焦於支撐GxP應用程式的底層IT環境——包含伺服器、網路、作業系統、資料庫平台等。

在製藥CDMO中，IT基礎設施是所有數位化製造系統的地基。MES出問題了？先查OS patch。LIMS資料遺失？先看backup策略是否合規。這本指南就是管控這個「地基層」的標準。

建築比喻

應用程式（MES、LIMS、QMS）是建築物，IT基礎設施是地基和鋼筋。即使建築物本身設計完美，若地基不穩定，整棟建築都有崩塌風險。這份指南確保「地基」本身符合GxP要求。

思考練習

  1. 為什麼IT基礎設施指南需要作為GAMP 4的「補充」而非單獨存在？
  2. CDMO的IT部門和QA部門在閱讀此指南時，各自的關注重點會有哪些不同？
  3. 「法規當局不保證接受」這個免責聲明對你的法規策略有何實際影響？
1.1

Overview | 概述

Why IT Infrastructure control matters for GxP compliance · 為何IT基礎設施管控對GxP合規至關重要

Original Text (English)

GxP regulated companies have an ever increasing dependency on computerized systems when conducting their day-to-day businesses.

The validated status of GxP applications that are dependent upon an underlying IT Infrastructure is compromised if that IT Infrastructure is not maintained in a demonstrable state of control and regulatory compliance.

The consequences of the IT Infrastructure being out of effective control can be significant. Depending on the nature of a failure, an entire site or geographic region of operations could be brought to a standstill while the problem is resolved.

The infrastructure should be brought into initial conformance with the company's established standards through a planned qualification process building upon acknowledged good IT practices. Once in conformance, this state should be maintained by documented standard processes and quality assurance activities, the effectiveness of which should be periodically verified.

Key aspects to consider include:

  • Installation and operational qualification of infrastructure components
  • Configuration management and change control in a highly dynamic environment
  • Management of risks to IT Infrastructure
  • Involvement of service providers in critical infrastructure processes
  • Security management — access controls, availability of services and data integrity
  • Backup, restore, and disaster recovery
  • Archiving
"IT Infrastructure" and "infrastructure" are used synonymously to indicate an aggregation of platforms and services including their associated processes, procedures, and personnel. — GAMP IT Infrastructure Guide, Footnote 1
CDMO 實務解讀

核心警示：連鎖失效風險

指南明確說明：若IT基礎設施失控，整個廠區或地區的作業可能停擺。在CDMO環境中，這意味著：

  • MES停機 → 批次記錄無法建立 → 生產暫停
  • LIMS無法存取 → 放行檢驗無法完成 → 批次卡關
  • DCS/SCADA失效 → 製程監控中斷 → FDA 21 CFR Part 11 數據完整性疑慮

CDMO的IT基礎設施涵蓋範圍

  • Server infrastructure：MES、LIMS、QMS的主機伺服器
  • Network：廠區內部網路、隔離的GxP網段
  • OS/Database：Windows Server、Oracle DB等
  • Virtualization：VMware環境（若使用）
  • Storage/Backup：批次記錄的長期保存系統

關鍵定義：IT Infrastructure

IT Infrastructure（IT基礎設施） = 平台（Platforms）+ 服務（Services）+ 相關流程、程序、人員的集合體。

這個定義很重要：IT基礎設施不只是硬體，還包含圍繞它運作的流程和負責的人員。

思考練習

  1. 列出你廠區中三個依賴IT基礎設施的GxP應用程式，並描述若底層伺服器發生故障的影響。
  2. 「可示範的控制狀態（demonstrable state of control）」在法規稽查時意味著需要準備哪些文件？
  3. 為何備份（Backup）和災難復原（Disaster Recovery）被列為IT基礎設施的關鍵考量？
1.2

Purpose | 目的

What this Guide aims to achieve · 本指南的目標

Original Text (English)

This Guide provides comprehensive guidance on meeting current regulatory expectations for compliant IT Infrastructure platforms, including the need to identify, qualify, and control those aspects impacted by GxP.

This Guide intends to satisfy the growing need for guidance on key IT Infrastructure subjects in relation to current international GxP regulations, and to align terminology and language with other GAMP® Good Practice Guides.

The Guide is intended primarily for regulated life science industries, including pharmaceutical, biological, and medical devices, but also provides valuable information for suppliers of systems, products, or services.

This Guide includes the description of a scaleable qualification framework which has been derived from key principles and practices. It describes how this framework can be applied to different platform types in order to determine the extent and scope of qualification efforts.

In addition, this Guide provides an overview of current best practices for the design, qualification, and operation of an IT Infrastructure with emphasis on the qualification requirements of the major components.

CDMO 實務解讀

三個核心動作：Identify → Qualify → Control

這三個動詞定義了整個IT基礎設施合規管理的生命週期：

  • Identify（識別）：哪些IT元件支撐GxP應用程式？哪些在GxP範圍內？
  • Qualify（資格確認）：執行IQ/OQ，確認元件能滿足規格要求
  • Control（管控）：持續的變更管理、組態管理、定期審查

可縮放資格確認框架（Scaleable Qualification Framework）

框架可依據以下因素調整規模：

  • 平台的GxP衝擊程度（風險驅動）
  • 公司規模（小型CDMO vs 跨國大廠）
  • 平台類型（獨立伺服器 vs 虛擬化環境 vs 雲端）

這表示框架不是一刀切的——你可以根據風險評估調整資格確認的深度和廣度。

思考練習

  1. 「可縮放框架」對資源有限的小型CDMO意味著什麼？你會如何優先排序？
  2. IT供應商（如外包的雲端服務商）閱讀此指南後，需要承擔哪些責任？
  3. 如何確保你廠區的IT術語與GAMP指南一致，避免稽查時的溝通誤差？
1.3

Scope | 適用範圍

What is included and excluded from this Guide · 本指南的涵蓋範圍與排除項目

Original Text (English)

This Guide addresses compliance with international GxP regulations and considers:

  • The establishment of new platforms and extensions to existing ones
  • Existing platforms already in support of GxP applications

GxP regulations considered:

  • Good Manufacturing Practice (GMP)
  • Good Clinical Practice (GCP)
  • Good Laboratory Practice (GLP)
  • Good Distribution Practice (GDP)

Specific regulations and guidelines considered:

  • US FDA regulations and Compliance Policy Guides
  • Relevant parts of EU GMPs, e.g., Annexes 11, 15, and 18
  • PIC/S Guidance

This Guide covers a range of IT Infrastructures, from those found in companies operating globally to isolated or semi-isolated GxP regulated infrastructures.

Out of Scope

Business Continuity Planning is led by business users and application owners — it is outside the scope of this Guide. This Guide covers IT disaster recovery and contingency planning, but not alternative operating procedures for business processes in case of failure.

CDMO 實務解讀

適用範圍清單（CDMO視角）

涵蓋（In Scope）：

  • 支撐MES、LIMS、QMS、DCS/SCADA的伺服器和網路
  • GxP資料庫平台（Oracle、SQL Server）
  • 作業系統（Windows Server、Linux）
  • 虛擬化平台（VMware等）
  • 儲存和備份系統
  • 既有平台（legacy）和新建平台

排除（Out of Scope）：

  • MES、LIMS等應用程式本身的驗證（由GAMP 4規範）
  • 業務連續性計畫（BCP）中的替代作業程序

新平台 vs 既有平台的實務差異

  • 新平台：從需求規格開始，完整走過IQ/OQ流程，文件較完整
  • 既有平台（Legacy）：需進行回溯性資格確認（retrospective qualification），評估現況是否符合要求，補齊文件落差

許多CDMO的IT基礎設施在指南出版之前已存在，因此「既有平台」的合規路徑尤其重要。

思考練習

  1. 你廠區的哪些IT系統屬於GMP範圍？哪些屬於GLP？哪些兩者都有？
  2. 若廠區同時支援GMP和非GMP客戶，你會如何在同一IT基礎設施中進行GxP邊界劃分？
  3. 業務連續性計畫（BCP）被排除在外，但IT災難復原（DR）在範圍內——兩者的界線在哪裡？
1.4

Benefits | 效益

Advantages of the horizontal platform-based approach · 水平式平台導向方法的優勢

Original Text (English)

This Guide applies a structured approach, including Risk Management, to the qualification, management, and control of IT Infrastructure platforms supporting GxP applications.

A vertical, or system based, approach to qualification and audit of IT Infrastructure would be inefficient and impractical, as overlapping and often identical platform elements would be dealt with repeatedly. To avoid unnecessary effort, this Guide describes a horizontal, or platform based, approach.

Benefits of a horizontal approach include:

  • Higher level of standardization throughout the entire life cycle
  • Minimal overlap in documentation
  • Minimal overlap in qualification
  • Minimal overlap in audits, inspections, and assessments

The approach also builds upon:

  • The relatively low residual risk to GxP applications attributable to IT Infrastructure platforms (in contrast to application software designed to create and manipulate data)
  • Industry standard components with built-in error detection and self-correction features
  • Current good IT practices and international standards for reliable network performance
  • Efficient, automatic, standardized IT monitoring and management software tools
  • Many similar platform components used in similar configurations across a company
CDMO 實務解讀

垂直 vs 水平方法：超市收銀機比喻

垂直方法（低效）：每台收銀機都獨立稽查一次POS系統的伺服器、網路、OS——但同一台伺服器可能服務20台收銀機，結果做了20次重複的工作。

水平方法（高效）：先資格確認「收銀機共用平台」一次，後續每台收銀機的應用程式驗證只需確認「平台已合規」即可。

在CDMO中，若一台伺服器同時支援MES和LIMS，水平方法讓伺服器只需資格確認一次。

為何平台的殘留風險較低？

平台（OS、資料庫）設計目的是保護資料完整性，而應用程式設計目的是建立和操作資料。應用程式更可能引入業務邏輯錯誤，導致數據問題；平台的風險通常是可用性（availability）而非數據正確性。

水平方法的CDMO實踐

  • Standard server build：建立標準化伺服器配置包，資格確認一次後可複製部署
  • Platform qualification package：一份平台資格確認文件，多個應用程式共用
  • One audit for the platform：稽查人員只需審查一次平台文件，不需重複查每個應用程式的底層基礎設施

思考練習

  1. 若你的廠區有5個GxP應用程式都運行在同一台虛擬化伺服器上，水平方法能節省多少資格確認工作量？
  2. 「標準化元件有自我錯誤偵測功能」這個特性如何支持較輕量的資格確認策略？
  3. 水平方法在哪些情況下可能不適用（例如：特殊配置或高度客製化環境）？
1.5

Objectives | 指導原則

GAMP Council guiding principles for this Guide · GAMP委員會制定本指南的指導原則

Original Text (English)

IT Infrastructure Control and Compliance should target those IT related aspects that could potentially affect product quality and public health. In order to be effective, applicable methods also must be practical and efficient.

To this end, the GAMP® Council set out the following guiding principles:

  • Provide a consistent, standalone document that would guide stakeholders to take advantage of current best practices in the field to achieve compliance with applicable regulations
  • Define infrastructure and other key terms and concepts referenced or introduced
  • Provide guidance on best practice for network, client, and server qualification and management
  • Provide guidance on security issues in the light of BS7799/ISO17799
  • Address change control in light of virus signature updates and security patches
CDMO 實務解讀

GxP IT管控的根本目的

指南開宗明義：IT管控的目標是保護產品品質和公眾健康，而非為了技術本身。這個框架讓你在回答稽查員問題時有明確的論述基礎：「我們的每一項IT控制措施都是為了確保GxP記錄的完整性和系統的可靠性，最終保護患者安全。」

Change Control中的特殊挑戰：Patch Management

指南特別提到病毒簽名更新和安全性補丁的變更控制——這在GxP環境中是高頻率的實際挑戰：

  • 安全補丁需要快速部署（資安要求）
  • 但每次OS patch都可能影響已驗證的應用程式（GxP要求）
  • 解決方案：建立patch管理SOP，包含影響評估和快速回歸測試程序

ISO17799（現為ISO 27001）在GxP中的應用

資訊安全標準ISO17799（現已演進為ISO 27001）與GxP的IT安全要求高度重疊，尤其在：訪問控制、審計日誌、事件管理、備份程序等方面。許多CDMO同時追求ISO 27001認證和GxP合規，兩者可以共用大量管控措施。

思考練習

  1. 當資安部門要求緊急部署安全補丁，但QA要求先進行影響評估——你如何設計一個能同時滿足兩方的流程？
  2. ISO27001認證和GxP IT合規有哪些重疊之處？在CDMO中如何整合兩套要求？
  3. 「實用且高效（practical and efficient）」的目標如何影響你在小型CDMO中設計合規程序的方式？

1.7

Key Concepts | 核心概念

Horizontal approach, key terminology, qualification vs validation · 水平方法、關鍵術語、資格確認vs驗證

Original Text (English)

1.7.1 Horizontal Platform Based Approach

The IT Infrastructure exists to support the primary business, by providing:

  • Platforms to run business applications (e.g., CDMS, IVRS, LIMS, or ERP)
  • IT Infrastructure processes that facilitate a capable and controlled IT environment
  • General IT services (e.g., email, office tools, intranet, file storage)

Where platform components support multiple applications, these components should be qualified separately from the applications to avoid unnecessary duplication of activities and effort.

Separate qualification of the IT Infrastructure means that adding or changing a business application would require only the validation of the application. Similarly, changing components in the IT Infrastructure may not require further validation of the business application; however, the risk to GxP applications of each controlled change should be assessed.

Standard, re-usable, qualified platform components are referred to as building blocks throughout this Guide.

1.7.2 Key Terminology

Requirements: Often specified in documents such as Service Level Agreements (SLAs). For infrastructures supporting real-time applications (such as process control), requirement specifications may be more specific.

Commissioning: A well planned, documented, managed engineering approach to start-up and handover to end-user, resulting in a safe and functional environment meeting established design requirements. In the context of IT Infrastructures, useful for aspects that do not support GxP activities directly.

Qualification: A process of demonstrating the ability of an entity to fulfill specified requirements. Demonstrates the ability of servers, clients, and peripherals to fulfill specified requirements. Basic requirements include: QA involvement, formally verified design solutions, test results compliant with GxP documentation requirements, traceability of actions.

Validation: In the context of an IT Infrastructure, validation applies to the GxP applications that run on the infrastructure, rather than the infrastructure platforms themselves. The focus for platforms is on qualification of components.

CDMO 實務解讀
Platform vs Application 層次架構圖
GxP Applications
MES / LIMS / QMS / DCS
↕ 驗證（Validation）— 應用程式層
Database Platform
Oracle / SQL Server
OS Platform
Windows Server / Linux
Virtualization
VMware / Hyper-V
Network
Switches / Firewalls
↕ 資格確認（Qualification）— 平台層
Physical Hardware
Servers / Storage
平台（綠色）= 本指南範圍 | 應用程式（紅色）= GAMP 4範圍

Building Blocks（積木）概念

標準化、可重用的已資格確認平台元件稱為「building blocks」。

實務範例：若你建立了一套標準Windows Server配置並完成資格確認，下次部署相同配置的伺服器時，只需確認配置一致，不需重新從頭做完整IQ/OQ——大幅降低重複工作。

Commissioning vs Qualification 的區別

項目 Commissioning Qualification
適用對象 非GxP直接相關的IT元件 GxP相關平台元件
QA介入程度 較低 必須有QA參與
文件要求 工程交接文件 GxP文件（可追溯性）
測試目的 確認功能正常運作 確認符合規格要求

Qualification vs Validation：關鍵區別

Qualification（資格確認）適用於IT基礎設施平台（伺服器、網路、OS、資料庫）。

Validation（驗證）適用於運行在基礎設施上的GxP應用程式（MES、LIMS）。

稽查員問你的LIMS伺服器有沒有「驗證」時，正確答案是：「伺服器已完成資格確認（qualified），LIMS應用程式已完成驗證（validated）。」

思考練習

  1. 你廠區的Oracle資料庫伺服器同時支援LIMS和QMS，請說明如何用「building block」方法進行資格確認。
  2. 若MES供應商發布新版本，根據水平方法，IT基礎設施平台需要重新資格確認嗎？
  3. SLA（服務水準協議）在IT基礎設施的GxP合規中扮演什麼角色？應包含哪些關鍵要求？
REF

GxP IT System Classification | GxP IT系統分類表

Which systems are GxP-impacted in a pharma CDMO · 製藥CDMO中哪些系統屬於GxP範圍

GxP IT System Classification

Table: GxP-Impacted Systems in Aseptic Fill-Finish CDMO

System GxP Category 21 CFR Part 11? Infrastructure Impact
MES
Manufacturing Execution System		 GMP Yes — electronic batch records High — production-critical servers
LIMS
Laboratory Information Mgmt System		 GMP GLP Yes — lab data and e-signatures High — data integrity requirements
QMS
Quality Management System		 GMP Yes — deviations, CAPAs, change controls Medium — document management servers
DCS / SCADA
Process Control Systems		 GMP Yes — process parameters, alarms High — real-time, OT network
ERP
Enterprise Resource Planning		 GDP (partial GMP) Partial — batch traceability Medium — business network
EDMS
Electronic Document Mgmt		 GMP Yes — controlled documents Medium — document servers
CDS
Chromatography Data System		 GLP GMP Yes — analytical data High — analytical lab servers
Email / Office Non-GxP No Low — general IT
CDMO 實務解讀

GxP衝擊判斷標準

一個IT系統是否屬於GxP範圍，取決於它是否直接影響以下任一項：

  • 產品品質：製程參數、批次記錄、放行檢驗
  • 患者安全：無菌保證、效價記錄
  • 記錄完整性：資料可被修改、刪除，或無法追溯

OT網路 vs IT網路的分離

在無菌製藥CDMO中，DCS/SCADA等製程控制系統（OT）的網路通常需要與一般IT網路實體隔離或邏輯隔離：

  • OT網路（製程控制層）：高可用性要求，不容許隨意patch
  • IT網路（辦公室/業務層）：標準IT管理
  • DMZ（非軍事區）：兩者之間的受控交換點

無菌製藥CDMO的IT基礎設施架構

Business IT Zone
Email, ERP, Office
Firewall / DMZ
GxP IT Zone
MES, LIMS, QMS, EDMS
Firewall / Air-gap
OT / Control Zone
DCS, SCADA, BAS

思考練習

  1. 若MES和ERP共用同一台資料庫伺服器，這個伺服器屬於GxP範圍嗎？你如何處理這個混合使用情況？
  2. SCADA系統的網路路由器需要進行GAMP資格確認嗎？屬於哪個類別？
  3. 一家CDMO的IT部門聲稱「雲端服務提供商的伺服器不在GxP範圍內，所以不需要資格確認」——你認為這種說法正確嗎？
REG

Regulatory Context | 法規背景比較

21 CFR Part 11 vs EU Annex 11 — key requirements for IT Infrastructure · 美歐法規對IT基礎設施的要求比較

Regulatory Requirements Comparison

Table: 21 CFR Part 11 vs EU Annex 11 — IT Infrastructure Relevance

Topic 21 CFR Part 11 (US FDA) EU Annex 11 (EMA)
Scope Electronic records and electronic signatures in FDA-regulated activities Computerized systems used in GMP-regulated activities
System validation §11.10(a): Validated systems to ensure accuracy, reliability, consistent performance Clause 4: Validation — risk-based approach, life cycle documentation
Audit trail §11.10(e): Computer-generated time-stamped audit trails Clause 9: Audit trails capturing user actions
Access control §11.10(d): Limiting system access to authorized individuals Clause 12.1: Physical and logical access restrictions
Data backup §11.10(c): Protection of records — retrievability Clause 7.2: Regular back-ups, verified ability to restore
Disaster recovery Business continuity (implied) Clause 16: Disaster recovery plans required
Change control §11.10(k): Use of operational system checks Clause 10: Changes — including infrastructure changes evaluated
E-signatures §11.50: Signature manifestations required Clause 17: Electronic signatures — EU directive compliant
IT Infrastructure Implicit in system validation requirements Clause 4.7: Infrastructure qualification explicitly mentioned
法規比較解讀

兩大法規的核心差異

  • 21 CFR Part 11：美國法規，重點在電子記錄和電子簽名的技術控制（以IT功能要求為主）
  • EU Annex 11：歐盟GMP附件，涵蓋整個電腦化系統生命週期，對IT基礎設施的明確要求更多

EU Annex 11 在2011年更新後，對供應商管理、雲端/外包、以及基礎設施資格確認都有更明確的規定，比Part 11更全面地涵蓋IT基礎設施。

CDMO合規策略：同時滿足兩套法規

服務美歐市場的CDMO必須同時符合兩套要求。實務上：

  • Audit trail：系統層級的時間戳記審計日誌（滿足Part 11 §11.10(e)和Annex 11第9條）
  • Backup & restore：定期備份並驗證還原能力（滿足Annex 11第7.2條）
  • Access control：角色型存取控制，最小權限原則（滿足兩者）
  • Change control SOP：涵蓋IT基礎設施變更（滿足Annex 11第10條）

EU Annex 11 第4.7條的重要性

EU Annex 11明確要求「IT基礎設施資格確認」，是法規史上少數直接點名IT基礎設施（而非只談應用程式）需要資格確認的法規條文。這直接呼應本GAMP指南的核心主張。

21 CFR Part 11 vs Annex 11 適用情境

  • FDA PAI（上市前稽查）：重點查Part 11合規
  • EMA GMP稽查：重點查Annex 11合規
  • PICS稽查（日本PMDA、澳洲TGA等）：通常遵循Annex 11框架
  • 雙重申報（美歐）：兩套要求都需滿足

思考練習

  1. 若你的DCS系統只向FDA申報（不申報歐盟），你是否還需要滿足EU Annex 11的要求？
  2. 21 CFR Part 11第11.10(e)的「電腦生成時間戳記審計日誌」——時間同步（NTP伺服器）是IT基礎設施還是應用程式的責任？
  3. EU Annex 11明確提到「外包服務」，若你的LIMS資料庫外包給第三方雲端，供應商協議需要包含哪些GxP要求？
2.1

Chapter 2 — Platforms | 第2章：平台

Platform components and GAMP categories · 平台元件與GAMP類別分配

Original Text (English)

On-going quality management of the IT Infrastructure includes assurance that all processes and procedures are in place to control the life cycle activities of the IT Infrastructure platforms, and that qualified personnel are available to complete assigned tasks.

The IT Infrastructure may be looked upon as consisting of three major elements of fundamentally different nature:

  • Platforms
  • Processes
  • Personnel

Platforms provide a well defined foundation for other well defined hardware or software components.

Table 2.1: Platform Components and GAMP® Categories

Platform Component GAMP Category Notes
Networks
Switches, hubs, routers, firewalls, wireless hotspots, cables		 HW Cat 1; SW Cat 1 or 2
(Customized cables: HW Cat 2)		 Critical configuration information should be recorded and managed. Internet-based networks add security/integrity challenges.
Hardware & Peripherals
Servers, power supplies, NIC cards, disk arrays, printers		 HW Category 1 Standard, commercially available components used in direct support of applications and IT Infrastructure services.
Firmware SW Category 2 (when updated independently) When firmware is updated independently of the hardware, it should be managed as software in its own right.
Operating Systems
OS + device drivers + communication protocols		 SW Category 1 (most) Configuration must be documented. OS access/privilege features used by applications may be validated as part of the application.
Data Management Software
File storage, DBMS, web services, interface software		 SW Category 1 (most); some may be Cat 2+ Elements often support more than one application. Complexity and configurability determine the category.
Servers
Standard or individually configured		 HW Cat 1 + SW Cat 1 or 2 (combination) Actual set-up dictates the qualification strategy. Standard server building blocks allow efficient duplication.
Clients
Thin to thick clients		 HW Cat 1 + SW Cat 1 or 2 (combination) Range from thin clients (no local processing) to thick clients (local data storage). Set-up dictates life cycle model.
Applications
Off-the-shelf to custom software		 SW Categories 3, 4, or 5 Validation of applications is OUTSIDE the scope of this Guide.
CDMO 實務解讀

GAMP類別速查（IT基礎設施版）

GAMP類別 描述 IT基礎設施範例
HW Cat 1 標準硬體 伺服器、網路交換器、NIC卡
HW Cat 2 客製化硬體 客製化線纜
SW Cat 1 基礎設施軟體（OS等） Windows Server、Linux OS、驅動程式
SW Cat 2 不可配置的標準軟體包 網路設備韌體、某些中介軟體
SW Cat 3 非配置的標準軟體 （偏應用程式層）
SW Cat 4 可配置的標準軟體 MES、LIMS（應用程式範圍）
SW Cat 5 客製開發軟體 客製化應用程式（應用程式範圍）

IT基礎設施平台主要落在 HW Cat 1, SW Cat 1-2；應用程式為 SW Cat 3-5。

為何大多數IT基礎設施是Cat 1？

Cat 1（基礎設施軟體）的假設是：這類軟體由大廠商（Microsoft、Cisco、VMware）廣泛測試和部署，行業已積累大量使用經驗，自我錯誤偵測能力強。因此，只需確認安裝正確、配置符合規格，不需要像應用程式一樣進行完整的業務功能測試。

實務提醒：韌體的特殊處理

韌體（Firmware）通常被視為硬體的一部分。但當韌體可以獨立更新時（如伺服器BIOS/UEFI、網路設備韌體），就需要像軟體一樣管理：

  • 納入變更管理流程
  • 分類為SW Category 2
  • 記錄版本和更新紀錄

在GxP環境中，韌體更新需要評估對上層GxP應用程式的潛在影響。

思考練習

  1. 你廠區的Cisco防火牆屬於哪個GAMP類別？其配置文件需要如何管理？
  2. 若VMware vSphere被用作GxP應用程式的虛擬化層，它應被分類為哪個GAMP類別？資格確認策略是什麼？
  3. 「thin client vs thick client」的選擇對GxP合規有哪些影響？本地儲存的資料如何管理？
2.2

Processes | 流程

ITIL-based IT Infrastructure processes for GxP compliance · 基於ITIL的IT基礎設施流程

Original Text (English)

The number of IT Infrastructure processes a company decides to implement and the method of implementation depend mainly on the criticality of the business processes being supported and on the size of the company.

The processes listed cover typical aspects required for good business practice, as well as compliance. This list, which takes into account ITIL (IT Infrastructure Library), is indicative only, and organizations may view different processes as being sub-processes to other processes.

Key IT Infrastructure Processes:

  • Change Management
  • Configuration Management
  • Security Management
  • Server Management
  • Client Management
  • Network Management
  • Problem Management
  • Help Desk (also known as Service Desk in ITIL)
  • Backup, Restore, and Archiving
  • Disaster Recovery
  • Performance Monitoring
  • Supplier Management

Key processes are considered further in Section 6 of this Guide.

CDMO 實務解讀

ITIL框架與GxP的整合

ITIL（IT基礎設施資源庫）是全球IT服務管理的最佳實踐框架。許多IT部門已遵循ITIL，而GAMP指南承認ITIL的有效性，意味著：

若你的IT部門已實施ITIL：大部分流程框架可直接用於GxP合規，只需在現有流程上增加GxP相關要求（如更嚴格的文件記錄和QA審查）。

若尚未實施ITIL：可以從GxP要求最高的流程開始建立，再逐步完善。

12個流程的GxP優先順序（CDMO視角）

流程 GxP重要性 主要風險
Change Management 極高 未控制的變更影響已驗證狀態
Configuration Mgmt 極高 配置漂移導致系統不符合規格
Backup & Restore 極高 GxP記錄遺失無法復原
Security Management 極高 未授權存取、資料完整性
Problem Management 高 系統失效影響GxP作業
Disaster Recovery 高 重大事件後無法恢復作業
Supplier Management 高 外包服務失控
Performance Monitoring 中 效能降級影響系統可靠性
Help Desk 中 問題記錄不完整

Change Management的特殊GxP挑戰

在GxP環境中，IT的「變更管理」比一般企業複雜：每一次OS patch、網路設備韌體更新、伺服器配置調整都需要評估是否影響已驗證的應用程式。這需要IT和QA緊密協作，而不是IT單獨決定。

思考練習

  1. 你廠區目前有哪些ITIL流程已實施？哪些尚未建立但GxP上是必要的？
  2. 「Configuration Management（組態管理）」在GxP環境中的「組態漂移（configuration drift）」是什麼意思？如何預防？
  3. 若廠區的IT Help Desk是外包的，如何確保Help Desk記錄的問題和解決方案符合GxP的文件追溯要求？
2.3

Personnel | 人員

Roles, responsibilities, training, and qualifications · 角色、責任、訓練與資格

Original Text (English)

Management should define roles and responsibilities (job descriptions) in terms of tasks to be undertaken, and the qualifications and experience needed. Individual job descriptions should be assigned to named individuals fulfilling those roles, permanently or on an ad-hoc basis.

Key roles that may be identified include:

  • Executive Management (Project Sponsorship)
  • Project Manager
  • Application (system/data) owner / administrator / application-oriented SMEs
  • Data owners (if not coinciding with application owner)
  • IT Infrastructure process owner / administrators / SMEs (e.g., IT support engineers)
  • Platform owner / administrator / SMEs (e.g., network engineers)
  • Independent QA in relation to information technology
  • IT Quality and Compliance

Technical and managerial staff with appropriate educational background and experience should be available. Provision of training should be planned to ensure the required skills are developed and maintained.

Staff should be made aware of any regulatory requirements that apply to their duties, trained in those procedures that are applicable to them, and re-trained as changes occur. Records of training should be maintained.

Appendix 1 of this Guide provides more detailed guidance on the various roles.

CDMO 實務解讀

IT / QA / Regulatory 角色責任比較表

角色 主要職責 GxP責任
IT Manager
IT基礎設施管理者		 IT基礎設施整體規劃、預算、資源管理 確保IT流程支持GxP合規；批准基礎設施變更
System Administrator
系統管理員		 伺服器、OS、資料庫日常維運；patch管理 執行變更時遵循GxP變更管理程序；維護配置文件
Network Engineer
網路工程師		 網路規劃、設計、配置管理 GxP網路區段的資格確認；防火牆規則的變更控制
Application Owner
應用程式擁有者		 業務系統（MES/LIMS）的需求與驗收 定義GxP需求；批准應用程式驗證文件；通知IT基礎設施需求變更
QA Reviewer
品保審查員		 資格確認和驗證文件審查與批准 獨立審查所有GxP相關IT文件；稽查IT流程；批准偏差
IT Quality & Compliance
IT品質合規專員		 IT與QA之間的橋樑；協調GxP IT活動 制定IT合規政策；監督GxP IT活動；處理法規查詢
Data Owner
資料擁有者		 特定GxP資料集的責任人 確保資料完整性；定義資料保留期限；批准資料存取

IT人員的GxP訓練要求

IT人員通常具備技術背景但缺乏GxP法規意識。必要的訓練項目包括：

  • 法規認知：21 CFR Part 11、EU Annex 11的基本要求
  • 流程訓練：GxP變更管理SOP、偏差處理程序
  • 文件要求：ALCOA+原則（可歸屬、清晰、同步、原始、正確、完整、一致、持久、可用）
  • 資格確認：IQ/OQ文件撰寫和執行

「獨立QA」的重要性

指南特別強調「independent QA in relation to information technology」——QA對IT活動的審查必須是獨立的，不能由IT部門自己審查自己的資格確認文件。

在小型CDMO中，QA可能沒有IT專業背景，這時可考慮：

  • 聘請兼具IT和GxP背景的IT Quality Compliance專員
  • 外部顧問提供獨立審查
  • 建立交叉審查機制

Application Owner vs Data Owner：不一定是同一人

指南明確區分兩個角色：

  • Application Owner：對LIMS系統（軟體）負責的人，通常是Lab Manager
  • Data Owner：對特定資料集負責的人，例如品保副總可能是「批次放行資料」的Owner，即使她不擁有LIMS系統

在GxP數據完整性調查中，釐清誰是Data Owner非常重要。

思考練習

  1. 你廠區是否有明確定義的「IT Quality and Compliance」角色？這個角色在組織架構中向誰匯報最合適？
  2. 若IT系統管理員執行了一個未記錄的伺服器配置變更，這在GxP稽查中會引發哪些問題？如何從人員/流程角度預防？
  3. 「訓練記錄應被維護」——你廠區的IT人員訓練記錄是在哪個系統中管理的？這個系統本身是否也需要GxP合規？
SUM

Chapter 1–2 Summary | 第1–2章總結

Key takeaways and self-assessment · 重點整理與自我評估

Key Takeaways

The Core Logic of IT Infrastructure GxP Compliance

  • GxP applications depend on IT Infrastructure → Infrastructure must be qualified
  • Horizontal (platform-based) approach avoids duplication — qualify the platform once, validate applications separately
  • IT Infrastructure = Platforms + Processes + Personnel (all three must be managed)
  • Platform components are mostly GAMP HW Cat 1, SW Cat 1–2 (lower risk than applications)
  • ITIL provides a solid foundation — add GxP requirements on top
  • Key regulatory hooks: 21 CFR Part 11 (US) and EU Annex 11 (EU GMP)

Common Inspection Findings — IT Infrastructure

  • Lack of documented IT infrastructure qualification (IQ/OQ) for GxP-supporting systems
  • Undocumented changes to servers/OS/database configurations
  • No formal change control for security patches in GxP environments
  • Backup not tested — no verified restore capability
  • Access control gaps — shared accounts, no audit trail
  • IT staff with no GxP training records
核心重點整理

Ch 1–2 的五條核心訊息

  1. IT基礎設施是GxP系統的地基：地基失控，上面的應用程式驗證就失效。
  2. 水平方法是核心策略：一次資格確認平台，多個應用程式受益，避免重複工作。
  3. 三元素缺一不可：平台資格確認了、但沒有受過訓練的人員和文件化流程，合規依然不完整。
  4. 風險驅動，規模可調：小公司不需要和大型跨國藥廠做同樣深度的資格確認，但框架邏輯相同。
  5. IT和QA必須協同：沒有獨立的QA監督，IT基礎設施的GxP合規就是空架子。

最終自我評估 — 你準備好了嗎？

  1. 你能向FDA稽查員解釋為什麼你們採用水平（而非垂直）的IT資格確認方法嗎？
  2. 你的廠區能立即提供所有GxP伺服器的IQ/OQ文件嗎？
  3. 你能說出每個GxP應用程式的Application Owner和Data Owner分別是誰嗎？
  4. 若明天伺服器發生故障，你能在RTO（恢復時間目標）內恢復GxP系統並提供完整的事件記錄嗎？
  5. 你的IT人員上次接受GxP相關訓練是什麼時候？訓練記錄在哪裡？

Learning Objectives  |  學習目標

  • Describe the 9 elements of a QMS for IT infrastructure and explain their GMP relevance
    描述IT基礎架構QMS的9個要素及其GMP相關性
  • Define roles and documentation requirements for IT QA governance
    定義IT QA治理的角色分配與文件要求

    將IT基礎架構V型模型各階段對應其交付成果
  • List the required contents of a Platform Qualification Plan
    列舉平台確效計畫的必要內容
  • Describe the legacy platform qualification approach including Experience Reports
    描述舊有平台的確效方法，包含經驗報告
3

Quality Management System for IT Infrastructure

IT基礎架構的品質管理系統  |  Pages 18–20

Chapter Introduction  |  章節導言

This chapter describes how a Quality Management System (QMS) may assist in providing evidence that the IT Infrastructure is in a controlled state, and the key requirements for the QMS to attain this goal.

本章描述品質管理系統（QMS）如何協助提供IT基礎架構處於受控狀態的證據，以及QMS達成此目標的關鍵要求。

Why IT Needs Its Own QMS | 為何IT需要自己的QMS

Traditional pharma QMS covers manufacturing processes. As IT infrastructure directly supports GxP computerised systems — which in turn manage critical product quality data — the IT function must operate within a structured quality framework of its own.

傳統製藥QMS涵蓋生產流程。由於IT基礎架構直接支撐GxP電腦化系統（而這些系統管理關鍵產品品質數據），IT部門必須在自身結構化品質框架內運作。

CDMO IT-QA Governance Model  |  CDMO IT-QA治理模型

Practical Structure for a CDMO IT-QA Function

In a fill-finish CDMO, IT-QA governance typically sits at the interface between QA, IT Operations, and Validation. Key accountability points:

  • QA — owns the IT Quality Manual, approves SOPs, conducts audits, signs off Qualification Plans
  • IT Operations — owns platform management, change control execution, backup/DR
  • Validation / CSV Team — owns IQ/OQ/PQ execution, test documentation, qualification reports
  • Application/Data Owners — define GxP criticality of systems they own; trigger risk assessments
  • Regulatory Affairs — interprets GxP obligations; informs infrastructure risk scope

The "Factory Floor" Analogy | 「工廠地板」比喻

Think of IT infrastructure as the factory floor that all GxP systems run on. Just as the physical manufacturing facility needs environmental monitoring, cleaning validation, and maintenance SOPs, the IT "floor" needs its own QMS to demonstrate control.

將IT基礎架構想象為所有GxP系統運行的工廠地板。正如實體生產設施需要環境監測、清潔確效和維護SOP，IT「地板」也需要自己的QMS來展示受控狀態。

3.1 Quality Manual  |  品質手冊

A Quality Manual should set quality objectives in line with corporate Quality Policy. A top level document relating to IT Infrastructure should cover:

  • Identification of key IT Infrastructure processes (especially those that pertain to IT Infrastructure qualification and operational management), and how they interact
  • Procedures, detailed work instructions, templates, and other standards that apply
  • Required records and documentation to be maintained

Quality Manuals and top level documents should be approved by QA. For further information, see ISO 9000:2000 Quality Management Systems – Fundamentals and Vocabulary.

品質手冊應根據企業品質政策設定品質目標。頂層文件應涵蓋關鍵IT流程識別、適用程序與標準、以及需維護的記錄與文件。品質手冊應由QA批准。

QMS Elements for IT Departments  |  IT部門QMS要素

QMS Element 要素 IT Application 應用 Key Output 關鍵輸出
3.1 Quality Manual IT-specific quality objectives aligned to corporate policy Approved IT Quality Manual / IT品質手冊
3.2 Roles & Responsibilities Job descriptions for IT, QA, Data Owners Role matrix / 職責矩陣
3.3 Record Management Controls for retrievability, storage, protection Records retention schedule / 記錄保留計畫
3.4 Documentation Platform docs, test results, consistent templates EDMS or doc control system / 文件管理系統
3.5 Testing Traceable test specs, acceptance criteria, QA review Executed test records / 已執行測試記錄
3.6 SOPs Critical IT processes and services documented IT SOP library / IT SOP文件庫
3.7 Training Planned, documented, includes contractors Training records / 培訓記錄
3.8 Periodic Review Risk-based frequency, maintains qualified status Periodic Review reports / 定期審查報告
3.9 QA Audit Independent QA audits of IT function Audit reports & CAPAs / 稽核報告與矯正

3.2–3.4 Roles, Records & Documentation  |  角色、記錄與文件

3.2 Roles and Responsibilities: Roles and responsibilities should be defined for all important functions. Job descriptions or other documents should reflect the assignment of roles and responsibilities.

3.3 Record Management: Appropriate controls need to be in place to ensure the retrievability, storage, and protection of records. The controls should provide evidence of quality levels of the IT platform, and compliance with regulations.

3.4 Documentation: Documentation for platforms, processes, test results, etc., should be maintained in order to meet requirements for inspections by regulatory authorities.

  • IT staff should ensure that documentation is readily available — this should be challenged during internal assessments and QA audits
  • Tools and utility systems should be available during regulatory inspections to provide displays and printouts
  • There should be a consistent approach to documentation across an organization
  • Systems and processes for the creation, review, and approval of documents should be established (e.g., standard templates, EDMS)

3.2 角色與職責應明確定義並反映於職務說明。3.3 記錄管理控制確保可檢索性、儲存與保護。3.4 文件管理須可供法規查核，並保持全組織一致性。

CDMO Practical Notes  |  CDMO實務要點

Common Inspection Finding: Undefined IT Roles

During FDA 483 observations in pharma, a frequent finding is that IT staff perform GxP-impacting tasks (e.g., user access management, backup verification) without documented role assignments or training records. ISPE Section 3.2 directly addresses this gap.

FDA 483常見缺失：IT人員執行影響GxP的任務（如使用者存取管理、備份驗證）卻無文件化的職責指定或培訓記錄。

Documentation Readiness for Inspections | 查核文件整備

  • All platform qualification records must be immediately retrievable (not archived off-site without recall procedure)
  • Configuration reports and system inventory printouts must be available on demand
  • EDMS should have a "inspector view" or read-only access mode
  • IT staff must be trained to generate config reports in real time

Analogy: The "Passport Control" Model | 「護照管制」比喻

Record management in IT is like passport control at an airport — every record must be findable (retrievable), authentic (protected from tampering), and current (stored correctly). If any of these three properties fails, the compliance "border" is breached.

3.5 Testing Requirements  |  測試要求

Test documentation generated as a result of the execution of test specifications during qualification should meet the following general requirements:

  • Traceable to the specification that required the documentation
  • Reviewed and approved by required units or individuals, usually including QA
  • Clear and objectively verifiable acceptance criteria
  • Each test step or test case traceable to the pertinent section in the applicable requirement or design specifications
  • Accurate records of observations made by identifiable and trained personnel
  • Entries should reflect the actual observation and not just pass or fail, except when the criteria for pass and fail are made absolutely clear by the specification
  • Hardcopies of screen dumps, or collation by computerized tool, should be added to support test results where appropriate
  • Entries should be made in legible, permanent handwriting, or using a suitable computerized tool
  • Corrections should be made without obscuring the original entry — the date, reason, and identity of the person making the correction should be clear

The rigor with which the above requirements are met will depend upon the impact and risks associated with the component being tested.

測試文件須可追溯至規格、經QA審查核准、具客觀可驗證的接受標準，並記錄實際觀察結果而非僅標示通過/失敗。

Testing Rigor vs. Risk Level  |  測試嚴格程度與風險等級

Risk-Based Testing Principle | 基於風險的測試原則

Not all IT components require the same level of test documentation rigor. The ISPE guide explicitly states that rigor is proportional to impact and risk. This allows efficient use of validation resources.

並非所有IT元件都需要相同程度的測試文件嚴格性。ISPE明確指出嚴格程度與衝擊和風險成正比。

Component Type 元件類型 GxP Impact GxP衝擊 Required Rigor 要求嚴格度
Network switch (non-GxP VLAN) Low Checklist-based IQ sufficient
Server hosting MES / LIMS High Full IQ/OQ with screen dumps, QA sign-off
Backup system for GxP data High OQ with restore verification, periodic re-test
Printer (administrative only) Minimal Installation checklist only
Active Directory (user access) Medium OQ for access controls, IQ for configuration

GAMP Comparison | 與GAMP對比

GAMP 5 uses a similar risk-based approach for application CSV. ISPE GAMP IT Infrastructure extends the same philosophy to infrastructure layers — a critical alignment point for CDMO validation programs that cover both application and infrastructure.

3.6–3.9: SOPs, Training, Periodic Review & QA Audit  |  SOP、培訓、定期審查與QA稽核

3.6 Standard Operating Procedures: SOPs should describe critical processes and services, be reviewed for compliance with user requirements, company IT policies, and regulations. Procedures should specify the records needed for maintenance, troubleshooting, and auditable evidence.

3.7 Training: Training should be planned and documented. Formal structured training programs (in-house or external) should be considered. Technical and regulatory training requirements for external service providers and contractors should also be determined.

3.8 Periodic Review and Evaluation: Subject matter experts or IT Quality and Compliance members should review processes, systems, or platforms to ensure they meet specified requirements. The review also monitors QMS effectiveness and identifies improvements.

  • Scope, depth, and frequency based on impact and risk
  • Operational history and known problems should be considered
  • A sampling technique typically is used when planning assessments
  • Periodic Reviews are an important element of maintaining the qualification status of IT Infrastructure throughout its operational life
  • May be scheduled or event-driven (e.g., following a major upgrade)

3.9 Audit by QA: Audits should be conducted by QA staff independent of the group being audited. The scope, frequency, and objective of audits should be determined by QA. External consultants or independent internal experts may assist.

3.6 SOP描述關鍵IT流程。3.7 培訓需規劃並記錄，含外包商。3.8 定期審查維持確效狀態，頻率基於風險。3.9 QA稽核須獨立進行。

IT SOP Library Checklist  |  IT SOP文件庫清單

Per ISPE Appendix 4 recommendations, a minimum IT QMS SOP library should include:

  • Change Control Procedure for IT Infrastructure 變更控制程序
  • Configuration Management SOP 組態管理SOP
  • User Access Management and Review 使用者存取管理與審查
  • Backup and Restore Verification 備份與還原驗證
  • Disaster Recovery Planning and Testing 災難復原規劃與測試
  • Periodic Review of IT Infrastructure 定期審查程序
  • Incident and Problem Management 事件與問題管理
  • Supplier / Vendor Assessment 供應商評估程序
  • IT Security Management 資訊安全管理
  • Platform Qualification Procedure 平台確效程序
  • Network Diagram Maintenance 網路圖維護
  • Performance Monitoring of Critical Systems 關鍵系統效能監測

Periodic Review Triggers | 定期審查觸發條件

  • Scheduled calendar-based review (e.g., annual)
  • After major hardware or platform software upgrade
  • Following a significant incident or near-miss
  • Prior to regulatory inspection
  • After significant organizational or supplier change

Practice Questions — Chapter 3  |  練習題

  1. A new CDMO site has an IT team that manages the network, servers, and backup systems for the MES and LIMS. What are the minimum QMS elements that the IT team must establish, and who should approve the IT Quality Manual?
    一家新CDMO場址的IT團隊管理MES和LIMS的網路、伺服器和備份系統。IT團隊必須建立哪些最低QMS要素？誰應批准IT品質手冊？
  2. During a regulatory inspection, an investigator asks to see all test records for the server hosting the batch record system. The IT manager cannot locate the qualification records from 3 years ago. Which ISPE sections have been violated, and what controls should have been in place?
    在法規查核期間，調查員要求查看批次記錄系統伺服器的所有測試記錄。IT管理員無法找到3年前的確效記錄。違反了哪些ISPE條款？應有哪些控制措施？
  3. Your IT contractor recently patched the operating system on a GxP server but there is no training record showing the contractor understood the GxP implications of the patch. Which section addresses this gap, and what should a compliant process look like?
    IT承包商最近修補了GxP伺服器的作業系統，但沒有培訓記錄顯示承包商了解補丁的GxP影響。哪個條款解決這個差距？合規流程應如何設計？
4

Applying Risk Management to IT Infrastructure

將風險管理應用於IT基礎架構  |  Pages 21–23

Chapter Introduction  |  章節導言

Risk Management is defined by ISO as the systematic application of management policies, procedures, and practices to the tasks of analyzing, evaluating, and controlling risk.

風險管理由ISO定義為系統性地應用管理政策、程序和實踐，以分析、評估和控制風險。

Risk Assessments should be performed for each major life cycle phase of an object or groups of objects (e.g., platforms, data) identified as important to a company's business.

風險評估應在識別為對公司業務重要的物件（如平台、數據）的每個主要生命週期階段執行。

5 Key Risk Management Activities | 5個關鍵風險管理活動

  1. Identify IT infrastructure components that may require qualification, based on analysis of applications and processes supported, and applicable regulations
  2. Assess components based upon identified hazards, vulnerabilities, and assessed impact on critical aspects — recognizing that in many cases the risk will be relatively low
  3. Implement controls commensurate with identified risks — document and justify controls with reference to identified risks
  4. Assess proposed changes to qualified components
  5. Monitor effectiveness of controls by Periodic Review

Companies also may decide to apply this Risk Management approach to IT Infrastructure components which do not support GxP applications, but which are business critical.

公司也可將此風險管理方法應用於不支援GxP應用程式但具業務關鍵性的IT基礎架構元件。

Risk-Based Qualification Scope Decision Matrix  |  基於風險的確效範疇決策矩陣

Component 元件 GxP Support?
支援GxP?		 Business Critical?
業務關鍵?		 Qualification Scope
確效範疇
GxP App Server Yes Yes Full IQ/OQ required
GxP Database Server Yes Yes Full IQ/OQ required
Network Backbone Indirect Yes Scoped IQ + risk controls
ERP (Finance only) No Yes Business controls only
AD / Identity Mgmt Indirect Yes Access controls OQ
Backup System (GxP) Yes Yes OQ incl. restore test
Office WiFi (admin) No No Minimal / checklist

Key Principle | 關鍵原則

Infrastructure staff should not be expected to assess GxP compliance independently. Application/data owners and QA define which platform components require qualification. This division of responsibility prevents both over- and under-qualification.

基礎架構人員不應被期望獨立評估GxP合規性。應用/數據擁有者和QA定義哪些平台元件需要確效。

4.1 Identification and Assessment of Components  |  元件識別與評估

Application/data owners and QA should define which platform components (or types of component) and tools require qualification. For IT Infrastructure components, the criticality of the GxP applications they support, along with impact on integrity and availability of data should be considered.

Platform management groups may assign the same level of criticality to all components and data unless system/data owners specify different levels of criticality.

Non-GxP applications operating on the IT Infrastructure may affect GxP applications — these should be identified within the Risk Assessment process, and suitable controls included.

The risk analysis process should identify potential hazards and vulnerabilities. Hazards in the context of platform qualification may result in risks to:

  • Records related to product quality or patient safety:
    • Integrity — short term or long term
    • Confidentiality — if required by the company
    • Availability — at the right place and time
  • Availability of services — affects business and compliance if persistent
  • Validity of IT Infrastructure processes, e.g., User Access Accounting
  • Availability and training of key staff

Once identified, the impact and likelihood of these hazards should be assessed and documented. Risk Assessment is typically an iterative process, performed progressively during planning and specification as more information becomes available.

風險分析過程應識別危害和漏洞，評估記錄完整性、可用性、服務可用性、流程有效性及人員可用性的風險。

IT Component Risk Classification Table  |  IT元件風險分類表

IT Component 元件 Risk Categories 風險類別 Typical Classification 典型分類 Key Controls 關鍵控制
GxP Data Server Data integrity, availability, confidentiality Critical RAID, backup, access control, audit trail
Network Infrastructure Service availability, data integrity in transit Major Redundancy, monitoring, segmentation
Active Directory User access validity, compliance with 21 CFR Part 11 Critical Access review, audit logging, password policy
Backup Systems Data availability, long-term integrity Critical Restore testing, off-site storage, encryption
HVAC control IT (BAS) Indirect product quality impact Major Environmental monitoring integration, alarms
Email / Collaboration Business continuity only Minor Standard IT controls
Antivirus / Patch Mgmt Platform integrity (indirect GxP) Major Validated patch process, qualification impact assessment

The "CIA Triad" in GxP Context | GxP脈絡中的「CIA三元組」

The ISPE risk hazard categories map directly to the classic information security CIA model: Confidentiality (data not exposed), Integrity (data not corrupted), Availability (data accessible when needed). All three are GxP requirements — not just IT security concerns.

4.2–4.4: Controls, Change Assessment & Periodic Review  |  控制措施、變更評估與定期審查

4.2 Implementation of Controls: A range of controls may be appropriate to mitigate the identified risks:

  • Testing
  • Redesign, including incorporation of redundancy
  • Deployment of automatic performance, diagnostic, alarm, and security monitoring tools
  • Updated or new policies, guidelines, and instructions
  • Extra education or training
  • Supplier assessments and management
  • Identification of new or updated roles and responsibilities
  • Provision of extra staff, facilities, tools, and office space

Successful implementation of the required controls should be verified during qualification, and Periodic Review.

4.3 Assessment of Changes to Qualified Components: The impact and risk associated with proposed changes to IT Infrastructure components should be assessed as part of the change management process, and appropriate controls implemented.

4.4 Periodic Review and Evaluation: During Periodic Review of IT Infrastructure, the company should reconsider the risks and verify that controls established during IT Infrastructure development and qualification are still effective. The review also should consider:

  • If previously unrecognized hazards are present
  • If the estimated risks arising from a hazard are no longer acceptable
  • If the original assessment is otherwise invalidated

4.2 控制措施包括測試、重新設計、自動監測工具、政策更新等。4.3 變更需評估對確效元件的影響。4.4 定期審查驗證現有控制是否仍然有效。

Risk Control Implementation & GAMP 5 Comparison  |  風險控制實施與GAMP 5對比

How ISPE IT Infrastructure Compares to GAMP 5 CSV Approach

Aspect GAMP 5 (Applications) ISPE GAMP IT Infrastructure
Risk-based scope Yes — 5 software categories Yes — component criticality
Documentation URS→FS→DS→TP→TR Platform specs→IQ→OQ→Report
Life cycle model V-model (application) V-model (infrastructure)
Change control Validation impact assessment Qualification impact assessment
Supplier assessment GAMP category-dependent Risk-determined (Q or full audit)
Periodic review Required (application level) Required + can feed app review

Change Control — The Critical Link | 變更控制的關鍵連結

Section 4.3 establishes that every change to a qualified IT component must go through a risk assessment. This is the mechanism that prevents qualification from becoming a one-time event. For CDMOs with frequent infrastructure updates (OS patches, hypervisor upgrades), a mature IT change control process is non-negotiable.

對確效IT元件的每次變更都必須進行風險評估，防止確效成為一次性事件。

Practice Questions — Chapter 4  |  練習題

  1. A non-GxP ERP system is installed on the same physical server cluster as the GxP LIMS. How should this situation be handled in the IT risk assessment, and what controls might be required?
    一個非GxP的ERP系統安裝在與GxP LIMS相同的實體伺服器叢集上。應如何在IT風險評估中處理此情況？可能需要哪些控制措施？
  2. Your qualified network switches are being replaced with a new model from a different vendor. What is the ISPE-required process for this change, and what documentation must be produced?
    您已確效的網路交換機正在被不同供應商的新型號替換。ISPE要求的流程是什麼？必須產生哪些文件？
  3. During a periodic review of the IT infrastructure, you discover that a monitoring alert for disk space was disabled 8 months ago and never re-enabled. Walk through the risk management steps you would take, referencing specific ISPE sections.
    在IT基礎架構定期審查期間，您發現磁碟空間監測警報在8個月前被停用且從未重新啟用。請引用具體ISPE條款，說明您將採取的風險管理步驟。
5.1

Qualification of Platforms — Overview of Process

平台確效 — 流程概述  |  Pages 24–25

Overview  |  概述

This section describes how a platform, or a major addition to an existing platform, may be brought into compliance with the company's established standards using a planned qualification process. Minor additions are usually managed via change control.

本節描述如何使用計畫性確效流程，將平台或對現有平台的重大新增項目帶入符合公司既定標準的狀態。輕微新增通常通過變更控制管理。

A Platform Project and Qualification Plan, describing the life cycle activities to be undertaken to qualify each platform type, should be created. The plan should cover:

  • The approved and effective SOPs required
  • Deliverables that will be the output of the qualification process
  • Responsibilities and approvals required

The qualification strategy is typically based on one of two scenarios:

Strategy 1: Building-Block (Generic Platform) | 策略1：積木式

Platform specifications are independent of any specific applications. Developed from generic requirements, bound by company policies. Application specifications take existing, standardized platform capabilities into account. Qualification commences with little interaction with application owners — qualified platforms are considered commodities.

適用於標準化IT環境，平台規格獨立於具體應用程式，確效平台視為商品。

Strategy 2: Case-by-Case | 策略2：逐案式

Platform requirements are mainly derived from system (application) specifications on a case-by-case basis. Building-block concept not fully usable; significant interaction with application owners required; platform qualification is largely a one-off exercise.

適用於高度客製化或特殊應用環境，需與應用程式擁有者密切協作。

Qualification Process Flow & Building-Block Strategy  |  確效流程與積木式策略

Sequential Qualification Steps | 確效步驟順序

  1. Risk Assessment → determines scope and intensity of qualification, which components and configurations are required, rigor of supplier assessment
  2. Procurement → supplier evaluation based on risk outcome
  3. IQ (Installation Qualification) → evidence that all components installed and configured as specified; certification evidence may support IQ
  4. OQ (Operational Qualification) → evidence that critical features of the platform perform as specified
  5. Qualification Report → summarizes results, formally concludes the qualification process

The Building-Block Advantage | 積木式策略的優勢

The preferred qualification strategy is to qualify types of building blocks, then run abbreviated qualifications of individual instances. Benefits:

  • Reduces qualification effort for each new server or workstation
  • Standardizes the IT environment — reduces variability and risk
  • Enables faster deployment of new GxP-supporting systems
  • Qualification work is reusable — ROI improves over time

對積木類型確效後，各實例可使用縮短確效，降低工作量並加快部署速度。

GAMP 5 Parallel | GAMP 5對應

Strategy 1 (Building Block) parallels GAMP 5's approach to Category 1 infrastructure — leveraging vendor documentation and standardized configurations. Strategy 2 parallels custom application validation where system-specific requirements drive the scope. A mature CDMO should aim for Strategy 1 wherever possible.

Practice Questions — Section 5.1  |  練習題

  1. Your CDMO is deploying 15 new workstations to support the QC laboratory. How would you apply the building-block qualification strategy, and what is the qualification scope difference between qualifying the workstation "type" vs. each individual instance?
    您的CDMO正在部署15台新工作站支援QC實驗室。如何應用積木式確效策略？確效工作站「類型」與每個個別實例的確效範疇有何差異？
  2. When is it appropriate to use change control rather than a full qualification process for additions to an existing platform? Give two examples from a fill-finish CDMO context.
    何時適合使用變更控制而非對現有平台新增項目執行完整確效流程？請舉出無菌充填CDMO環境中的兩個例子。
  3. What must the Platform Project and Qualification Plan contain at minimum, and who should approve it?
    平台專案和確效計畫至少必須包含什麼內容？誰應批准它？
5.2

IT Infrastructure Life Cycle Model

IT基礎架構生命週期模型  |  Pages 25–26

Life Cycle Model Overview  |  生命週期模型概述

The following life cycle model outlines one way to manage complex IT Infrastructure projects. Smaller additions to existing IT Infrastructures may use a model that combines phases. While indicating a general flow of life cycle phases, the model is not intended to imply that all phases are strictly sequential — typically, overlap and iterations will occur during the project.

此生命週期模型概述管理複雜IT基礎架構專案的一種方式。各階段並非嚴格循序，通常會有重疊和迭代。

Life Cycle Phase 生命週期階段 Typical Deliverables 典型交付成果
Planning Phase
規劃階段（貫穿全程）		 Project Plans and Project Qualification Plans; project scope, responsibilities, deliverables and approvals, project related risks, quality/regulatory considerations, SOPs, timelines, training, funding
Specification & Design Phase
規格與設計階段		 Pertinent requirements sources; platform specifications; design specifications; degree of customization; drawings and diagrams; parameter settings; grouping of standard configurations into building blocks
Risk Assessment & Qualification Test Planning
風險評估與確效測試規劃		 Impact assessment; hazard identification; design considerations; likelihood of detection; assessment of IT Infrastructure process effectiveness; scoping of qualification; defined test/inspection specifications; acceptance criteria; reviews and approvals
Procurement, Installation & IQ Phase
採購、安裝與IQ階段		 Supplier evaluation; requests for tender; completed IQ; supplier release and installation documentation; labeling and issuance; construction, integration, assembly; tests of network assemblies; verified configuration item list; verification of SLAs/contracts/licenses; introduction of Configuration Management and change control
OQ and Acceptance Phase
OQ與驗收階段		 Operational tests and verification of specifications and agreed deliverables (completed OQ)
Reporting & Handover Phase
報告與移交階段		 Summary reports; approval of acceptance criteria; transition plans; transfer of source documents and access rights; service contract inauguration
Operation & Maintenance Phase
運營與維護階段		 Change Management; Configuration Management; Security Management; management of servers, clients and networks; Problem Management; Help Desk; Backup/Restore/Archiving; Disaster Recovery; performance monitoring; Supplier Management; Periodic Reviews
Retirement (Decommissioning) Phase
退役（停用）階段		 Decommissioning plans; data/information archiving; transfer of processes and data

IT Infrastructure V-Model Diagram  |  IT基礎架構V型模型圖

IT Infrastructure V-Model (Text-Based) | IT基礎架構V型模型

Left = definition phases | Right = verification phases | Bottom = build/test
User/Business Requirements
業務需求
━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Periodic Review & Retire
定期審查與退役
Platform Specification & Design
平台規格與設計
✦
OQ — Operational Tests
操作確效
Risk Assessment & Test Planning
風險評估與測試規劃
✦

安裝確效
↙                              ↘
Procurement, Build, Install & Configure
採購、建構、安裝與組態設定
← ACHIEVING QUALIFICATION →  |  ← MAINTAINING QUALIFICATION →

The left arm defines what the system should be. The right arm verifies that the system is as defined. The bottom is the implementation. Planning spans the entire V.

Key Life Cycle Distinctions | 關鍵生命週期區別

Phase Group Purpose QMS Hook
Achieving Qualification
達成確效		 Plan → Specify → Build → IQ → OQ → Report QA approval of plan and report
Maintaining Qualification
維持確效		 Change Control, Config Mgmt, Periodic Review Ongoing SOP compliance
Retirement
退役		 Decommission, archive, transfer Data retention compliance

Non-Sequential Nature | 非順序性特點

Unlike a waterfall model, the ISPE IT Infrastructure lifecycle explicitly acknowledges overlap and iteration. For example, risk assessment continues throughout planning and specification as more information becomes available — the initial risk assessment done during planning is refined as design details emerge.

與瀑布模型不同，ISPE明確承認各階段的重疊和迭代，尤其是風險評估持續貫穿規劃和規格階段。

Practice Questions — Section 5.2  |  練習題

  1. Match each V-model phase to its primary deliverable: (a) Specification & Design, (b) Procurement/IQ, (c) OQ & Acceptance, (d) Reporting & Handover. Then explain why the Planning phase spans the entire left arm of the V.
    將每個V型模型階段與其主要交付成果配對，並解釋為何規劃階段橫跨整個V型左臂。
  2. A colleague argues that once OQ is complete, the qualification work is done. How would you use the IT Infrastructure lifecycle model to explain why this is incorrect?
    同事認為OQ完成後確效工作就結束了。您如何用IT基礎架構生命週期模型解釋為何此觀點不正確？
  3. During the Retirement phase of an old server, what are the three key deliverables that must be produced, and why are they important from a GxP compliance perspective?
    在舊伺服器的退役階段，必須產生哪三個關鍵交付成果？從GxP合規角度，這些為何重要？
5.3

Planning — Platform Qualification Plan

規劃 — 平台確效計畫  |  Pages 27–28

5.3.1 Platform Qualification Plan  |  平台確效計畫

Separating the qualification of platforms from the validation of GxP applications means that adding or changing an application will not affect the qualified status of the platform (unless the change involved modifications to the platform).

  • GxP application validation → managed by Validation Plans (per GAMP 4)
  • Platform qualification → managed by Platform Qualification Plans

The Platform Qualification Plan should reference:

  • Applicable company policies and requirements
  • Any specific requirements derived from the applications or services the platform is intended to support
  • Any existing pre-qualified building blocks (e.g., standard server building block qualification packages)
  • Required new or referenced processes
  • Any new or modified SOPs

GAMP categorization of the platform assists with developing an appropriate qualification strategy. During preparation of the plan, an initial high level Risk Assessment should be performed based on the platform's potential to cause harm to those records and functions that the system/data owner has identified as critical.

The Platform Qualification Plan should include or refer to:

  • Responsibilities for qualification
  • Life cycle activities
  • Deliverables — specifications, test plans, test data, and reports, preferably organized to generate building blocks
  • Timelines and interdependencies
  • Required reviews and approvals
  • Constraints and prerequisites
  • Overview of IT Infrastructure platforms, components, and boundaries
  • Critical records managed by the platform
  • Training requirements
  • Initial Risk Assessments
  • Need for verification of operational procedures

QA should approve the Platform Qualification Plan and corresponding report to ensure it addresses all expected regulatory and security-related expectations.

平台確效計畫應由QA批准，涵蓋職責、生命週期活動、交付成果、時程、審查批准、限制條件、平台元件概覽、關鍵記錄、培訓要求和初步風險評估。

Qualification Planning Deliverables Table  |  確效規劃交付成果表

Deliverable 交付成果 Owner 負責人 QA Review?
QA審查?		 Timing 時機
Platform Qualification Plan
平台確效計畫		 IT / Validation Yes — approve Before any qualification activity
Initial Risk Assessment
初步風險評估		 IT / QA / App Owner Yes — review During plan preparation
Platform Specifications
平台規格		 IT Engineering Yes — review Specification & Design phase
Design Specifications
設計規格		 IT Engineering Yes — review Specification & Design phase
IQ Test Plan & Executed IQ
IQ測試計畫與執行		 Validation / IT Yes — approve Procurement & Installation phase
OQ Test Plan & Executed OQ
OQ測試計畫與執行		 Validation / IT Yes — approve OQ & Acceptance phase
Qualification Summary Report
確效摘要報告		 Validation / IT Yes — approve Reporting & Handover phase
System Inventory / Config Item List
系統清單/組態項目清單		 IT Operations Referenced Maintained ongoing
Training Records
培訓記錄		 IT / HR / QA Referenced Before and during execution

Platform vs. Application Qualification: Separation of Concerns | 平台與應用程式確效的分離

The explicit separation of Platform Qualification Plans from Application Validation Plans is a strategic design that enables "horizontal" (platform-based) qualification. When a platform is pre-qualified, multiple GxP applications can leverage that qualification without re-executing the same infrastructure tests — dramatically reducing total validation effort.

平台確效計畫與應用確效計畫的明確分離使「水平」（基於平台）確效成為可能，多個GxP應用程式可利用預先確效的平台，大幅減少總體確效工作量。

Timeline Interdependency Example | 時程相依性範例

For a new IT Infrastructure: network qualification must complete before hardware/server/client qualification commences. However, separate teams could perform work in parallel on a given network qualification, utilizing pre-qualified client building blocks. Planning must capture these dependencies explicitly.

Practice Questions — Section 5.3.1  |  練習題

  1. Your CDMO is upgrading the LIMS application software. The LIMS vendor specifies a new minimum server OS version. What is the correct sequence of qualification activities, and which qualification plan documents would need to be updated or newly created?
    您的CDMO正在升級LIMS應用程式。LIMS供應商指定了新的最低伺服器OS版本。確效活動的正確順序是什麼？哪些確效計畫文件需要更新或新建？
  2. Explain how the building-block concept in Platform Qualification Planning creates a "horizontal qualification" benefit across multiple GxP applications, and give a concrete example.
    解釋平台確效計畫中的積木式概念如何為多個GxP應用程式創造「水平確效」優勢，並舉一個具體例子。
  3. During the preparation of a Platform Qualification Plan, what level of Risk Assessment is required, and what is the key input from the application/data owner?
    在準備平台確效計畫期間，需要什麼層次的風險評估？應用程式/數據擁有者的關鍵輸入是什麼？
5.3.2

Considerations for Legacy Platforms

舊有平台的考量事項  |  Pages 28–30

Legacy Platform Definition & Approach  |  舊有平台定義與方法

A legacy platform, in the context of this Guide, is a platform that has been in use for some time without any formal qualification.

Key questions for such a platform include:

  • What are the functional, performance, and security requirements for the platform?
  • What is the status of existing processes?
  • Is there an established QMS or a list of SOPs?
  • Is there an updated inventory, high level network diagram, or configuration item list?

Experience Report | 經驗報告

For a legacy platform that is running in a substantiated satisfactory manner, any intensive testing of the system may affect the continued operation. Therefore, consideration should be given to the production of an 'Experience Report' that summarizes the inventory and operational status and history of the platform, as a basis for further planning.

對於運行令人滿意的舊有平台，密集測試可能影響持續運行，因此可考慮製作「經驗報告」作為進一步規劃的基礎。

Given the often extensive nature of IT Infrastructures, qualification of legacy platforms is likely to be a significant exercise that should be carefully planned, budgeted, and resourced. This is further complicated by the fact that the IT Infrastructure is subject to a high degree of change.

5.3.2.1 Determining Extent of Qualification  |  確定確效範圍

The legacy IT Infrastructure should be audited against company procedures and current regulatory expectations. Gaps should be identified and documented; Risk Assessments should be used to justify which legacy platforms require qualification to remediate identified gaps.

Key regulatory and business drivers for qualifying the IT Infrastructure include:

Driver Category 驅動因素類別 Specific Concerns 具體考量
Impact on GxP Applications
對GxP應用程式的衝擊		 Impact of platform failure; impact of platform changes
Maintaining Secure Environment
維護安全環境		 External connections; access control to GxP applications; access control to platform; securing GxP records
Facilitating Disaster Recovery
促進災難復原		 Network diagrams; inventory of components; configuration management and change control; document management

Legacy Qualification Strategy & Testing Priorities  |  舊有平台確效策略與測試優先順序

5.3.2.2 Existing Documentation | 現有文件最大化利用

Maximum use of existing documentation should be made to minimize timelines and rework effort. Focus should be on the required document content being present and accurate, rather than document formatting.

It is probable that relevant information and documentation for the support of platform qualification will already exist within application validation documentation and records.

應最大化利用現有文件以縮短時程和減少返工。重點應放在文件內容的存在性和準確性，而非格式。

5.3.2.3 Legacy Testing Priority Order | 舊有平台測試優先順序

Priority should be given to critical platform components identified by the Risk Assessment:

Test Type 測試類型 Purpose 目的 Note 注意事項
Basic IQ — Installation Verifications Verify hardware/software items match documented specifications Re-installing working components solely for IQ documentation may NOT be appropriate — highlight in Risk Assessment
Confirming Verifications Confirm key configuration settings match documented specifications Config reports and screenshots sufficient
Operational Tests (OQ) Identify potential gaps or issues relating to reliable operation Also basis for performance/monitoring procedures

OQ areas for legacy systems to consider: Storage Capacity, Response Times, Concurrent Sessions/Users, Availability, Backup/Recovery Testing, Access Security Processes/Procedures

For existing IT Infrastructures performing satisfactorily: stress and load testing is NOT a priority unless there are specific, reported performance issues.

CDMO Real-World Context | CDMO真實情境

Most CDMOs inheriting IT infrastructure from a parent company or previous owner face this exact scenario. A common approach: generate an Experience Report documenting the current state, perform a gap analysis against GAMP/21 CFR Part 11 requirements, and use the risk assessment to prioritize remediation — focusing first on access control, backup, and data integrity controls for GxP systems, before addressing documentation formatting issues.

大多數繼承IT基礎架構的CDMO面臨此情境。常見方法：生成經驗報告→差距分析→風險評估確定優先順序→先聚焦存取控制、備份和數據完整性。

Critical Warning on Re-Installation | 重新安裝的關鍵警告

ISPE explicitly warns that re-installing working GxP components solely to generate IQ documentation is often not appropriate — the act of re-installation itself introduces risk to the live system. The risk assessment must justify whether documentation-only approaches (configuration reports, vendor documentation) are sufficient, or whether re-installation is truly necessary.

Legacy Platform Qualification Planning Checklist  |  舊有平台確效規劃清單

  • Audit legacy IT infrastructure against company procedures and regulatory expectations 審查舊有IT基礎架構
  • Identify and document all gaps 識別並記錄所有差距
  • Perform Risk Assessment to justify qualification priorities 執行風險評估以確定確效優先順序
  • Produce Experience Report for satisfactorily operating systems 為運行良好的系統製作經驗報告
  • Identify existing documentation reusable for qualification 識別可重用的現有文件
  • Review application validation packages for platform info 審查應用程式確效文件包中的平台資訊
  • Develop remediation plan with budget and resource allocation 制定含預算和資源的補救計畫
  • Prioritize IQ/OQ based on Risk Assessment outcomes 依風險評估結果排定IQ/OQ優先順序
  • Confirm network diagrams and component inventory current 確認網路圖和元件清單為最新
  • Assess access control and security posture 評估存取控制和安全態勢
  • Verify backup and disaster recovery procedures 驗證備份和災難復原程序
  • Establish configuration management and change control 建立組態管理和變更控制

Comparing New vs. Legacy Qualification Approach  |  新建與舊有平台確效方法比較

Aspect 層面 New Platform 新建平台 Legacy Platform 舊有平台
Starting point Clean-slate requirements Gap analysis vs. current state
Documentation base Created from scratch Leverage existing records
Testing approach Full IQ/OQ as designed Risk-based; may use Experience Report
Re-installation risk Not applicable Avoid unless Risk Assessment justifies
Stress/load testing Considered per risk NOT a priority if performing satisfactorily
Planning complexity Moderate High — carefully planned, budgeted, resourced
Key regulatory drivers GxP app requirements GxP impact, security, disaster recovery

Practice Questions — Section 5.3.2  |  練習題

  1. Your CDMO has acquired a manufacturing site that has been operating for 12 years with no formal IT qualification. The site runs a legacy LIMS and MES on servers with no IQ/OQ documentation. Describe your step-by-step approach to qualify this legacy environment, citing ISPE sections and the role of the Experience Report.
    您的CDMO收購了一個運營12年但無正式IT確效的製造場址。該場址在沒有IQ/OQ文件的伺服器上運行舊有LIMS和MES。請描述確效此舊有環境的逐步方法，引用ISPE條款並說明經驗報告的作用。
  2. During legacy qualification planning, a team member proposes re-installing the operating system on all GxP servers to generate clean IQ documentation. What is the ISPE position on this, and what alternative approach would you recommend?
    在舊有確效規劃期間，團隊成員建議重新安裝所有GxP伺服器的作業系統以生成清晰的IQ文件。ISPE對此的立場是什麼？您會推薦什麼替代方法？
  3. A legacy network has no current network diagram and the component inventory hasn't been updated in 3 years. Under which of the three legacy qualification driver categories does this fall, and what should be the immediate remediation steps?
    舊有網路沒有最新的網路圖，元件清單3年未更新。這屬於哪個舊有確效驅動因素類別？應採取哪些立即補救步驟？
∑

Section Summary & Key Takeaways

章節摘要與關鍵要點  |  Chapters 3–5.3

Core Principles Summary  |  核心原則摘要

Chapter 3 — QMS for IT | IT的QMS

  • IT infrastructure needs its own QMS with 9 defined elements
  • QA approves the IT Quality Manual, Qualification Plans, and audit findings
  • Testing rigor is proportional to impact and risk of the component
  • Periodic Reviews maintain qualified status throughout operational life
  • IT staff must not independently assess GxP compliance

Chapter 4 — Risk Management | 風險管理

  • 5-step process: Identify → Assess → Implement Controls → Assess Changes → Monitor
  • CIA triad (Confidentiality, Integrity, Availability) maps to GxP hazard categories
  • Non-GxP systems on GxP infrastructure must be included in risk assessment
  • Risk assessment is iterative — not a one-time event
  • Every change to a qualified component requires risk assessment

Chapters 5.1–5.3 — Qualification Planning | 確效規劃

  • Two qualification strategies: Building-Block (preferred) vs. Case-by-Case
  • IT lifecycle V-model: Planning → Specification → Risk Assessment → IQ → OQ → Report → Operations → Retirement
  • Platform Qualification Plan must be approved by QA before any qualification activity
  • Platform qualification is separate from application validation — enabling horizontal reuse
  • Legacy platforms: gap audit → risk assessment → Experience Report → targeted IQ/OQ
  • Re-installation of working legacy systems for IQ docs is generally not appropriate

How This Section Connects to CDMO Operations  |  與CDMO運營的連結

Operational Relevance for Aseptic Fill-Finish CDMOs | 對無菌充填CDMO的運營相關性

ISPE Requirement CDMO Operational Impact
IT Quality Manual approved by QA QA must be actively engaged in IT governance — not just auditing at year-end
Risk-based qualification scope Saves resources: focus qualification on MES/LIMS/BAS servers, not the office WiFi
Building-block strategy Pre-qualify a standard server type once; deploy 20 more with abbreviated qualification
Change = risk assessment Every OS patch on a GxP server needs a qualification impact assessment first
Periodic Review maintains status Annual IT infrastructure review is a GxP requirement, not optional
Platform ≠ Application qualification Customer auditors may ask: "Is the server platform qualified separately from the application?"

Self-Assessment Checklist for Your Site | 場址自評清單

  • Does your site have an IT Quality Manual approved by QA?
  • Are IT roles and responsibilities formally documented?
  • Is there a risk assessment covering all IT components supporting GxP applications?
  • Do all qualified IT components have an IQ/OQ on file?
  • Does your change control process cover IT infrastructure changes?
  • Is there a Platform Qualification Plan for each qualified platform type?
  • Are periodic reviews of IT infrastructure scheduled and documented?
  • For legacy systems — is there an Experience Report or equivalent?
