5.7

OQ and Acceptance  |  運行確效與驗收

Operational qualification testing for IT platforms — the final stage before handover

Original Text (ISPE GAMP)  |  原文

The final stage of Qualification is to confirm that the IT Infrastructure component operates in an expected manner as defined in appropriate specifications.

Provided the platforms are all commercially available standard products, the focus of OQ should be to test connectivity and where applicable capacity using integrated or computerized tools, rather than core functionality.

At a minimum, OQ should consist of a set of instructions to be followed, which describe the necessary test steps, expected results, and evidence to be collected. OQ should be based on the outcome of the Risk Assessments already carried out to verify that the sum of requirements derived from serviced applications, if applicable, are met.

Typical tests to consider would include:

  • Verification of key Data Management Software (e.g., database connectivity)
  • Verification of all permanent IP-addresses, and response times under conditions specified by the Qualification Plan
  • Verification of the routing pattern under conditions required by the Qualification Plan (e.g., trace network packet to destination)
  • Verification of security settings across all platform components and checking that default passwords have been altered
  • Verification of critical firewall features — positive and negative testing
  • Verification of key Operating System (OS) functionality (e.g., accessibility to defined disk volumes)
  • Verification of time synchronization

Tests should be traceable to requirements where appropriate. In simple cases, IQ and OQ may be combined in one activity; however, the sequence of installation followed by operational testing should be maintained unless pre-qualified building blocks are used.

Commentary & CDMO Application  |  解析與製藥應用

What is OQ for IT Infrastructure?  |  IT基礎架構OQ是什麼？

OQ (Operational Qualification) for IT platforms is NOT about testing software features. It proves that the platform operates as intended — connectivity works, security is configured, time is synchronized. Think of it as testing the "road" before allowing "cars" (applications) to drive on it.

IT平台的OQ不是測試軟體功能，而是確認平台本身如預期運作：連通性正常、安全設定正確、時間同步一致。如同在讓應用程式「上路」前，先確認「道路」本身沒問題。

OQ Test Categories for IT  |  IT OQ測試類別

Category 類別 What to Test 測試內容 GxP Risk 風險
Connectivity 連通性 IP addresses, response times, routing paths, DNS resolution Application unavailability
Security 安全 Default passwords changed, firewall rules (positive + negative), security settings Data breach, unauthorized access
OS Functionality 作業系統 Disk volumes accessible, OS services running, time synchronization Data integrity, audit trail accuracy
Data Management 資料管理 Database connectivity, query response, backup connectivity Data loss, record inaccessibility
Performance 效能 Capacity under load, throughput, latency benchmarks System slowdown affecting operations

Key OQ Principles  |  OQ關鍵原則

  • Risk-based scope: OQ tests are derived from the Risk Assessment output — not everything needs testing, only what matters for GxP applications.
  • Firewall negative testing: You must prove the firewall BLOCKS what it should block, not just that it allows what it should allow.
  • Traceability: Each test should link back to a documented requirement.
  • IQ+OQ combined: Allowed for simple systems, but installation sequence must always precede operational testing.

CDMO Analogy  |  CDMO比喻

In sterile manufacturing, we test autoclave OQ by running temperature distribution studies at specified loads. For IT, we run OQ by testing network connectivity at specified loads, firewall rules with both valid and invalid traffic, and database response under concurrent users — same risk-based logic, different technology.

就像滅菌釜OQ要在規定負載下測溫度分布，IT OQ要在規定條件下測網路連通性與防火牆規則。邏輯相同，技術不同。

OQ Activity Summary Table  |  OQ活動摘要表

Test Area 測試項目 Test Method 測試方法 Expected Evidence 預期證據 Risk if Failed 失敗風險 GxP Relevance GxP相關性
IP Address Verification IP位址驗證 ping / nslookup commands All IPs respond within specified time Applications unreachable High — 21 CFR Part 11 system availability
Network Routing 網路路由 traceroute to critical destinations Expected hop path documented Data routed via insecure paths High — data integrity
Security Settings 安全設定 Automated security scan + manual review Default passwords changed; hardening checklist signed Unauthorized system access Critical — audit trail integrity
Firewall Rules 防火牆規則 Positive + negative traffic injection tests Allowed traffic passes; blocked traffic denied with log Unauthorized data transfer Critical — data confidentiality
Time Synchronization 時間同步 Compare server clock vs. NTP source Drift within acceptable tolerance (e.g., ±1 sec) Audit trail timestamps inaccurate Critical — 21 CFR Part 11 §11.10(e)
Database Connectivity 資料庫連通 Connection test + query execution Connection established; query returns expected result Data inaccessible or corrupt High — data integrity
Disk Volume Access 磁碟存取 Read/write test to critical volumes Expected permissions; data written and read correctly Data loss on system failure High — backup readiness
Backup/Restore Test 備份復原測試 Execute backup; restore to test environment Data restored matches source; no missing records Cannot recover critical GxP data Critical — regulatory record retention
Performance Baseline 效能基準 Load simulation at specified concurrent users Response time within SLA; no errors under load System degradation during peak use Medium — operational continuity
5.8

Reporting and Handover  |  確效報告與移交

Qualification report content and handover from project team to operations

Original Text (ISPE GAMP)  |  原文

Following the successful execution of Installation and Operational Qualification specifications and closure of any issues, a report should be written which confirms that all of the specified activities have been successfully completed, as well as confirming that all the critical processes are described and implemented. The report should be reviewed and approved by QA.

Depending on the project characteristics, this could be a single report, one per building block, one per platform, or a combination thereof.

The approved report enables platform owners to demonstrate compliance to auditors and inspectors, and provides assurance to application owner(s) that the platforms are in a state of control.

Once all these activities have been confirmed and approved, the platform is ready to load the application and any migrated data and platform qualification documentation produced should support the validation of the application(s).

Commentary & Application  |  解析與應用

Qualification Report — Required Content  |  確效報告必要內容

  • Reference to the Qualification Plan and applicable specifications
  • Summary of IQ and OQ execution results (all tests, pass/fail status)
  • Disposition of all deviations and issues found during testing
  • Confirmation that critical processes are documented and implemented
  • QA review and approval signatures with dates
  • Statement that the platform is in a qualified, controlled state
  • List of outstanding items (if any), with risk assessment

Handover: Project Team → Operations  |  移交：項目組 → 運維組

IQ Complete
→
OQ Complete
→
Issues Closed
→
Report Approved (QA)
→
Handover to Ops
→
Application Load

The handover package should include: qualification documentation, SOPs for ongoing management, configuration baselines, and agreed SLAs with the operations team.

CDMO Perspective  |  CDMO視角

In a CDMO, the qualification report for IT infrastructure (e.g., LIMS server, MES platform) is a prerequisite for loading validated GxP applications. Auditors from clients (e.g., Big Pharma) will request this report during technical audits to verify that the underlying platform is controlled before they trust the application data it hosts.

在CDMO，IT基礎架構確效報告是載入經驗證GxP應用程式的先決條件。客戶稽查時會索取此報告，以驗證平台在承載其應用程式資料前已受控。

Report Granularity Options  |  報告顆粒度選項

  • Single report: Suitable for simple, single-platform deployments
  • Per building block: Useful for pre-qualified component approach — reusable across projects
  • Per platform: Best for complex multi-server environments where each platform serves different applications
  • Combined: Building block summaries rolled into a platform-level report
6

Maintaining the Qualified State During Operation  |  維持運行期間的合規狀態

Overview of 13 operational management processes — the ongoing discipline after handover

Original Text (ISPE GAMP)  |  原文

The IT Infrastructure typically changes frequently, sometimes on a daily or hourly basis, depending on the size of the infrastructure. The IT Infrastructure should be maintained in a documented state of control by ensuring appropriate:

  • Change Management
  • Configuration Management
  • Security Management
  • Server Management
  • Client Management
  • Network Management
  • Problem Management
  • Help Desk Provision
  • Backup, Restore, and Archiving
  • Disaster Recovery
  • Performance Monitoring
  • Supplier Management
  • Periodic Review

In order to be efficient and cost-effective, the required documented state of control should be achieved and maintained in an appropriate manner, e.g., automatic tools available should be exploited wherever possible. The use of a documented QMS should address all the listed requirements.

Chapter 6 Operational Management — 13 Processes Overview  |  第六章：13個運營管理程序

# Process 程序 核心目的 GxP Link GxP連結
6.1 Change Management 管理變更對GxP應用的影響 Re-qualification trigger
6.2 Configuration Management 記錄並控制所有組態項目(CI) Baseline & restoration
6.3 Security Management 保護CIA三原則（機密、完整、可用） Data integrity / Part 11
6.4 Server Management 確保伺服器效能、可用性與安全 Application uptime
6.5 Client Management 管理終端設備的更新、修補與安全 Endpoint security
6.6 Network Management 確保網路可用性與效能；更新拓撲圖 Connectivity / data flow
6.7 Problem Management 追蹤並解決問題根因，趨勢分析 CAPA / deviation
6.8 Help Desk 日常支援使用者；記錄案例 Operational continuity
6.9 Backup, Restore & Archiving 保護資料完整性；授權還原控制 Record retention / recovery
6.10 Disaster Recovery 減少關鍵應用停機時間 Business continuity
6.11 Performance Monitoring 持續確認平台符合SLA及合規狀態 Continued qualification
6.12 Supplier Management 管理供應商評估、合約及SLA Vendor qualification
6.13 Periodic Review 確認GxP程序仍有效並合規 Revalidation / requalification

The "Living System" Concept  |  活系統概念

Qualification is not a one-time event. IT infrastructure changes daily — patches, new users, network topology updates. The 13 processes are the quality system that keeps the platform in a "state of control" between requalification events. Each process is a gear in the machine. If one gear stops, the whole machine is at risk.

確效不是一次性活動。IT基礎架構每天在變。這13個程序就是讓平台在確效事件之間持續保持「受控狀態」的品質體系。

6.1

Change Management & Configuration Management  |  變更管理與組態管理

Sections 6.1–6.2: The inseparable pair that controls all platform evolution

6.1 Change Management  |  變更管理

The change control process cannot be separated from Configuration Management. When changes are proposed, both change control and Configuration Management activities need to be considered in parallel, particularly when evaluating impact of changes.

Due to the simplicity, the frequency and occasionally the urgency of some changes (e.g., network port patching or security patching), change control procedures need to accommodate timely and effective, yet documented, updating methods.

Change management processes should define how changes to configuration items should be managed, and should include an assessment of the impact on supported GxP applications and the extent of re-qualification required, where applicable.

6.2 Configuration Management  |  組態管理

Configuration Management (CM) covers the identification, recording, and reporting of components, including their version, constituent components, and relationships.

As a minimum, all items identified as critical for maintaining the qualified state of the platforms should be kept under CM — providing an approved baseline for further evolution and allowing safe restoration of a qualified baseline in case of problems.

Components are typically referred to as Configuration Items (CIs). CIs include hardware items, software items, critical parameter settings, documentation, and any other part of the IT Infrastructure that an organization wishes to control.

CIs are defined down to the lowest level at which a component can be independently installed, replaced, or modified.

GxP Impact Analysis  |  GxP影響評估框架

Change Control Decision Tree for IT  |  IT變更管控決策樹

Change Type 變更類型 GxP Impact? Required Action 必要行動
Emergency security patch (緊急安全修補) Assess Expedited review; document retrospectively if urgent
OS version upgrade (作業系統升級) High Full change control + re-qualification assessment
Network cable swap (網路線替換) Low Standard work order; update CI record
Firewall rule change (防火牆規則變更) High Change control + OQ retest of affected rules
New server added (新增伺服器) High Full IQ/OQ for new component
Antivirus update (防毒更新) Low Standard update; log in CM system

Configuration Items (CIs) — Examples  |  組態項目範例

  • Hardware CIs: Servers, switches, routers, UPS units, storage arrays
  • Software CIs: OS versions, application versions, firmware, drivers
  • Settings CIs: IP address tables, firewall rule sets, NTP server assignments
  • Documentation CIs: Network diagrams, configuration baseline documents, SOPs

The CM baseline = the approved "photograph" of the system at qualification. Any deviation from baseline requires change control.

CM基準線 = 確效時系統的核准「快照」。任何偏離基準線的變更均需變更管控。

CDMO Example: Security Patching Urgency  |  CDMO案例：緊急安全修補

A critical vulnerability (e.g., zero-day exploit) requires immediate patching of the LIMS server. The change control process must accommodate this urgency — many regulated companies use an "emergency change" category with: (1) management approval by phone/email, (2) full documentation within 24 hours, (3) retrospective QA review within 5 business days.

關鍵漏洞需立即修補LIMS伺服器。多數法規公司採用「緊急變更」類別：先電話/email核准，24小時內完整記錄，5個工作天內QA回溯審查。

6.3

Security Management  |  安全管理

CIA triad: Confidentiality, Integrity, Availability — protecting regulated data and systems

Original Text (ISPE GAMP)  |  原文

IT Infrastructure security is required both for business purposes and to satisfy various regulations. Lack of security may compromise availability of applications and services, record integrity and confidentiality, reputation with stakeholders, and may lead to unauthorized use of systems that ultimately would impact on product quality.

Information security is often characterized as the preservation of:

  • Confidentiality — ensuring that information is accessible only to those authorized to have access
  • Integrity — safeguarding the accuracy and completeness of information and processing methods
  • Availability — ensuring that authorized users have access to information and associated assets when required

Information security is achieved by implementing a suitable set of controls, which could include:

  • Security incident management
  • Intrusion detection
  • Server hardening (remove superfluous applications, tools, and blocking unused ports)
  • Virus signature updates
  • Considerations to origin of software (from approved suppliers only)
  • Disaster recovery planning
  • User access administration

CIA Triad in Pharma IT  |  製藥IT資訊安全三角

CIA Triad — GxP Implications  |  CIA三原則的GxP含義

Principle 原則 Pharma Meaning 製藥意義 Violation Example 違反範例 Regulatory Risk 法規風險
Confidentiality 機密性 Only authorized personnel access batch records, formulas, patient data Competitor accesses proprietary process data IP loss; potential 483 if patient data involved
Integrity 完整性 Batch records, analytical results, audit trails are accurate and unaltered Audit trail modified or deleted Critical — data integrity warning letter
Availability 可用性 Systems accessible when needed for GxP operations LIMS down during critical batch release window Production delay; potential batch failure

Server Hardening Checklist  |  伺服器強化清單

  • Remove all unnecessary software and services
  • Close all unused network ports
  • Change all default credentials
  • Enable audit logging for all privileged actions
  • Configure automatic session timeout
  • Apply OS and application security patches on schedule
  • Restrict admin access to named accounts only
  • Enable intrusion detection / alerting
  • Only install software from approved suppliers

Key Regulatory Connection  |  法規關聯

21 CFR Part 11 §11.10: Requires systems to "limit system access to authorized individuals" — directly maps to Confidentiality controls.

EU GMP Annex 11 §7.1: Requires physical and logical access controls for computerized systems.

Data Integrity Guidance (MHRA/FDA): Integrity of audit trails depends on security controls preventing unauthorized modification.

6.4–5

Server Management & Client Management  |  伺服器管理與用戶端管理

Ensuring availability, performance, and security of servers and client devices

6.4 Server Management  |  伺服器管理

The objective of the server management process is to ensure that specified requirements for operational availability, performance, and security are consistently fulfilled by the server. An important part of the process is to manage the server configuration and changes needed to meet the objectives.

The handling and qualification of changes depend on the potential impact that a given change may have on the served platforms and applications. If the change affects GxP applications, the extent of re-qualification required should be considered.

6.5 Client Management  |  用戶端管理

The objective for the Client Management process is to ensure that specified requirements for operational availability, performance, and security are consistently fulfilled by the client. An important part of the process is to manage preparation, deliveries, adaptations, patching, and security issues for the multitude of stationary and mobile units in use across the organization.

The Client Management Group is advised to use computerized tools where possible to centrally manage updates, patches, and security scans to enforce corporate policies.

Practical Guidance  |  實務指引

Server vs. Client Management — Key Differences  |  伺服器與用戶端管理的差異

Aspect 面向 Server Management 伺服器 Client Management 用戶端
Volume 數量 Few, high-criticality systems Many (10s–100s) diverse endpoints
Change frequency 變更頻率 Controlled, less frequent Frequent (patches, updates)
Management approach 管理方式 Manual + automated monitoring Central push tools (SCCM, Intune)
GxP impact 影響 Typically high (hosts applications) Variable (depends on use)
Re-qual trigger 再確效觸發 OS/hardware changes → assess Standard updates → usually low

Analogy  |  比喻

Server management is like maintaining the central pharmaceutical manufacturing suite — high-stakes, tightly controlled, few but critical. Client management is like managing the gowning lockers and workstations throughout the facility — many, diverse, requiring centralized policy enforcement to be efficient.

伺服器管理像維護核心無菌灌裝間——少量但高度關鍵。用戶端管理像管理全廠更衣室與工作站——數量多樣，需集中政策執行才能有效。

CDMO Challenge: Mobile Devices  |  CDMO挑戰：行動裝置

CDMOs increasingly use tablets and mobile devices for batch record reviews and real-time shop-floor data capture. These must be included in client management scope — same patching, security scanning, and access control requirements apply. A bring-your-own-device (BYOD) policy for GxP operations is generally not recommended.

CDMO日益使用平板與行動裝置進行批次記錄審查。這些設備必須納入用戶端管理範圍，不建議GxP操作使用BYOD政策。

6.6–7

Network Management & Problem Management  |  網路管理與問題管理

Maintaining network performance and proactively managing infrastructure problems

6.6 Network Management  |  網路管理

The objective of Network Management is to ensure that specified requirements for operational availability, performance, and security are consistently fulfilled by the network. Fulfillment of this objective involves identification and use of effective and reliable computerized tools, applications, and devices to assist network staff in monitoring and maintaining network performance in support of other platforms and services.

Network diagrams should be updated when the topology changes during maintenance and the inventory list of components should be updated to reflect the actual network configuration.

6.7 Problem Management  |  問題管理

Problem Management includes control and active management of both problems and errors. A 'problem' is an unknown underlying cause of one or more incidents, and a known error is a problem that is successfully diagnosed, and for which a workaround has been identified.

All filed problems should be tracked and resolved via approved channels; those that require changes should be input to the Change Management Group.

Problem Management should trend problem reports and strive to counteract escalation of problems by providing timely reports to the platform administration, e.g., to avoid severe service degradation caused by growing congestion in a given network segment.

Commentary & Application  |  解析與應用

Network Management — Key Requirements  |  網路管理關鍵要求

  • Live network diagrams: Topology documentation must reflect actual configuration — stale diagrams = non-compliance finding
  • Inventory accuracy: Every switch, router, cable must be tracked in the CM system
  • Monitoring tools: Use automated tools (e.g., SNMP monitoring, bandwidth analyzers)
  • Alert limits: Define thresholds; alerts trigger investigation, not just logging
  • Segmentation records: Document network zones (e.g., GxP vs. non-GxP segments) and firewall boundaries

Problem vs. Incident vs. Change  |  問題/事件/變更的區別

Term 術語 Definition 定義 GxP Action 行動
Incident 事件 Service disruption or degradation (symptom) Log; restore service; open Problem if recurring
Problem 問題 Unknown root cause of one or more incidents RCA investigation; workaround if needed
Known Error 已知錯誤 Problem with identified root cause + workaround Document; plan permanent fix via Change Control
Change 變更 Permanent fix or improvement to the system Full change control process; re-qual assessment

Trend Analysis — Regulatory Connection  |  趨勢分析的法規意義

Trending of problem reports is not just IT best practice — it directly maps to the GxP requirement for CAPA (Corrective and Preventive Action). If the LIMS server generates 15 timeout incidents in a month, trend analysis should trigger a formal CAPA, not just 15 individual tickets. This is what inspectors look for during data integrity audits.

問題報告趨勢分析直接對應GxP的CAPA要求。若LIMS每月出現15次逾時，應觸發正式CAPA，而非15張個別工單。

6.8–9

Help Desk & Backup / Restore / Archiving  |  服務台與備份、還原、封存

User support infrastructure and data protection — protecting records in regulated environments

6.8 Help Desk  |  服務台

The Help Desk process has the goal of providing the day-to-day support to users of the IT Infrastructure with problems, questions, and general support needs. Staff employed in the Help Desk must be technically skilled with respect to the actual platforms and technology used in the IT Infrastructure to support the business processes in the company.

The Help Desk is typically contacted via a central point (e.g., telephone or using a web application), where the Help Desk case is either solved immediately, or registered in a Help Desk system that manages the Help Desk process.

Where a Help Desk case requires the involvement of subject matter experts, the Help Desk service forms the liaison between the user and those experts.

6.9 Backup, Restore, and Archiving  |  備份、還原與封存

The backup, restore, and archiving capability of data on any computer platform is essential to preserve the integrity of the information in case of system failures.

Whether a given application requires full or incremental types of backup, a Risk Assessment process should be applied to achieve an appropriate frequency, commensurate with the acceptable residual risk of losing data for a given period of time, and the resulting impact on business.

Archiving is a process that ensures long term availability of data by provisions of safe storage, indexing, and refresh activities.

When a request to perform a restoration is received, consideration should be given to whether the person requesting the restoration is authorized to do so, and whether they are authorized to view the data being restored. Procedures also should ensure that the restore process does not inadvertently overwrite data that must not be lost.

Backup/Restore for GxP — Deep Dive  |  GxP備份還原深度解析

Backup Strategy — Risk-Based Decision Matrix  |  備份策略決策矩陣

System 系統 GxP Level Backup Type 類型 Frequency 頻率 Retention 留存
LIMS (batch results) Critical Full + incremental Daily + hourly Batch record retention period
MES (batch execution) Critical Full + incremental Daily + transaction log ≥5 years or shelf-life +1 yr
Email system Low Full Weekly Business policy (e.g., 3 years)
Network config backup Medium Config snapshot After each change Until next change + 1 version
QMS documents Critical Full Daily Regulatory requirement (varies by market)

Restore Authorization Control  |  還原授權管控

This is a data integrity issue that inspectors probe: Who can request a restore? Who can execute a restore? Can the restored data overwrite live production data?

  • Restore requests must be formally authorized (not verbal)
  • Restore should go to a sandbox/test environment first when possible
  • Prevent overwrite of current production data without explicit approval
  • Log all restore activities in the audit trail
  • Verify data integrity after restore (record count, checksums)

Backup vs. Archiving — The Difference  |  備份vs封存的區別

Aspect Backup 備份 Archiving 封存
Purpose 目的 Recovery from failure 故障復原 Long-term retention 長期留存
Frequency 頻率 Daily/hourly On defined schedule (e.g., batch close)
Accessibility 存取 Fast retrieval May be offline/nearline
Data refresh 更新 Overwrites old backups Immutable; media refresh required
GxP regulation 規定 Operational continuity Regulatory record retention
6.10–11

Disaster Recovery & Performance Monitoring  |  災難復原與效能監控

Business continuity planning and ongoing qualification evidence through monitoring

6.10 Disaster Recovery  |  災難復原

Loss of vital parts of the IT Infrastructure and business applications may have serious impact on the business of a company. With the often complex configuration and interdependence of the infrastructure platforms and business applications, business becomes sensitive to even smaller incidents in the IT Infrastructure and business applications.

Therefore, Disaster Recovery is an important part of the company's Business Continuity Planning. The primary goal of Disaster Recovery is to reduce downtime of critical business applications to an acceptable level following an incident.

Disaster recovery is closely related to the identified Configuration Items (CIs) within the Configuration Management process as well as the backup, restore, and archiving process.

6.11 Performance Monitoring  |  效能監控

The objective of performance monitoring is to monitor and record satisfactory operation of the IT Infrastructure as evidence in support of its continued qualification status, and secondarily, to ensure fulfillment of the Service Level Agreement (SLA) and any other stated or implied expectations.

The review of results or alarms based on this monitoring activity will trigger maintenance, update, support, or disaster recovery activities.

To assure that platform performance requirements are continuously met, surveillance procedures should be developed and alert and action limits defined.

A baseline should be created at the time of installation (or during the Performance Qualification (PQ) of a supported software application), and actual values should be considered based upon those readings.

DR Planning & Performance for CDMOs  |  CDMO的災難復原與效能監控

CDMO Disaster Recovery Planning Framework  |  CDMO災難復原規劃框架

System 系統 RTO 復原時間目標 RPO 復原點目標 DR Strategy 策略
LIMS (批次放行) < 4 hours < 1 hour Hot standby + replicated DB
MES (生產執行) < 2 hours < 30 min Hot standby; fallback to paper BPR
QMS (文件管理) < 8 hours < 4 hours Cold standby + daily backup
Environmental Monitoring < 1 hour Real-time Redundant servers + local loggers
IT Infrastructure (AD, DNS) < 1 hour < 2 hours Redundant domain controllers

RTO = Recovery Time Objective (最長可接受停機時間) | RPO = Recovery Point Objective (最多可接受資料遺失量)

Performance Monitoring — Typical Metrics  |  效能監控典型指標

  • CPU utilization: Alert at >80%; Action at >95%
  • Memory usage: Alert at >85% of available RAM
  • Disk I/O latency: Alert when exceeds baseline + 50%
  • Network bandwidth: Alert at >70% sustained utilization
  • Application response time: Alert when >SLA threshold
  • Backup job completion: Alert on any backup failure
  • Error log rate: Alert when error frequency exceeds trend baseline

Performance Monitoring = Continued Qualification Evidence  |  效能監控 = 持續確效證據

This is a concept many IT teams miss: performance monitoring data is not just operational — it is qualification evidence. When an inspector asks "how do you know your LIMS server is still operating within the qualified state?", the answer is your performance monitoring records and trend reports.

效能監控記錄是「持續確效證據」。稽查員詢問「如何確認LIMS伺服器仍在確效狀態內運行？」，答案就是效能監控記錄與趨勢報告。

DR Testing Requirement  |  災難復原測試要求

A DR plan that is never tested is not a plan — it is a document. Regulatory expectation (particularly for 21 CFR Part 11 and EU Annex 11) is that DR plans are periodically tested (typically annually) and results documented. Test exercises must demonstrate actual data recovery capability, not just that backup files exist.

未經測試的DR計劃只是文件。法規期望定期測試（通常每年），且必須記錄實際資料復原能力，而非僅確認備份檔案存在。

6.12–13

Supplier Management & Periodic Review  |  供應商管理與定期審查

Controlling outsourced services and confirming ongoing GxP compliance

6.12 Supplier Management  |  供應商管理

The management of services and deliveries to the IT Infrastructure typically will follow the general policies of supplier management in the regulated company including evaluation of suppliers, selection of suppliers and the management of the relationships with the suppliers. Agreements between the regulated company and the supplier should be documented in contracts, or SLAs, and reviewed at appropriate intervals.

The regulated company should maintain a list of approved or preferred suppliers to ensure that the suppliers meet the company requirements regarding performance, cost, and quality. To mitigate the risk of shortage or unacceptable deliveries from a supplier it may be valuable to have more than one supplier — also known as 'second sourcing'.

To exploit the concept of building blocks, it may be advantageous to set up requirements related to the supplier regarding availability of qualified IT Infrastructure building blocks (e.g., servers, clients, SW-licenses).

6.13 Periodic Review  |  定期審查

Periodic Reviews should establish that procedures meeting current applicable GxP regulatory requirements are approved and in use. The review should establish that qualification and operational records, and review reports are complete, current, and accurate. Periodic Reviews are considered in further detail in Appendix 5 of this Guide.

Supplier & Review Framework  |  供應商與審查框架

IT Supplier Qualification Framework  |  IT供應商確效框架

Supplier Type 類型 Qualification Requirement 確效要求 SLA Key Terms 關鍵SLA條款
Cloud service provider (AWS, Azure) Security audit, compliance certifications (ISO 27001, SOC 2) Uptime ≥99.9%, data residency, audit access rights
Hardware vendor (servers, switches) Approved vendor list; delivery lead time guarantee Stock availability of qualified building blocks
Managed IT service provider Supplier audit; quality agreement Incident response time, change notification requirements
Software vendor (OS, DB) Support lifecycle commitment; patch delivery Security patch SLA; end-of-life notice period

Periodic Review — What to Assess  |  定期審查評估內容

  • Are all current SOPs approved and consistent with actual practice?
  • Have any regulatory requirements changed since the last review?
  • Are qualification records complete and current?
  • Have change controls been properly executed and closed?
  • Are problem management trends showing acceptable patterns?
  • Are all configuration items documented accurately in the CM system?
  • Are supplier SLAs being met? Any supplier issues to escalate?
  • Has DR been tested? Results documented and acceptable?
  • Are backup schedules being executed and verified?

Second Sourcing — Why It Matters in CDMO  |  備用供應商在CDMO的重要性

Single-source dependency for critical IT components is a business risk. If your only server vendor has a 12-week lead time and a server fails, production can be impacted. CDMOs should identify critical hardware components and ensure at least one alternative qualified supplier or maintain a strategic spare inventory (especially for GxP-qualified servers and network equipment).

單一供應商依賴是業務風險。CDMO應對關鍵硬體確保替代供應商或戰略備件庫存，尤其是GxP確效過的設備。

7

Retirement of Platforms  |  平台退役

Decommissioning, data migration, archival, and regulatory record retention requirements

Original Text (ISPE GAMP)  |  原文

Business applications often outlive the underlying platforms, and in such circumstances, data needs to be migrated onto the new platform(s). For example, a validated LIMS application may be operational for many years using modified versions of application software until a desirable version is released which requires a server platform update. Alternatively, the existing platform may no longer comply with company standards and become too cumbersome or even impossible to maintain, as suppliers cease providing support on economically acceptable terms.

When a platform is replaced, special consideration should be given to data migration, especially when conversion is required as part of the process.

Documented assurance should be provided that:

  • All data elements are migrated
  • All critical data attributes are preserved (e.g., security settings)
  • All supporting data are correctly transferred
  • No extra data elements are inadvertently introduced
  • Any specified conversions have consistently produced the expected results

In many cases, it may be appropriate to apply statistical methods to obtain the required assurance; in other cases, it may be necessary to devise computerized tools to provide a complete, automated verification. The verification method should be determined by assessing and documenting the risks involved.

Retirement Planning & Data Migration  |  退役規劃與數據遷移

Platform Retirement Checklist  |  平台退役清單

  • Formal retirement plan approved (project plan + timeline)
  • Data migration strategy documented (full migration or archival only?)
  • Data migration risk assessment completed
  • Verification method selected (100% check / statistical sampling / automated tool)
  • New platform IQ/OQ completed before data migration
  • Dry run migration executed in test environment
  • All data elements migrated — count verified
  • Critical data attributes preserved (security settings, audit trail, metadata)
  • No extra data elements introduced — verified by comparison
  • Data conversion results verified (e.g., format changes produce expected output)
  • Old system placed in read-only mode after migration, not immediately destroyed
  • Regulatory archive of old system data in compliant long-term storage
  • Old hardware decommissioned with data sanitization (NIST 800-88 or equivalent)
  • Retirement report written and approved by QA
  • CM system updated to remove retired components
  • Qualified supplier list updated (retired hardware models removed)

Data Migration Assurance Methods  |  資料遷移驗證方法

Data Volume 數據量 GxP Criticality Recommended Method 建議方法 Example Tool 範例工具
Small (<10,000 records) Critical 100% record-by-record comparison Database comparison script
Medium (10K–1M records) Critical Statistical sampling + checksum verification Automated migration validation tool
Large (>1M records) Critical Automated full-data integrity check (hash/checksum) Supplier-provided migration validator
Any volume Medium Representative sample (e.g., 10% or risk-stratified) Manual review + automated count check
Archival only (no active use) Low Format verification + accessibility test Document retrieval test

Regulatory Record Retention Requirements  |  法規記錄留存要求

Record Type 記錄類型 Regulation 法規 Retention Period 留存期限 Notes 備注
Batch production records 批次記錄 21 CFR 211.180 / EU GMP ≥1 year past expiry or ≥3 years post-release Longer of the two applies
Validation/qualification records 確效記錄 21 CFR 211 / EU GMP Part I Life of equipment + observation period Typically ≥5 years after system retirement
Audit trails 稽核軌跡 21 CFR Part 11 / Annex 11 Same as the records they protect Must remain readable throughout
Clinical trial data 臨床試驗資料 ICH E6(R2) / 21 CFR 312 15 years post-trial (or per protocol) Archive must remain accessible
Change control records 變更管控 EU GMP Part I Life of the changed item + defined period Links to qualification records
Computer system validation docs 電腦系統驗證 Annex 11 §4.8 Throughout system life + post-retirement Exact period per company policy / HA requirement

Data Sanitization at Retirement  |  退役時的資料清除

When retiring a server that hosted GxP data, simply deleting files is not sufficient. Use a recognized standard such as NIST SP 800-88 (Guidelines for Media Sanitization) to ensure data cannot be recovered from decommissioned hardware. Document the sanitization method and retain the certificate of destruction as part of the retirement record.

退役含有GxP資料的伺服器，刪除檔案不夠。應採用NIST SP 800-88等標準進行資料清除，並保留銷毀證明作為退役記錄的一部分。

Common Retirement Triggers  |  常見退役觸發原因

Trigger 觸發原因 Example 範例 Key Risk at Retirement 主要風險 Special Consideration 特別注意事項
Application upgrade requires new platform 應用升級需新平台 LIMS v8 requires Windows Server 2022 (current: 2012) Data migration completeness Validate new platform before migrating data
Supplier end-of-support 供應商停止支援 OS vendor stops security patches Security vulnerability if kept in service Plan replacement before EOL date; avoid operating on unsupported OS
Hardware failure beyond repair 硬體故障無法修復 RAID failure; no spare parts available Data loss during unplanned retirement DR plan should pre-authorize emergency replacement procedure
Consolidation / cloud migration 整合/雲端遷移 Multiple on-premise servers migrated to cloud Data integrity across format/platform change Cloud platform must itself be qualified; assess new security perimeter
Regulatory requirement change 法規要求變更 New data integrity expectations require audit trail upgrade Compliance gap during transition Phased retirement with parallel running period
Q

Practice Questions  |  練習題

Covering Chapters 5.7, 5.8, 6.1–6.13, and 7 — test your understanding

Block 1: OQ & Reporting (Ch. 5.7–5.8)  |  OQ與確效報告

Q1. OQ Focus for Commercial IT Platforms

When performing OQ on commercially available standard IT products (e.g., a database server running Oracle on Windows Server), what should be the primary focus of testing, and why?

Guidance: The guide is specific that for commercial off-the-shelf (COTS) products, OQ should focus on connectivity and capacity, not core functionality. Explain the rationale — the vendor has already tested core functionality. Your testing confirms it works in YOUR environment with YOUR configuration.

當對商業現成IT產品進行OQ時，主要測試重點是什麼？請說明原因。

Q2. Firewall OQ — Positive and Negative Testing

Explain the difference between positive and negative firewall testing in the context of IT OQ. Give one example of each, and explain why negative testing is critical for GxP compliance.

Guidance: Positive = traffic that should be allowed, passes. Negative = traffic that should be blocked, is blocked. The GxP relevance is data integrity and confidentiality — an improperly configured firewall could allow unauthorized data exfiltration.

說明防火牆正向測試與負向測試的差異，並各舉一例。為何負向測試對GxP合規至關重要？

Q3. Qualification Report Requirements

Your company has just completed IQ and OQ for a new LIMS server infrastructure. List five key elements that must be included in the qualification report before it can be approved by QA and used to support the subsequent LIMS application validation.

Guidance: Think about what an auditor would need to see to be confident the platform is in a state of control: test execution summary, issue disposition, critical process documentation, QA approval, and statement of qualification status.

列出確效報告在QA核准前必須包含的五個關鍵要素。

Q4. Time Synchronization — Regulatory Significance

Time synchronization is listed as a required OQ test for IT infrastructure. Explain specifically why inaccurate server clock time is a GxP data integrity issue under 21 CFR Part 11 and EU Annex 11.

說明為何伺服器時間不準確是21 CFR Part 11下的GxP資料完整性問題。

Block 2: Operational Management (Ch. 6)  |  運營管理

Q5. The 13 Operational Processes — Grouping

The guide lists 13 processes for maintaining the qualified state. Group them into three categories: (a) Change and Configuration Control, (b) Security and Infrastructure, (c) Continuity and Oversight. Which processes belong in each group?

Guidance: (a) Change Management, Configuration Management. (b) Security Management, Server Management, Client Management, Network Management. (c) Problem Management, Help Desk, Backup/Restore/Archiving, Disaster Recovery, Performance Monitoring, Supplier Management, Periodic Review.

將13個程序分為三組：變更/組態管控、安全/基礎架構、持續性/監督。

Q6. Emergency Security Patch — Change Control Dilemma

A critical zero-day security vulnerability has been disclosed for your LIMS server's OS. A patch is available from Microsoft. The standard change control process takes 10 business days. How should you handle this situation in a GxP-regulated CDMO environment?

Guidance: Use the emergency change category — expedited approval (phone/email), apply patch, document within 24 hours, QA retrospective review within 5 business days. The guide acknowledges urgency must be accommodated while still being documented.

零日漏洞補丁需緊急安裝，但標準變更流程需10個工作天。在GxP環境中如何處理？

Q7. CIA Triad — Practical Application

For each element of the CIA triad (Confidentiality, Integrity, Availability), identify one specific threat to a CDMO's pharmaceutical IT environment and one specific control that addresses it.

針對CIA三原則各項，識別一個針對CDMO製藥IT環境的具體威脅及其對應管控措施。

Q8. Backup vs. Archiving — Regulatory Context

A batch released 3 years ago used an HPLC system whose data was stored on a server that has now been decommissioned. The backup tapes from 3 years ago still exist. Is this sufficient for regulatory compliance? What additional requirements apply?

Guidance: Backup alone may not be sufficient. The data must remain accessible and readable for the required retention period. The backup media must be periodically refreshed, and the format must remain readable with available software — this is archiving, not just backup.

3年前批次的HPLC資料備份磁帶存在，是否足以滿足法規要求？還需要什麼？

Block 3: Platform Retirement (Ch. 7)  |  平台退役

Q9. Data Migration — Five Assurance Requirements

The ISPE guide specifies five documented assurance requirements for data migration during platform retirement. List all five and for each one, provide a practical example of how you would verify it for a LIMS migration from an Oracle database on Windows Server 2012 to Windows Server 2022.

Guidance: (1) All data elements migrated — record count comparison. (2) Critical data attributes preserved — security settings, timestamps, audit trail. (3) Supporting data correctly transferred — linked documents, attachments. (4) No extra data introduced — row count and data hash comparison. (5) Conversions produced expected results — test specific data format changes.

列出資料遷移的五個文件保證要求，並說明如何在LIMS遷移中驗證每項。

Q10. Statistical Sampling for Data Migration

A CDMO is migrating 5 million batch analytical results from an old LIMS to a new system. 100% record verification would take 6 months. The guide mentions statistical methods as an acceptable approach. How would you design a statistically valid sampling plan, and what risk factors should influence your sample size?

500萬條批次分析結果需遷移。如何設計統計抽樣驗證計劃？哪些風險因素影響樣本量？

Q11. Retirement Timing — Supplier End-of-Life

Microsoft announces that Windows Server 2019 will reach end-of-extended-support in October 2029. Your LIMS runs on this OS. Describe the regulatory implications of continuing to operate after the EOL date, and outline a phased retirement and migration plan.

Guidance: After EOL, no security patches = security management process cannot be fulfilled. This compromises the qualified state. Regulators (FDA, EMA) increasingly flag unsupported OS as a data integrity risk. Plan should include: 12-18 months lead time for new platform IQ/OQ + LIMS revalidation + data migration.

描述在OS支援終止日期後繼續運行的法規影響，並概述階段性退役遷移計劃。

Q12. Decommissioning — Data Sanitization

After successfully migrating all LIMS data to a new platform, the old server is to be decommissioned and the hardware returned to the leasing company. What steps must you take regarding data sanitization, and what records should be retained?

Guidance: Simply deleting files is insufficient — data can be recovered with forensic tools. Use NIST SP 800-88 (Clear, Purge, or Destroy method based on data sensitivity). Retain certificate of destruction, record the sanitization method used, and update the CM system to remove the decommissioned CI. Consider whether the hardware contains audit trail data requiring retention evidence before sanitization.

描述伺服器退役時的資料清除要求與應保留的記錄。

Q13. Integration Question — Full Lifecycle

A CDMO is planning to replace its legacy MES platform over 18 months. Describe how the following processes from Chapter 6 must be coordinated during the transition period when both old and new systems are running in parallel: Change Management, Configuration Management, Backup/Restore, and Performance Monitoring.

說明在新舊MES平台並行運行的18個月過渡期中，如何協調變更管理、組態管理、備份復原與效能監控。

REF

Quick Reference Summary  |  快速參考摘要

Key rules and numbers from Chapters 5.7–7

Numbers to Remember  |  關鍵數字

  • 7 typical OQ test areas (connectivity, routing, security, firewall, OS, data management, time sync)
  • 5 data migration assurance requirements (all migrated, attributes preserved, supporting data, no extras, conversions verified)
  • 13 operational management processes for maintaining qualified state (Ch. 6)
  • 3 CIA security principles (Confidentiality, Integrity, Availability)
  • 2 tests for every firewall rule (positive AND negative)

Critical GxP Requirements Summary  |  關鍵GxP要求摘要

  • OQ must be risk-based and traceable to requirements
  • Qualification report must be QA-approved before application load
  • Change management must address GxP impact assessment and re-qualification need
  • Security management must implement CIA triad controls
  • Backup restore must have authorization controls
  • DR plan must be periodically tested and results documented
  • Performance monitoring data is continued qualification evidence
  • Retirement requires documented data migration assurance
  • Decommissioned hardware requires certified data sanitization

Common Audit Findings in These Areas  |  這些領域的常見稽查發現

  • OQ: Tests not traceable to documented requirements; IQ/OQ combined without justification
  • Security: Default credentials not changed; unsupported OS still in production; no intrusion detection
  • Change control: IT changes not assessed for GxP impact; emergency changes not retrospectively documented
  • Backup: Backup exists but restore procedure never tested; restore authorization not documented
  • DR: DR plan exists but never tested; no documented RTO/RPO
  • Performance: No alert limits defined; no monitoring records as continued qualification evidence
  • Retirement: Data migration not verified; no data sanitization certificate; old system destroyed before retention period
  • Network: Network diagrams not updated after changes; no change control for topology changes

"The IT Infrastructure should be maintained in a documented state of control."

— ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guide: IT Infrastructure Control and Compliance, Chapter 6

IT基礎架構應維持在有文件記錄的受控狀態。

4

Chapter 4: Appendices 1–3: Roles, Risk Assessment & Deliverables

附錄1-3：角色職責、風險評估範例與確效交付物 | App 1-3

Appendices 1–3: Roles, Risk Assessment & Qualification Deliverables

附錄一至三：職責分工、風險評估與確認交付物
ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guide: IT Infrastructure Control and Compliance | App. 1–3 (p52–p67)

本章學習目標

  • 理解 IT 基礎架構中各角色（Platform Owner、Application Owner、IT Quality & Compliance、Independent QA）的職責邊界
  • 掌握「所有權不可外包」原則——受監管公司永遠保有 QA 最終責任
  • 學習 GAMP 兩階段風險評估方法：Stage 1（可能性 × 衝擊）→ Stage 2（偵測概率）→ 風險優先級
  • 了解 Type 與 Instance 資格確認的概念差異，以及 Table A3.1 各角色在各交付物的參與方式
Appendix 1 — Roles and Responsibilities 職責分工

原文內容 Original Text

1 Introduction

Companies are organized in a variety of ways that fit each individual company's mode of operation, size, objectives, geographic layout, culture, etc.

Companies typically identify roles and responsibilities in a similar way; this Appendix discusses their interrelationships and a possible way of grouping them together.

The term 'owner' is used in this context both as a suggested title for personnel accepting ownership of a given item or process, and for the high level of accountability associated with assuming that role. Often, true ownership can be achieved only by personnel whose primary business objectives are directly dependent on the item's availability and performance.

The term 'independent QA' is used to denote the role of the Quality Assurance group as required by regulatory authorities.

Executive management is responsible for the successful implementation and qualification of the IT Infrastructure platforms, and commits and empowers resources to ensure adherence to all relevant GxP requirements, and other requirements such as those pertaining to security.

The key roles that a company may find useful to identify and allocate resources may include:

  • Executive Management
  • Project Manager
  • Application (System/Data) Owner/Administrator/SMEs
  • Data Owner, if not coincident with the Application (System) Owner
  • IT Infrastructure Process Owner/Administrator/SMEs
  • Platform Owner/Administrator/SMEs
  • Independent QA
  • IT Quality and Compliance

Roles should be organized to prevent critical objectives from being overlooked. Job descriptions should be assigned to named individuals. Such decisions should be justified and documented.

Technical and managerial staff with appropriate educational background and experience should be available. Provision of training should be planned to ensure the required skills are developed and maintained. Staff should be made aware of any regulatory requirements that apply to their duties, trained in those procedures that are applicable to them, and re-trained as changes occur. Records of training should be maintained.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：「Owner」的意義

Owner（負責人）不只是頭銜，更是一種業務問責。指南特別強調：真正的 ownership 只能由「其業務目標直接依賴該系統可用性與效能」的人承擔。

換言之，Owner 必須是使用者，不是 IT 維運人員。若系統停擺會直接衝擊他的業務 KPI，他才有動機負責。

比喻說明

就像工廠生產線的線長（Line Leader）：他不一定最懂機器原理，但機器停了他最心急——因為產量是他的責任。IT 系統的 Owner 應該是同樣心態的人，而不是「幫別人保管系統」的 IT 工程師。

重點提示：8 大角色要記住

GAMP IT 指南定義了 8 個關鍵角色。在 CDMO 中，這 8 個角色不一定對應 8 個人——一個人可能身兼多職，但每個角色的職責邊界必須書面化（Job Description + 簽名）。

練習思考

  1. 在您的組織中，LIMS 系統的「Application Owner」是哪個部門？IT 還是 QC？為什麼？
  2. 若一個人同時是 Platform Owner 和 Data Owner，這樣的安排是否有利益衝突風險？如何緩解？
§2 Executive Management & §3 Project Manager

原文內容 Original Text

2 Executive Management (Project Sponsorship)

Driven by business needs, executive management appoints members of management to assume the roles of 'sponsoring' projects and defining general requirements to the IT Infrastructure. Key initial activities include:

  • financing the initial feasibility stages
  • determining the acceptable level of risk for the organization
  • selecting steering committee members
  • developing business cases and other formalities needed to obtain a fully funded and supported project established

Close interaction with QA is recommended in these initial stages.

"Whether a regulated company owns its IT Infrastructure or leases services from service providers, it is responsible for the qualification status and should specify, therefore, expectations and monitor the continuous fulfillment of those expectations, e.g., negotiate, agree, fund, and monitor general SLAs with IT Infrastructure service providers."
"Note that ownership and quality assurance of systems and data should not be outsourced for reasons of Control and Compliance."

3 Project Manager

Controls all project activities, including:

  • Liaison with system and data owners on working processes and system requirements
  • Monitoring compliance of project deliverables with GxP and company standards for documentation, data control, training, software development (if inside the project scope), and technical support
  • Preparing the Infrastructure project and quality plan, or Infrastructure Qualification Plan
  • Review, approval, and reporting on key project deliverables under the qualification life cycle
  • Review and reporting on all change requirements
  • Assessing and managing project related risks
  • Ensuring timely resolution and escalation of issues

A critical aspect in the initial project phases is the involvement of end-users, QA, and other long term stakeholders. A smooth transfer to the platform owner is a key objective at the end of the project.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

重點提示：「不可外包的原則」

這是整個 Appendix 1 最重要的句子：「系統與資料的 Ownership 和 QA 不可外包。」

即使你把整個 IT 基礎架構委外給 AWS 或外部 IT 廠商，受監管公司仍然：

  • 保有 qualification status 的責任
  • 必須設定 SLA 期望值並監控執行
  • 不能將 QA 最終判斷外包給廠商

比喻說明

就像藥廠委外生產（CMO）：成品的 QP 放行責任仍在製造授權持有人（MAH）身上，不在 CMO。IT 也是同理——即使系統跑在 Azure 雲上，GxP compliance 的負責人仍是藥廠自己。

Project Manager vs. Platform Owner：轉移時機

Project Manager（專案經理）：在專案期間負責協調；專案完成後「交棒」給 Platform Owner 進行日常維運。

指南強調「順暢的交接」是 PM 最重要的收尾目標之一——文件必須完整，才能讓 PO 接手後繼續維持 compliance。

練習思考

  1. 您的公司使用 AWS 或 Azure 作為 IT 基礎架構，當稽核員問「誰負責 qualification？」時，您應如何回答？
  2. IT 基礎架構專案的 PM，是否需要具備 GxP 知識？為什麼？
§4 Application Owner & §5 Data Owner

原文內容 Original Text

4 Application (System/Data) Owner/Administrator/SMEs

A system consists of the application plus whatever platforms and parts of the infrastructure are required to enable the application run. Therefore, depending on the applicable approach for a given project, the application (system/data) owner(s)/administrator(s) should specify the detailed requirements a given application has of the underlying platform and IT Infrastructure processes, accordingly.

For GxP applications, the application (system/data) owner has further computer system validation specific responsibilities (see GAMP 4).

In relation to the infrastructure, the system administrator typically would have the following responsibilities:

  • creation and maintenance of all required documentation, e.g., copies of platform qualification reports, as required
  • performance of required review activities
  • liaison with the platform groups and application specialists and ensuring clarity in mutual expectations
  • managing system user access profiles and permissions
  • managing SLAs with service providers
  • managing critical records and specifying any additional requirements to security for the platform groups
  • managing or approving system specific changes including those that are initiated from the platform side and may affect application performance or record integrity
  • making appropriate use of SMEs, such as application specialists

The administrator should have a deep understanding of the system's functionality and impact on the businesses it supports or automates.

5 Data Owner

In cases where the data that a system stores, displays, manipulates, or transports are not logically owned by the application (system) owner, a company may choose to nominate data owners. For example, when the system or file storage service provides hosting capabilities for a number of users who must account for inputted data over long periods of time, owners of such data need to be aware of their responsibilities.

Data owners would be responsible for ensuring that the established quality and security provisions are adequate. Considerations should be made for the provision of:

  • backup and restoration
  • archiving
  • change management and audit trails
  • access restrictions in general and possibly specific settings
  • availability

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

三個「Owner」的區別

Application Owner（應用系統負責人）：對整個應用系統負責，包含其所依賴的 IT 基礎架構。他向 Platform Owner 提出平台需求。

Data Owner（資料負責人）：當資料的邏輯歸屬與系統管理者不同時，另立資料負責人。例如：共用檔案伺服器的各部門資料，Application Owner 是 IT，但每個部門才是自己資料的 Data Owner。

Platform Owner（平台負責人）：管理底層平台（伺服器、網路、客戶端）。

比喻說明：大樓 vs. 租戶

想像一棟辦公大樓：
Platform Owner = 大樓管理員（負責電梯、電力、空調）
Application Owner = 各樓層租戶（負責辦公室裡的業務系統）
Data Owner = 租戶的重要文件夾主人（負責自己的資料安全）

大樓出了問題，租戶提需求給管理員；但租戶自己文件的保管，是自己的責任。

重點提示：Data Integrity 的關鍵

Data Owner 必須確保的 5 項核心：備份還原、歸檔、變更管理與稽核軌跡、存取限制、可用性——這與 FDA 21 CFR Part 11 的 ALCOA+ 原則高度對應。在 GxP 環境中，Data Integrity 是監管稽查最常被挑戰的點。

練習思考

  1. 在您的 CDMO，LIMS 的 Application Owner 和 Data Owner 應該是同一人嗎？
  2. 如果備份系統故障導致 GxP 資料遺失，誰最終需要對監管機構負責？
§6 Infrastructure Process Owner & §7 Platform Owner

原文內容 Original Text

6 Infrastructure Process Owner/Administrator/SMEs

Depending on the size of a company, and thus, the infrastructure, it may be appropriate to assign dedicated staff or organizational units to take care of specific infrastructure processes.

As the objectives for the processes vary greatly so do the responsibilities of the owners, but in all cases, the scope and purpose of the process should be defined and described in SOPs or SLAs, as appropriate.

Critical tasks should be described in SOPs and approved by authorized senior staff and IT Quality and Compliance or QA, as appropriate. Ongoing assessment methods should be documented.

Key performance indicators should be established and agreed upon, including adequate reporting and escalation mechanisms.

Infrastructure process owners also may own any supporting IT Infrastructure systems, in which case, they should be aware of any GxP impact that may warrant validation.

Infrastructure process owners should support audits and be trained in good conduct during regulatory inspections within their scope of responsibility.

7 Platform Owner/Administrator/SMEs

The role of owning an infrastructure process may coincide with the role of owning a platform, e.g., the server management process may coincide with or include the ownership of a given type of server hardware platforms.

Depending on the company's size, the responsibility for each type of technical platforms would be assigned to dedicated staff or organizational units allowing them to concentrate and specialize on characteristics of each platform type, e.g., servers, networks, clients, peripherals.

If the platform supports one or more GxP applications (business or infrastructure), the platform owner should provide the necessary qualification documentation for inclusion or reference. The platform owner should:

  • decide on short and long term strategies for the platforms
  • fund the platform operation and maintenance
  • appoint a platform administrator or SMEs as needed to take care of daily operations
  • act as escalation level for complaints and major problems

The platform administrator/SMEs typically would have the following responsibilities:

  • creating and maintaining all required documentation and operating procedures
  • qualifying the platforms – including 'building blocks,' and ensuring continued compliance
  • performing required review activities
  • managing user access profiles and permissions to shared services
  • managing SLAs with service providers
  • providing second and third level support
  • managing records
  • managing the implementation of service and security patches
  • conducting ongoing performance management
  • managing the configuration and platform specific changes
  • providing expertise in the exploitation of the platform and the various versions in operation
  • initiating and supporting supplier audits, as appropriate
  • presenting the platform documents and justifying all critical decisions to QA and regulators on request

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

Platform Owner 在 CDMO 的實際角色

Platform Owner（平台負責人）是 IT 基礎架構的核心技術角色，通常分成四類平台：

  • Clients（桌電、筆電、工作站）
  • Servers（應用伺服器、資料庫伺服器）
  • Networks（區域網路、防火牆、VPN）
  • Hardware/Peripherals（印表機、標籤機、儀器介面）

每類平台可能有各自的 PO，也可能一人管多類——規模決定分工。

重點提示：向稽查員說明的準備

Platform Owner 最後一條職責很重要：「向 QA 和監管機構呈現平台文件，並為所有重要決策提出正當理由。」

這意味著 PO 必須能在稽查時上場回答技術問題，不能只說「這是 IT 的事」。在 CDMO，IT 人員需要具備基本 GxP 素養。

比喻：Infrastructure Process Owner vs. Platform Owner

Process Owner = 「制定維修 SOP 的工務主管」
Platform Owner = 「負責某類設備（如空調系統）的技術工程師」
兩個角色有時重疊（同一人），有時分開——但 SOP 必須清楚界定各自的職責範圍。

練習思考

  1. 您公司的 IT 工程師，是否被訓練過「如何在稽查時回答問題」？這是誰的責任？
  2. Security patch 的安裝屬於 Platform Owner 的職責，但它可能影響 GxP 應用系統——誰有最終決定權？
§8 Independent QA & §9 IT Quality and Compliance

原文內容 Original Text

8 Independent Quality Assurance

Quality Assurance, independent of IT, has ultimate responsibility for assessing whether compliance with regulatory and company standards is achieved and maintained.

The degree of technical literacy should be commensurate with defined responsibilities in relation to the IT Infrastructure.

QA should:

  • provide governance/oversight
  • provide high level company procedures to meet compliance obligations
  • develop and maintain policies, processes, procedures, and other guidance documents that comprise the compliance framework
  • review and approve documentation/records as appropriate, based on impact to GxP
  • plan and perform internal and external audits
  • review and approve Periodic Review reports, as appropriate
  • host regulatory inspections

9 IT Quality and Compliance

IT Quality and Compliance provides quality and compliance expertise to projects and operations in support of a controlled environment and associated processes that meet the quality and compliance requirements of the company.

IT Quality and Compliance staff need in depth compliance and technical insight, and should:

  • provide governance/oversight
  • liaise with QA to ensure alignment with the overall company compliance obligations
  • liaise with system and platform SMEs
  • liaise with appropriate industry groups to leverage and influence industry best practices and standards
  • keep abreast of the business, legal, and regulatory environment for interpretation, and assess the impact on IT Infrastructure
  • support the development and maintenance of policies, processes, procedures, and other guidance documents that comprise the compliance framework
  • review and approve documentation/records as appropriate, based on impact to GxP and business critical elements
  • escalate to QA for approval in accordance with company procedures (e.g., key documents, retention periods, critical changes)
  • provide education and awareness; develop and maintain an education program
  • train staff as appropriate
  • provide guidance/consultancy/validation management/SMEs such as test engineers
  • participate in projects, as appropriate, based on risk
  • participate in process reviews and support continuous improvement
  • perform internal quality and compliance assessments of IT processes
  • develop and maintain the assessment programs
  • perform periodic assessments/reviews
  • conduct supplier audits
  • support external audits of the IT Infrastructure organization
"The relationship between independent QA and IT Quality and Compliance, including delegation of activities, should be documented."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

兩個 QA 角色的關鍵差異

Independent QA（獨立品保）：對 IT 保持獨立，是最終監管判斷者。有最高 sign-off 權力，負責主持法規稽查。

IT Quality & Compliance（IT 合規）：深嵌在 IT 組織中，具備技術深度，是 QA 和 IT 之間的橋樑。他們不能取代 QA 的最終判斷，但可代為執行許多日常合規工作。

兩者職責的邊界必須書面化（關鍵原則）。

比喻：醫院的質量管理

Independent QA = 醫院的醫療品質委員會（外部視角，有最終否決權）
IT Quality & Compliance = 各科室的品管護士（日常操作，熟悉技術細節，向委員會匯報）

科室品管護士不能批准違反醫療規範的操作，這需要委員會——但委員會不可能盯著每個細節，所以需要科室品管護士作為第一道防線。

重點提示：CDMO 常見缺失

許多中小型 CDMO 沒有設置專門的 IT Quality & Compliance 角色——這等於讓普通 IT 工程師直接面對 QA，但工程師通常不懂 GxP 框架。結果：

  • 變更管理不完整（缺乏合規評估）
  • 稽查時 IT 人員答不出來
  • QA 無法有效監督 IT 活動

建立這個橋樑角色，是 IT compliance 成熟度的重要指標。

練習思考

  1. 在您的組織，IT 與 QA 之間是否有正式的合規橋樑角色？若無，誰在扮演這個功能？
  2. 「delegation of activities should be documented」——您的公司是否有文件化 QA 和 IT Q&C 之間的職責分工？
Appendix 2 — Example of Risk Assessment and Controls 風險評估範例

原文內容 Original Text

1 Background

Risk assessments should be performed at each major life cycle phase of any object or groups of objects (e.g., platforms or data) identified to be important or even critical for a company to fulfill its mission.

Risk Assessment may be taken to comprise two phases: risk analysis and risk evaluation. Note that NIST's Guide to Risk Management for Information Technology Systems suggests a further refinement into nine steps. GAMP 4, Appendix M3 describes a process for performing Risk Assessments of a computerized system to ensure design, specification, and test efforts are appropriately focused. This Appendix describes how a combined approach may be adopted for IT Infrastructures.

2 Risk Analysis

The purpose of risk analysis is to provide clarity of the boundaries of the infrastructure under analysis, and review the history of threats (hazards) and vulnerabilities in the light of its potential impact on the company's mission, which for GxP regulated companies includes considerations of public health.

Input to the process should include:

  • platform specifications (hardware and software)
  • architecture/topology diagrams
  • applied or planned security policies and requirements
  • requirements from application (system/data) owners
  • levels of staff training and experience
  • history of attacks, weaknesses, failures, flaws
  • any audit or self assessment comments
  • current or planned controls that may prevent, detect, or otherwise mitigate harm before irreparable damage occurs

Output from the analysis process would include:

  • identification of the infrastructure objects scoped by the process
  • the hazards threatening the infrastructure's obligation to meet critical requirements
  • the vulnerabilities that may warrant further consideration
  • a list of critical controls

The next step is to determine the likelihood that a given harm occurs, the magnitude of the impact of the harm, and the effect of any identified mitigation factors, e.g., early detection.

Each of the factors mentioned above should be rated in relation to each other as high, medium, or low in a two stage process:

Figure A2.1: GAMP Risk Assessment, Stage 1 — Output from this step is a classification of each hazard in one of three levels: one, two, or three.

Figure A2.2: GAMP Risk Assessment, Stage 2 — The next step is to evaluate the effect of mitigation factors, e.g., probability of detection before any harm to critical aspects occurs. Output from this stage is the risk priority.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

GAMP 兩階段風險評估框架

Stage 1（風險水平）：

將「發生可能性（Likelihood）」× 「衝擊程度（Impact）」組合，產出 Level 1/2/3 的風險分類。

Stage 2（風險優先級）：

在 Stage 1 結果的基礎上，加入「偵測概率（Probability of Detection）」——若傷害很早就能被偵測到，風險優先級可以降低；若難以偵測，優先級提升。

風險評估邏輯（概念式）

Stage 1:
  Likelihood (高/中/低) × Impact (高/中/低)
  → Risk Level: 1 (低) / 2 (中) / 3 (高)

Stage 2:
  Risk Level + Detection Probability (高/中/低)
  → Risk Priority: 高優先 / 中優先 / 低優先

風險優先級高 → 需要更嚴格的 Control 措施
風險優先級低 → 可接受現有 Control 或監控即可

比喻：工廠火災風險

Stage 1：工廠附近有化學品（高衝擊）× 員工操作不熟練（中可能性）→ Risk Level 2
Stage 2：是否有火災感測器（Detection）？若有完善感測器 → 優先級下降；若感測器老舊 → 優先級維持高

IT 安全的邏輯相同：防火牆設定錯誤（高衝擊），加上是否有日誌監控（Detection）來決定最終優先級。

重點提示：主觀性與人員素質

指南明確承認：「輸入此步驟的資料大多是主觀的，因為通常缺乏定量數據支撐評估。」這就是為什麼參與風險評估的人員素質至關重要——必須是有均衡技術背景和經驗的人員，而非單純的 IT 工程師或單純的 QA。

§3 Risk Evaluation & Table A2.1 — Example Risk Assessment

原文內容 Original Text

3 Risk Evaluation

Once a risk is prioritized, it should be evaluated to determine whether it is acceptable to the company under the influence of all identified factors. If this is not the case, some degree of rework is required to improve the situation, and the Risk Assessment process should be repeated for the change.

The results of the assessment, along with the assumptions made, should be documented.

Note that assessing risks typically is an iterative process, repeated as activities progress and as more information becomes available.

4 Application of the GAMP Risk Assessment Approach to the Infrastructure

Table A2.1 presents some proposals for considering the scope of typical scenarios/events and shows a broad spectrum of infrastructure components directly related to GxP or business critical aspects.

Table A2.1: Example of Infrastructure Risk Assessment
Hazard Risk Scenario Impact Likelihood of Occurrence Probability of Detection Risk Priority Controls
Incorrect physical connection No function or malfunction High Med High Low Network Diagrams; IQ
Failure of component, e.g., network interface card Performance degradation or loss of connection High Low High Low Defined Problem Management process; Defined alarm logs
Access security compromised Unauthorized modifications of data/records, potential access to other (GxP) network areas High Med Low High Security procedures; IQ/OQ; Periodic Review
Anti-virus definitions not maintained Lack of availability; Unauthorized modifications; Breach of confidentiality High Med High Med Security procedures; Periodic Review
Firewall incorrectly configured Corruption of GxP records; Lack of availability; Unauthorized modifications; Breach of confidentiality High Low Low High Specifications maintained for firewall configuration; IQ/OQ; Periodic Review
Storage capacity limit Records/data not stored. Applications may halt. High Med High Med Performance monitoring routines
Insufficient network bandwidth/speed Applications run slowly Med Med High Low Performance monitoring routines
Network diagrams not maintained Unable to rebuild network in event of a disaster High Med Low High Availability of diagrams; Change control process; Configuration Management; Periodic Review
Installation of unauthorized software Interference with operation of existing software High High Low High Security Procedures; Periodic Review
Inaccurate or missing configuration records Inability to restore configuration in case of disaster High Low High Low Configuration Management process; Periodic Review

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

重點提示：風險評估是迭代的

指南明確說「風險評估通常是反覆進行的過程」——這不是一次性活動。每當：

  • 發現新漏洞或威脅
  • 系統發生重大變更
  • 稽查後有新發現

風險評估就應重新執行。這與 ICH Q9 的風險管理原則完全一致。

表格解讀：三個高風險案例

1. 存取安全遭破壞（Access security compromised）
高衝擊 + 中可能性，但偵測概率低 → 風險優先級高。這正是為什麼 GxP 系統需要完整的 audit trail——讓偵測概率提升。

2. 防火牆設定錯誤（Firewall misconfigured）
高衝擊 + 偵測困難 → 高優先。控制手段：維護正式的 firewall spec + IQ/OQ + Periodic Review。

3. 安裝未授權軟體（Unauthorized software）
高衝擊 + 高可能性 + 低偵測 → 高優先。這是最常見的 IT 風險之一，控制手段需要 Security Procedures + 定期審查。

比喻：防火牆就是工廠的大門

防火牆設定錯誤，就像工廠大門沒鎖好——外人可以進入（breach of confidentiality），也可以偷改生產紀錄（unauthorized modifications）。偵測困難（誰進去誰不知道）→ 風險優先級自然高。

解決方案：門要有設計規格（Spec）、安裝後要驗收（IQ/OQ）、定期檢查（Periodic Review）。

練習思考

  1. 在 Table A2.1 中，「存儲容量上限」的風險優先級為「中」，但如果是 GxP 批次紀錄系統，您認為衝擊應評為多高？
  2. 「未授權軟體安裝」的控制措施是 Security Procedures + Periodic Review，您的組織多久進行一次這類審查？
Appendix 3 — Qualification Deliverables 資格確認交付物

原文內容 Original Text

This Appendix provides guidance on specifying life cycle qualification deliverables and deciding which organizational units are involved in preparation, review, and approval. Companies should determine actual involvement required commensurate with the assessed risks. Traceability between requirements, specifications, and qualification should be maintained, e.g., through the use of traceability matrices.

For Table A3.1, the following abbreviations apply:

  • PO — Platform Owner or Administrator
  • SME — Subject Matter Expert / IT Quality and Compliance
  • QA — Independent QA
Table A3.1: Qualification Deliverables
Elements / Platforms Clients Servers Networks Hardware/Peripherals
Qualification Plan PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA
Requirements PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA
Design Specifications PO, SME PO, SME PO, SME, QA 1 PO, SME
Risk Assessment PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA
Type 2 IQ PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA
Instance 3 IQ SME SME SME SME
Type OQ PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA
Instance OQ SME SME SME SME
Type Qualification Report PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA PO, SME, QA
Instance Qualification Report SME (via remote management) PO, SME PO, SME PO, SME

1 Role of QA in ensuring that up-to-date Network Topology Diagrams are available should be determined.
2 Type: the generic specifications and derived documents relating to building blocks (standard configurations). Type qualification includes all the above except Instance IQ and OQ.
3 Instance: the individual documents specifying qualification details and capturing results for instances of building blocks. Instance qualification typically includes Instance IQ and OQ only, referring to the associated building block type documentation.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

Type vs. Instance：最重要的概念

Type（類型）資格確認：針對「標準建構模組（Building Block）」的通用規格。例如：「Windows Server 2022 Standard Configuration」的 IQ/OQ——只做一次，適用於所有相同標準配置的伺服器。

Instance（實例）資格確認：針對每一台實際部署的伺服器個別執行。僅需做 Instance IQ 和 OQ，並引用 Type 文件作為依據。

這個分層架構的好處：不必為每台伺服器重新做完整資格確認，大大提升效率。

比喻：房屋建設

Type 資格確認 = 建築師為「標準戶型」審核並核准設計圖（只做一次）
Instance 資格確認 = 工地監工對每棟實際蓋出來的房子做竣工驗收（每棟都要做，但不需要重新審核設計圖）

設計圖（Type 文件）已通過 QA 批准；每棟房子的施工記錄（Instance 文件）只需 SME 確認，引用設計圖即可。

重點提示：QA 在 Instance 層級不需出現

注意表格中的規律：

  • Type 層級：所有交付物都需要 PO + SME + QA 三方參與
  • Instance 層級（IQ/OQ/Report）：只需 SME（或 SME + PO），不需要 QA

這是效率設計——標準已由 QA 在 Type 層審批，Instance 的個別執行授權 SME 負責，降低 QA 的行政負擔。

實務應用：CDMO 新設伺服器

情境：您的 CDMO 新增第 5 台 LIMS 伺服器，與前 4 台規格相同。

  • Type IQ/OQ（第 1 台時完成）：PO + SME + QA 參與 — 已有文件
  • 第 5 台 Instance IQ/OQ：SME 執行，引用 Type 文件，不需要 QA 重新審批
  • Instance Qualification Report：SME + PO 簽署即可

效率提升顯著——規模擴張時的合規負擔大幅降低。

練習思考

  1. 如果一台伺服器的配置與 Type 文件有小差異（例如記憶體規格不同），仍可使用 Instance 流程嗎？
  2. Table A3.1 中，Client（桌電）的 Instance Qualification Report 由「SME via remote management」負責——這在實務上如何實現？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • 附錄 1：8 個關鍵角色各有邊界——Platform Owner 管底層平台，Application Owner 管業務系統，IT Q&C 是技術橋樑，Independent QA 有最終判斷權。無論 IT 委外與否，QA 責任永遠留在受監管公司。
  • 附錄 2：GAMP 兩階段風險評估——Stage 1（可能性 × 衝擊 → 風險等級），Stage 2（加入偵測概率 → 風險優先級）。風險評估是迭代過程，必須隨系統生命週期持續更新。
  • 附錄 3：Type（標準模組）vs. Instance（個別部署）的資格確認分層——Type 層需要 PO + SME + QA 三方，Instance 層只需 SME（+ PO），有效降低規模擴張時的合規負擔。追溯性矩陣確保需求→規格→確認的完整鏈結。
  • 跨附錄主題：IT 基礎架構的合規是「風險驅動」的——從角色分工、風險評估到資格確認的參與深度，都應與所評估的 GxP 風險相稱。
5

Chapter 5: Appendices 4–5: SOPs & Periodic Reviews

附錄4-5：標準作業程序清單與定期審查 | App 4-5

ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guide: IT Infrastructure Control and Compliance | Appendix 4 (p68–p73)

本章學習目標

  • 理解為何 IT 基礎設施需要正式的 SOP 框架，而不只是技術設定文件
  • 掌握 Table A4.1 矩陣的三欄結構：流程領域 → SOP 需求 → 典型交付文件
  • 辨別哪些 SOP 類別最常出現於 FDA 483 觀察項目，特別是 CDMO 環境
  • 連結資料管理、安全管控與 21 CFR Part 11 合規性要求
概述 — Appendix 4 Purpose

原文內容 Original Text

This Appendix provides guidelines on addressing the individual aspects that may need to be controlled by SOPs and the quality records that should be produced. Detailed selection and organization of documents depends on the circumstances for each company: size, complexity, geographic layout, impact on critical aspects, etc.

"Detailed selection and organization of documents depends on the circumstances for each company: size, complexity, geographic layout, impact on critical aspects, etc."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Standard Operating Procedure / 標準作業程序 (SOP): 正式書面化、經核准的程序文件，描述如何一致且可重複地執行特定作業。在 GMP 環境下，SOP 不只是「最佳做法建議」——它是法規稽核的直接檢視對象。

Quality Records / 品質記錄: 作業執行後產生的客觀證據。SOP 告訴你「怎麼做」，records 則證明「真的照著做了」。兩者缺一不可。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像 SOP 是餐廳的食譜手冊，quality records 則是每次出菜前的品管核對單。光有食譜不夠——每次出餐都需要留下記錄，才能在客訴時追溯責任。IT 基礎設施的 SOP 邏輯完全相同：稽核員來訪時，他們要看的不只是文件，更要看執行記錄。

重點提示 Key Note

附錄強調文件選擇取決於公司規模、複雜度、地理分布、對關鍵面向的影響等因素。這意味著 SOP 不是「一套通用版本套用所有公司」——CDMO 必須根據自身的客戶多樣性、產品複雜度以及驗證狀態，客製化其 IT SOP 架構。

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析：矩陣三欄結構

Table A4.1 採用三欄格式，反映 GMP 文件管理的核心邏輯：

  • 欄一 Area or Aspect（領域）：定義需要管控的功能區域（例如安全管理、資料備份）
  • 欄二 Processes Requiring SOPs（需要 SOP 的流程）：列出該領域下每項需要書面程序的具體作業
  • 欄三 Typical Deliverable Documentation（典型交付文件）：作業執行後產生的品質記錄，供稽核追溯

這個三欄結構的精髓：光有「做了」還不夠，必須有文件證明「怎麼做」（SOP）和「做了什麼」（記錄）。

重點提示：為何 IT 需要 SOP — 不只是驗證

許多製藥公司誤以為 IT SOP 只在系統「驗證」期間有用。這是危險的誤解。IT 基礎設施 SOP 的功能包括：

  • 法規合規的持續性：FDA 21 CFR Part 11、EU Annex 11 要求電子記錄系統在整個生命週期均受管控，不只是上線時
  • 人員流動的風險緩解：SOP 讓新進 IT 人員能按一致方式操作，不依賴個人記憶
  • 偏差調查的依據：當系統異常或資料遺失時，SOP + 記錄是判斷責任歸屬的唯一客觀標準
  • 客戶稽核的信心建立：CDMO 的製藥客戶在審計時，通常會要求查看 IT SOP 清單及執行記錄

比喻說明：SOP 矩陣如同醫院的感染管控計畫

醫院的感染管控計畫不只規範「手術室消毒」這一個動作。它涵蓋進出管控、人員訓練、設備維護、廢棄物處理、緊急應變——每一個環節都有對應的 SOP 和記錄要求。IT 基礎設施的 SOP 架構邏輯完全相同：從「誰可以進機房」到「備份失敗時如何處理偏差」，全部都需要正式化。

安全管控 SOP：21 CFR Part 11 的直接連結

矩陣中「Logical Security」（邏輯安全）部分要求的 SOP，直接對應 FDA 21 CFR Part 11 的條文要求：

  • User account management（使用者帳號管理）：對應 §11.10(d) — 限制系統存取僅限授權人員
  • Password management（密碼管理）：對應 §11.300 — 確保電子簽名的唯一性與不可否認性
  • Digital signature certificate management（數位簽章憑證管理）：對應 §11.100 — 電子簽名的身分認證要求
  • Logs of creation, deletion, transfers（帳號創建/刪除/職責移轉記錄）：對應 §11.10(e) — 完整的稽核軌跡

重點：唯一使用者帳號 + 稽核軌跡 = 21 CFR Part 11 合規的最基本要求。任何多人共用帳號或無法追溯的存取行為，都是立即的 483 觀察項目。

資料管理 SOP：備份不等於驗證

許多公司有執行備份，但忽略了矩陣要求「Restoration testing as part of disaster recovery testing」（還原測試）。這是 FDA 483 觀察的常見痛點：

  • 備份計劃存在 ✓
  • 每日執行備份 ✓
  • 備份媒體離站存放 ✓
  • 定期驗證備份可成功還原 ✗ ← 最常被忽略

稽核員會問：「你上次成功執行 restore test 是什麼時候？有記錄嗎？」沒有還原測試紀錄等同於備份系統的有效性無法被證明。

CDMO 視角：FDA 483 高風險 SOP 類別排名

高風險（最常被引用）：
  1. Logical Security — 使用者帳號/密碼/稽核軌跡
  2. Data Backup & Restore — 缺少還原測試記錄
  3. Change Management — 未經變更管制的 IT 變更
  4. Training — IT 人員訓練記錄不完整

中風險（常見但可快速補救）：
  5. Configuration Management — 組態文件過時
  6. Quality Management — 未定期進行 IT 內部稽核
  7. Continuity Management — 災難復原計畫未定期測試

低風險（結構性問題，較少單獨被引用）：
  8. Job Scheduling — 批次作業偏差報告機制
  9. Networks — 第三方網路連接文件

實務應用：CDMO 的 SOP 優先建置順序

對於正在建立或重整 IT SOP 架構的 CDMO，建議依以下優先順序建置：

  1. 第一優先（法規直接要求）：Logical Security SOP 套件、Change Management SOP、Data Backup & Restore SOP（含還原測試）
  2. 第二優先（稽核高頻查詢）：User Access Review 程序、Training Effectiveness Assessment、Configuration Management
  3. 第三優先（營運韌性）：Disaster Recovery Plan（含年度演練）、Capacity Management、Incident Management

不需要一次把所有 SOP 完美建立——先建立高風險的核心文件，其餘依照風險評估逐步補齊。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的公司目前是否有針對 IT 使用者帳號的「離職員工帳號停用」SOP？離職後帳號最晚在幾小時內必須停用？
  2. 上次你們的 IT 團隊執行備份還原測試（Restoration Testing）是什麼時候？測試結果有沒有正式記錄？
  3. 如果 FDA 稽核員要求查看過去 12 個月的 IT Change Control Records，你能在 30 分鐘內提交嗎？
深度解析：關鍵 SOP 類別

Security SOP Requirements — 安全 SOP 詳解

The Logical security category contains the most extensive SOP requirements, covering:

  • User account management — creation, modification, deletion
  • Password management — functionality rules, changes, event reporting
  • Digital signature certificate management
  • Access rights maintenance
  • Management of administrator accounts
  • Management of emergency access

Corresponding deliverables include logs of creation, deletion, transfers of responsibilities, and logs of password renewals, deletions, suspensions.

"Management of emergency access" — This acknowledges that break-glass access scenarios must themselves be controlled and documented, not left as informal workarounds.

Data Management SOP Requirements

The Data Backup and Restore SOP requirements are notably comprehensive:

  • Backup scheduling, logging, recorded data verification
  • Problem detection and deviation reporting
  • Media labeling and storage (on-site, off-site)
  • Risk analysis
  • Restore process (including authorization to restore)
  • Media management
  • Restoration testing (as part of disaster recovery testing)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

「Emergency Access Management」的 GMP 意涵

矩陣特別點名「Management of emergency access」（緊急存取管理）需要 SOP，這是業界常見的合規漏洞。當系統緊急異常時，IT 人員可能使用共用的 emergency/root 帳號繞過正常的存取管制。

合規要求：

  • 緊急存取帳號必須有 SOP 規範啟用條件、授權層級
  • 每次使用必須記錄，事後補簽授權並進行審查
  • 使用後必須重設密碼，防止憑證外洩
