「緊急狀況」不能成為跳過管控的藉口——恰恰相反，緊急狀況時的紀律性更是法規關注的重點。

比喻說明：備份如同保險，還原測試才是理賠演練

買了保險但從未確認保單內容是否有效——這就是「有備份但無還原測試」的情況。定期執行 Restoration Testing 等同於每年讓保險公司確認你的理賠條件仍然符合。沒有還原測試記錄，等於你的「保險」可能是一張空頭支票。

「Authorization to Restore」的重要性

矩陣要求 Restore 流程必須包含「authorization to restore」——這不只是技術操作，而是品質決策。在受 GxP 管控的環境中，從備份還原資料可能影響：

  • 正在進行中的批次記錄完整性
  • 電子批次記錄 (eBR) 的資料一致性
  • 稽核軌跡的連續性

因此，「誰有權授權執行還原」必須在 SOP 中明確定義，不能由 IT 人員自行決定。

Change Management SOP 的三個必要元素

矩陣要求 Change Management 包含：變更本身的 SOP + Risk Assessment + Management approval/rejection。這三者缺一不可：

  • 變更 SOP：定義如何提出、評估、實施變更
  • Risk Assessment（風險評估）：變更對 GxP 系統的潛在影響評估，決定是否需要再驗證
  • Management approval/rejection（管理層核准）：確保變更決定有適當的組織授權，不能只由 IT 自行拍板

未經核准的 IT 變更（即使是「小」更新，如 patch 安裝）是 FDA 483 觀察中最常見的問題之一。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的公司的 IT Change Management SOP 是否明確規定，哪些類型的變更需要 QA 審查？「緊急變更」的審批流程是什麼？
  2. 如果一名 IT 人員今天離職，你能在 24 小時內確認所有相關系統的帳號已被停用嗎？這個流程是否有 SOP 支持？
品質管理與持續性管理 — Quality & Continuity Management SOPs

原文內容 Original Text

QUALITY MANAGEMENT

QA/IT Quality and Compliance requires SOPs covering:

  • Compliance with standards and SOPs
  • Implementation of corrective actions
  • Process improvement participation
  • Service Level Agreement performance monitoring

Deliverables: IT Operational Standards, Internal audit schedule, Audit reports, Process Evaluations, Performance reports.

Risk Management requires:

  • Use of Risk Model

Deliverables: Risk Assessment results, Mitigation steps.

CONTINUITY MANAGEMENT

Disaster recovery and contingency planning requires:

  • Continuance of service provision in event of catastrophes

Deliverables: Disaster Recovery Plan (as part of business continuity planning), Disaster Recovery Test Reports.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

QA 與 IT 的交界：IT Quality and Compliance

「QA/IT Quality and Compliance」這個 SOP 類別要求 IT 部門本身有自我審計機制。這不只是 QA 部門的責任——IT 必須：

  • 維護自己的 Internal audit schedule（IT 自查排程）
  • 追蹤 corrective actions（矯正措施）的完成狀態
  • 定期監控 SLA performance（服務水準協議履行情況）

這意味著 IT 部門不能只是被動回應稽核發現——必須主動建立品質管理循環。

災難復原計畫：不是一份文件，是一個演練程序

矩陣要求的不只是 Disaster Recovery Plan（計畫文件），更要有 Disaster Recovery Test Reports（測試報告）。這強調 DRP 必須被定期演練並留有記錄。

FDA 稽核員的典型問題：

  • 「你們的 DRP 最後一次演練是什麼時候？」
  • 「演練結果是否有識別出差距？差距如何補救？」
  • 「演練覆蓋了哪些關鍵 GxP 系統？」

一份從未被測試的 DRP，在稽核員眼中幾乎等同於沒有 DRP。

實務應用：SLA 監控與 CDMO 客戶合約

對 CDMO 而言，SLA 監控 SOP 有特殊的商業意義。當 CDMO 承接大型製藥客戶的 IT 服務時（例如提供 eBR 系統存取、資料傳輸介面），客戶合約中通常包含系統可用性的 SLA 條款（例如 99.5% uptime）。

SLA 監控 SOP 幫助 CDMO：

  • 客觀記錄系統可用性數據，保護自身免受不合理的違約索賠
  • 主動識別系統效能下滑趨勢，在客戶投訴前先行處理
  • 在客戶品質協議 (Quality Agreement) 稽核時提供具體的履約證明

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的 CDMO 是否有正式的 IT Internal Audit 程序？上次 IT 自查是什麼時候？發現的問題有沒有對應的 CAPA 記錄？
  2. 你們的 Disaster Recovery Plan 是否包含 GxP 關鍵系統（例如 LIMS、EBR、環境監控系統）的復原優先順序？復原目標時間 (RTO) 和復原點目標 (RPO) 分別是多少？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • SOP 不只是驗證文件：IT 基礎設施 SOP 涵蓋整個系統生命週期——從安裝資格確認到停役封存，是持續合規的核心工具，而非一次性的驗證作業。
  • 三欄矩陣邏輯：領域（Area）→ 需要 SOP 的流程（Processes）→ 交付文件（Deliverables）三者構成完整的「說到做到、做了留證」閉環。
  • Logical Security = 21 CFR Part 11 的實踐基礎：唯一帳號、密碼管理、緊急存取管制和完整稽核軌跡，是電子記錄合規性的最低標準，缺一不可。
  • 備份驗證的關鍵差距：「有備份計畫」≠「備份有效」——Restoration Testing 是最常被忽略、也最常被稽核員查核的 IT SOP 要項。
  • CDMO 優先行動項目：Logical Security SOP、Change Management SOP、Data Backup & Restore SOP（含還原測試記錄）是 FDA 483 觀察中最高頻的三個類別，應優先建立並定期審查。
ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guide: IT Infrastructure Control and Compliance | Appendix 5 (p74–p83)

本章學習目標

  • 理解 IT 基礎設施定期審查（Periodic Review）的目的與法規要求
  • 掌握資安管理（Security Management）中與 21 CFR Part 11 最相關的查核項目：使用者帳號、密碼規則、存取稽核軌跡
  • 區分備份（Backup）與復原測試（Restoration Testing）的法規要求差異，說明為何兩者缺一不可
  • 解讀災難復原（Disaster Recovery）條款「access to archives commensurate with recovery lag times」的實務含義
  • 能為 CDMO 設計年度 IT 基礎設施定期審查計畫架構
A5.1 Periodic Review — Purpose and Scope | 定期審查的目的與範圍

原文內容 Original Text

For the Infrastructure, a Periodic Review should establish that procedures meeting current applicable GxP regulatory requirements are approved and in use. The review also should establish that qualification and operational records and review reports are complete, current, and accurate.

Companies may choose, for business reasons, to address non-GxP elements of the infrastructure during Periodic Reviews.

Companies should define and agree in advance the topics to cover during specific Periodic Reviews, taking into account possible hazards and risks. The following example checklist may be used when drawing up such a list of topics. Depending on circumstances, companies should select which aspects to include since the complete list will not always be required or appropriate.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Periodic Review（定期審查）：已驗證/確效系統在上線後，須定期確認其持續維持於受控狀態的正式審查活動。頻率通常為每年一次，但可依風險調整。

兩大確認目標：

  • SOP 符合現行 GxP 法規，且已核准並實際執行中
  • 確效記錄、操作記錄與審查報告均完整、最新、正確

比喻說明 Analogy

定期審查就像汽車的年度安全檢驗（車輛大保養）。買車時做過驗收（IQ/OQ），但車子每天運行、零件老化、法規更新——不定期複查，無法確保它仍符合上路標準。IT 基礎設施同理：確效只是起點，持續維持受控才是目標。

重點提示 Key Notes

審查範圍須事先定義並取得共識——不是把整份 Table A5.1 全部做完。依據風險評估選取適用項目，並以書面記錄選項的理由。這份清單是工具箱，不是硬性要求全部執行的義務清單。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若您的 CDMO 新導入一套雲端 ERP 系統，Periodic Review 應在上線後多久開始進行？依據什麼決定？
  2. 非 GxP 項目（如員工出勤系統）是否需要列入 IT 定期審查？從商業風險角度說明您的判斷。
A5.2 IT Management and Organization | IT 管理與組織

原文內容 Original Text

IT Management and Organization

Roles and Responsibilities

  • Are management roles and responsibilities defined (e.g., job description)?
  • Are quality roles and responsibilities defined (e.g., job description)?
  • Are technical and support roles and responsibilities defined (e.g., job description)?
  • Is the organization documented (e.g., organization charts)?

Capability and Competency

  • Are training plans in place?
  • Have personnel received training in regulatory expectations (where appropriate)?
  • Are training records in place to demonstrate that training has been delivered (for both employed and contracted staff)?
  • Do training records document:
    • Description of Training
    • Date of Training
    • Instructor
    • Evidence of Attendance
  • Do training records demonstrate that the attendee understood the training?
  • Is current documentation in place detailing personnel qualifications, education and experience (i.e., resume or CV)?

Internal Organization Interfaces

  • Are interfaces between infrastructure organizations defined (e.g., international sites)?
  • Are service agreements or procedures in place between internal infrastructure organizations?
  • Are requirements of the business defined?
  • Are system and data owners defined?

External Support Organizations

  • Are contracts and/or service agreements/escrow agreements in place for all external service/support organizations?
  • Have external service/support organizations been assessed (e.g., audited) against contract requirements?
  • Is service performance monitored against defined service levels?
  • Have service providers been trained in your company's procedures where relevant?
  • Have service providers been trained in your company's security policy?
  • Are there controls in place to ensure that only authorized personnel from the service organization have access to your network and files?
  • Is there a mechanism in place to ensure that applicable changes at the external organization will be assessed for any impact on your organization (and vice versa)?
  • Are your company's records segregated from those of the service provider's other clients?

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

System Owner / Data Owner（系統擁有者／資料擁有者）：這兩個角色在 GxP 環境中具有明確法律責任。System Owner 負責確效狀態的維持；Data Owner 對資料的完整性與保留負最終責任。在 CDMO 中，通常是不同部門主管擔任。

Escrow Agreement（軟體託管協議）：供應商若倒閉，客戶仍可取得原始碼繼續維護系統。這是對外部 IT 服務供應商的重要風險控管。

重點提示 Key Notes

訓練記錄的完整性是 FDA 查廠最常檢視的文件之一。特別注意：記錄「上課了」還不夠——必須能證明受訓者理解了內容（如測驗成績、主管確認簽名）。約聘人員（contracted staff）也同樣適用此要求，不能因為是外包就略過。

比喻說明 Analogy

要求外部服務商接受您公司的安全政策訓練，就像要求進廠施工商簽署保密協議並上工安課程。他們的錯誤可能造成您的合規問題——責任在您，所以控制措施也必須由您主導。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 場景：您的工廠委外一家 IT 廠商維護 LIMS（實驗室資訊管理系統）。定期審查時需確認：（1）是否有服務合約及 SLA；（2）廠商是否做過 GxP 相關訓練；（3）廠商的網路存取是否有授權記錄；（4）您的批次記錄資料是否與廠商其他客戶的資料隔離存放。

A5.3 Quality Systems | 品質系統

原文內容 Original Text

Quality Systems

General

  • Are projects managed in accordance with life cycle project management systems?
  • Is there an overview document (e.g., Quality Manual) describing the quality management system?
  • Is the quality management system, periodically reviewed for its effectiveness?
  • Are quality metrics in place to enable measurement of quality system performance?
  • Are documentation and records management processes, systems and/or procedures in place?

Are infrastructure qualification standards in place including:

  • Planning
  • Specification and Design
  • Risk Assessment and Qualification Test Planning
  • Procurement, Installation, and IQ
  • OQ and Acceptance
  • Reporting and Handover

Are these standards being followed?

Does the QMS address infrastructure operation and maintenance processes e.g.:

  • Change Management
  • Configuration Management
  • Security Management
  • Server Management
  • Client Management
  • Network Management
  • Problem Management
  • Help Desk
  • Backup, Restore, and Archiving
  • Disaster Recovery
  • Performance Monitoring
  • Supplier Management
  • Retirement

Regulatory

  • Has impact of applicable regulatory inspection findings been considered and addressed?
  • Has impact of changes in regulatory requirements, industry best practice, and introduction of other regulations (e.g., financial regulations) been considered and addressed?

Tools and Infrastructure Applications

  • Are tools and infrastructure applications compliant with regulatory and company requirements, e.g., SOP systems, Configuration Management, change control, access authorization, etc?
  • Are the risks of deploying infrastructure tools, e.g., virus protection, backup, performance monitoring, assessed?
  • Are tools verified to ensure they meet company standards and deliver the required functionality without unexpected side effects?
  • Is an inventory of tools maintained, such as:
    • Communication Protocols
    • Performance Monitoring Software
    • Virus Protection
    • Backup and Restoration
    • Software Deployment Tools

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

QMS（Quality Management System，品質管理系統）涵蓋 IT 運維：許多 CDMO 的 QMS 只覆蓋製程和產品，忽略了 IT 基礎設施本身也需要 QMS 管理。這份清單明確指出：變更管理、設定管理、備份、災難復原等，都必須有對應的 SOP 並納入 QMS。

Qualification Standards（確效標準）：公司必須有內部的 IT 確效標準文件，涵蓋從規劃到移交的完整生命週期——這不只是 GAMP 建議，而是 FDA 查廠時會要求出示的文件。

重點提示 Key Notes

「Regulatory」子項要求審查時主動考量最新法規查察發現（inspection findings）的影響。這意味著您必須追蹤 FDA Warning Letters、483 觀察項目及 EMA 查廠報告，並評估是否影響自身系統。這是法規合規的主動義務，不能等到被查才反應。

比喻說明 Analogy

IT 工具清單（virus protection、backup、performance monitoring）就像無菌充填工廠的設備清冊（equipment inventory）。每個工具都需要確認它符合公司標準、功能正常、沒有不預期的副作用——就像設備需要校正（calibration）一樣。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的 CDMO 使用防毒軟體掃描 LIMS 伺服器。這個防毒軟體本身需要做什麼形式的確效或驗證？理由為何？
  2. 若 FDA 在同業查廠時發現 audit trail 相關 483 觀察項目，您的公司應如何回應？納入哪個定期審查流程？
A5.4 Qualification Planning, Specification and Design | 確效規劃、規格與設計

原文內容 Original Text

Qualification Planning

Are Qualification Plans produced in advance, defining responsibilities, and required activities, procedures, deliverables, timelines, reviews and approvals, constraints, training requirements, critical data being stored?

Are Qualification Plans based upon initial Risk Assessments?

Specification and Design — Hardware

  • Are inventories of Hardware components in place?
  • Are specifications, diagrams or other documentation in place to describe the Site Local Area Network including:
    • Network layout of the site
    • For each area or building, the location of major network components and cable paths
  • Are documented specifications in place for each platform component enabling accurate replacement in case of failure?

Network Organization

  • Are network segregations, domains, etc., documented (including access controls)?

Software and Configuration

  • Is there an inventory of all applications and data storage areas within the network?

Cable Infrastructure

  • Are (internal or external) standards used to define cable requirements?
  • Are cabling diagrams or specifications in place?
  • Are cables tagged or labeled to aid identification?

Control of External Connections

  • Are connections to WANs defined?
  • Are controls in place to ensure that only authorized users can access the system remotely (e.g., secure ID or callback)?
  • When a remote access link is terminated, is the user automatically logged off the network?

Electrical Supplies

  • Do electrical supplies conform to earthing, loading, filtering and safety standards?
  • Are power conditioning in place (prevention of spikes and brown outs)?
  • Are backup power supplies (e.g., UPS) in place to guard against power loss to critical components?
  • Are UPS loads determined and monitored?
  • Is UPS performance verified?

Redundancy and Fault Tolerance

  • Have redundancy requirements been assessed, e.g., disk mirroring, RAID?
  • Have requirements for automatic standby systems been defined?

Risk Assessment and Qualification Test Planning

  • Is the scope of qualification testing based on documented Risk Assessments, carried out by qualified staff?

Procurement, Installation, and IQ

  • Are suppliers assessed in accordance with documented Risk Assessments?
  • Are platform components subject to installation qualification in accordance with Qualification Plans?
  • Is adequacy of documentation verified?

OQ and Acceptance

  • Are platform components subject to OQ in accordance with Qualification Plans?

Reporting and Handover

  • Is there a summary report, approved by QA, to confirm successful completion of qualification?
  • Does the approved report enable platform owners to demonstrate compliance to auditors and inspectors and provides assurance to application owner(s) that their platforms are in control?

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

IQ（Installation Qualification，安裝確效）：確認 IT 硬體/軟體按規格正確安裝，並留有文件記錄。

OQ（Operational Qualification，操作確效）：在受控條件下，確認系統功能符合預定規格。

UPS（Uninterruptible Power Supply，不斷電系統）：須定期確認其負載容量與效能——僅安裝 UPS 不代表它在緊急時能正常運作。

重點提示 Key Notes

遠端存取控制是 21 CFR Part 11 的核心關切之一。Periodic Review 需確認：遠端連線是否要求強身份認證（secure ID）；連線結束後是否自動登出（避免 session 被盜用）。這在 COVID 後大量遠端維護的環境中尤為重要。

QA 核准的確效報告是轉移系統控制給業主（platform owner）的正式依據，必須能讓審計員直接用來評估合規狀態。

比喻說明 Analogy

RAID 磁碟陣列就像備用引擎的飛機：一顆硬碟故障，系統繼續運行，資料不遺失。但「有 RAID」不等於「安全」——你仍需要備份，因為 RAID 無法防止人為誤刪或勒索病毒。冗餘（redundancy）與備份（backup）是兩個不同層次的保護。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的 CDMO 更換了存放批次記錄的伺服器硬體。這是否需要重新做 IQ？評估的依據為何？
  2. 供應商評估（supplier assessment）在 IT 採購中與 QRM 如何連結？風險高的供應商應有哪些額外控制措施？
A5.5 Change Management and Configuration Management | 變更管理與設定管理

原文內容 Original Text

Change Management

  • Are change control procedures in place to manage changes to hardware, firmware and software, including impact assessment on any application affected by the change?
  • Do change control procedures consider the need for testing to be conducted, based on risk, when hardware or software is added, removed or modified within the infrastructure?
  • Are changes to platform components that support GxP applications qualified?
  • Do change control procedures address the management of emergency changes, patches, or configuration changes?
  • Are responsibilities for change management defined (e.g., SME/QA/User)?
  • Are development, test, and production environments managed in order to ensure that software, hardware and configuration integrity is maintained?
  • Are GxP and non-GxP areas segregated or are GxP level controls applied to both?
  • If GxP and non-GxP items are segregated, is there a documented justification for what is and is not defined as GxP?

Configuration Management

  • Are adequate means defined to protect configuration items from deletion, removal, or unauthorized alteration or use?
  • Are specifications, configuration item lists and other documentation updated following changes to hardware and software?
  • Does the configuration item list enable an accurate restore of critical components in case of break down, by documenting, e.g.:
    • Item name or identifier
    • Serial number
    • Model or hardware type
    • Manufacturer
    • Item location
    • Storage devices
    • Operating system software, including version
    • Layered products, including version
    • Relevant application software, including version and the application (system/data) owner
  • Are controls in place to control access to system documentation?
  • Are retention periods defined for system documentation in line with the site/function record retention schedule?

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Configuration Item List（設定項目清單）：系統所有硬軟體元件的詳細目錄，包含型號、序號、版本、位置及負責人。這是災難復原的基礎文件——沒有它，故障後無從精確重建系統。

GxP vs. 非 GxP 隔離：若選擇隔離，必須有書面理由說明哪些系統屬於 GxP 範圍。若無法清楚區分，則對兩者都適用 GxP 等級的控制——這通常是更安全的選擇。

重點提示 Key Notes

緊急變更（Emergency Changes）是合規高風險區域。許多公司在緊急時繞過正常變更管理流程，事後補文件。Periodic Review 必須確認緊急變更 SOP 存在且有實際遵循記錄——包括緊急執行後的追溯確效或評估。

開發、測試、生產環境的三環境分離是防止未測試的程式碼進入生產系統的關鍵控制措施，同時也是 21 CFR Part 11 對存取控制的隱含要求。

比喻說明 Analogy

設定管理清單就像醫院的病歷系統——每一次變動都必須有記錄，且要讓下一個接手的人能完整重建患者狀態。IT 系統的設定清單功能完全一樣：讓任何工程師在任何時間點，都能精確知道系統的「當下狀態」。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的 LIMS 供應商發布了一個安全性修補程式（security patch）。這是否觸發變更控制？需要哪些測試才能部署到 GxP 生產環境？
  2. 設定管理清單中的「layered products including version」具體指什麼？如果版本資訊過時，可能造成什麼問題？
A5.6 Security Management | 資安管理（21 CFR Part 11 重點區域）

原文內容 Original Text

Security General

  • Are processes, systems and/or procedures in place to address the requirements of the security policy and principles?
  • Are responsibilities for security management defined?
  • Is virus detection software in place and maintained up to date?
  • Are firewalls in place and documented in order to control access to the network?
  • Are controls in place to ensure that unauthorized software and files cannot be loaded into the network?
  • Are procedures in place to detect and investigate potential security violations?

Physical Access Controls

  • Are servers, other critical hardware, backups and archives located in secure areas where access is controlled by key or other security device (e.g., card key)?

Logical Access Controls

  • Are procedures in place to ensure that users are restricted to those parts of the network required to fulfill their defined role?
  • Is logical access based on at least two components and is that component combination unique for each person?
  • Do user accounts automatically time out after a period of inactivity?
  • Are user accounts disabled after a defined period of inactivity?
  • Are users removed from the system when they leave the company or change jobs?
  • Are there Periodic Reviews of obsolete or dormant accounts?
  • Do procedures exist to cover both permanent staff and temporary/contract staff?
  • Are temporary/contract staff accounts set up with an expiry date?
  • Are there documented rules for password management?
  • Are unauthorized access attempts detectable, reported, and investigated?
  • Do procedures exist to manage cards and tokens?
  • Are User access rights documented?

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts — 21 CFR Part 11 連結

這一節的查核項目直接對應 21 CFR Part 11 的核心要求：

  • §11.10(d)：限制系統存取至授權使用者（role-based access）
  • §11.10(g)：使用有效且安全的密碼，且組合對每人唯一
  • §11.10(j)：使用者身份驗證機制的控制
  • §11.300：電子簽名的識別碼與密碼管理

若 FDA 查廠時發現上述任何項目不符，可能直接導致 Warning Letter。

重點提示 Key Notes — 最高風險查核項目

離職/轉調帳號未停用是 FDA 483 觀察項目中最常見的資安問題之一。Periodic Review 必須確認有流程讓 HR 變動觸發 IT 帳號停用，且實際執行有記錄。

Dormant account review（休眠帳號定期審查）：即使員工未離職，長期未使用的帳號也是潛在資安漏洞，必須定期清查並有書面記錄。

約聘人員帳號設定到期日：這是主動控制措施，避免合約到期後帳號仍存在的情況。

比喻說明 Analogy

「未授權存取嘗試須可偵測、回報並調查」就像工廠閘口的徽章讀取系統——每次刷卡失敗都會記錄，保全會定期查看異常。IT 系統的 login failure log 功能完全相同：不是只防止入侵，而是要能發現有人在嘗試入侵。

資安查核重點清單 Security Review Checklist Priority

【高優先順序 — 直接 Part 11 合規】
□ 帳號唯一性：每人獨立帳號，不共用
□ 密碼規則：長度、複雜度、定期更換規定
□ 離職帳號停用流程（HR → IT 通知機制）
□ 未授權存取嘗試記錄與調查程序

【中優先順序 — 資安基礎】
□ 休眠帳號定期審查記錄
□ 約聘人員帳號到期日設定
□ 角色型存取控制（RBAC）文件

【基礎建設】
□ 防毒軟體版本更新記錄
□ 防火牆文件
□ 伺服器實體存取控制（卡鑰）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一位 CDMO 的 QC 分析師轉調到生產部門。從資安合規角度，哪些帳號相關行動必須在多少時間內完成？
  2. 「logical access based on at least two components, unique for each person」——舉出 LIMS 系統中具體滿足此要求的實作方式。
A5.7 Server, Client, and Network Management | 伺服器、用戶端與網路管理

原文內容 Original Text

Server Management — System Time

  • Are dedicated time servers in place to distribute time traceable to a reliable source, e.g., BIPM (Bureau International des Poids et Mesures)?
  • Are procedures in place to ensure setting of system time does not break sequence of any logging, e.g., always adjust ahead and in small, frequent increments?
  • Are winter/summer time settings formally managed, and has impact on time stamped logs been assessed?

Environmental Conditions

  • Are computer rooms and data centers environmentally controlled?

Client Management

  • Is the standard client defined?
  • Are local extensions/configurations to standard clients defined?
  • Are processes in place to manage the deployment of client applications?
  • Are processes in place to audit client configuration?
  • Is client configuration documented?
  • Are processes in place to manage the build of new clients?
  • Are processes in place to manage upgrades to the client?
  • Are processes in place to maintain up to date virus protection?
  • Is the client configuration locked to prevent unauthorized user changes?

Network Management

  • Is the network management process defined in SOPs or SLAs?
  • Are network monitoring tools and equipment tested, calibrated, or qualified as per qualification plan?
  • Have metrics been defined?

Problem Management

  • Are procedures in place for reporting, investigating and documenting network faults?

Service Management / Help Desk

  • Have service start-up and close down processes been defined?
  • Have processes for implementing and communicating service restrictions been defined?
  • Are facilities in place for fault reporting, tracking and trending (e.g., Help Desk)?
  • Are support services defined (e.g., 1st, 2nd, 3rd line support)?
  • Are escalation procedures in place for management of service shortfalls?
  • Are continuity plans in place to address critical service outage?

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

系統時間準確性對 GxP 至關重要：所有電子記錄的時間戳記（timestamp）必須準確且可追溯至 BIPM 等標準時間源。若時間設定不當，可能讓稽核軌跡（audit trail）中的事件順序出錯，無法重建事件時序——這直接違反 21 CFR Part 11 §11.10(e)。

Client Configuration Lock（用戶端設定鎖定）：防止一般使用者自行更改 PC 設定，是確保所有工作站維持一致確效狀態的關鍵控制。

重點提示 Key Notes

日光節約時間（Daylight Saving Time）問題：每年時鐘撥快/撥慢一小時時，系統日誌可能出現重複時間戳記或時間跳躍。這在 GxP 環境中必須有正式的 SOP 處理，確保批次記錄時序完整。部分製藥廠已採用協調世界時（UTC）記錄以規避此問題。

Help Desk 的1st/2nd/3rd line 支援分層不只是 IT 管理最佳實踐，也是合規要求：問題須有記錄、追蹤、趨勢分析，作為持續改善的基礎。

比喻說明 Analogy

時間伺服器就像工廠所有時鐘都同步到的「標準大鐘」。如果每台電腦各自對時、各有誤差，批次記錄中的操作順序就會混亂，就像工廠生產記錄上每台設備的時鐘不一致——無法重建真正發生的順序。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的 CDMO 位於台灣（UTC+8，無日光節約時間）。但美國 FDA 客戶要求電子批次記錄使用 UTC 格式。這對您的 LIMS 時間設定有何影響？
  2. 「network monitoring tools tested, calibrated, or qualified」——這對一般 IT 網管工具有何實際意義？如何在 Periodic Review 中驗證？
A5.8 Backup, Restore and Archiving | 備份、復原與封存（合規核心）

原文內容 Original Text

Backup and Restore

  • Are procedures in place to assess backup requirements against business and regulatory needs?
  • Have backup and restoration procedures been formally tested?
  • Do backup procedures address:
    • Frequency of backups
    • Physical labeling of media
    • Review and retention of backup logs
    • Periodic testing of backups to verify that the backup procedure is functioning
    • On site and off site storage of media. Full backups should be periodically stored off site.
    • Rotation of backup media
    • Type of backup (full versus incremental)
  • Do off-site backup storage considerations include:
    • Location of facility
    • Formal processes and controls over physical access to media both on a schedule and "on request" basis?
    • Storage conditions?
  • Are procedures in place to assess ability to recover to point of failure?
  • Do restoration procedures adequately address the retrieval of single files, multiple files, and complex data backups (e.g., database restore)?
  • Are installed versions of operating systems, communication protocols, applications, etc., archived in order to facilitate backup?

Archive

  • Are decommissioning processes in place?
  • Are processes in place for management of data deletion?
  • Do archive procedures include:
    • Identification of archive media
    • Management of archived media
    • Documentation of records to be archived
    • Retention periods
    • Secure and safe storage of archive media
    • Frequency of archiving
    • Periodic evaluation of archive media
    • Migration following system upgrades
    • Considerations for data conversion, where appropriate
  • Do archive restoration procedures provide the ability to read records from the archive (have available appropriate hardware, software, and instructions)?
  • Do archive restoration procedures address:
    • Authorization to request records from archive
    • Procedure for performing restoration

External Data Management Organizations

  • Are external organizations managing backup and archive facilities subject to appropriate controls including:
    • Service Definition, including responsibilities, documentation requirements, escalation process
    • Contacts
    • Audit
    • Performance Monitoring

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Backup vs. Archive（備份 vs. 封存）的本質差異：

  • 備份（Backup）：短期保護，用於系統故障後快速恢復。備份是臨時性的，媒體會被輪替覆蓋。
  • 封存（Archive）：長期保存，用於監管記錄保留。封存是永久性的（依法規期限），必須確保未來仍可讀取。

兩者有不同的程序、媒體管理、保留期限，不能混為一談。

重點提示 Key Notes — 為何復原測試是法規要求

許多公司做備份，但從未測試過復原（restore）。Periodic Review 明確要求：備份程序和復原程序都必須正式測試，且有記錄。

原因很清楚：備份失敗通常只有在需要還原時才發現。若您無法在批次記錄遺失後成功還原，即使有備份也等於沒有備份——這直接違反 21 CFR 211.68 對電子記錄的要求。

「recover to point of failure」（還原至故障點）：需評估 RPO（Recovery Point Objective，可接受的最大資料損失時間）。

重點提示 Key Notes — 封存讀取能力

系統升級後的資料遷移（migration following system upgrades）是最常被忽略的風險之一。舊格式封存資料在新系統上可能無法直接讀取。您必須：

  • 保留能讀取舊格式的硬體/軟體，或
  • 在系統升級時將封存資料轉換為新格式（須驗證轉換完整性）

這直接關係到 FDA 要求電子記錄在法定保留期限內必須可讀取的義務。

比喻說明 Analogy

備份而不測試復原，就像買了一個保險箱但從未測試過鑰匙能不能打開。緊急時發現鑰匙壞了，保險箱等於沒用。定期「演練還原」（restore drill）是確認保護機制真正有效的唯一方法。

備份合規框架 Backup Compliance Framework

備份頻率設計原則：
  RPO（可接受資料損失）→ 決定備份頻率
  RTO（可接受系統停機時間）→ 決定復原方案

典型製藥 CDMO 備份架構：
  全量備份（Full Backup）：每週一次，異地存放
  增量備份（Incremental）：每日一次，本地 + 異地
  日誌備份（Log Backup）：每小時（資料庫）

Periodic Review 必查：
  □ 最近一次復原測試記錄（含日期、測試人、結果）
  □ 異地存放確認記錄
  □ 備份媒體輪替日誌
  □ 封存媒體定期評估記錄（媒體老化）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的 CDMO 的 LIMS 批次記錄保留要求為 30 年。但 LIMS 供應商預計 10 年後停止支援舊版格式。您在 Periodic Review 中應如何處理此風險？
  2. 描述一個完整的「備份→復原測試」SOP 應包含哪些步驟，以及如何記錄測試結果才能滿足 GxP 要求。
A5.9 Disaster Recovery, Performance Monitoring, Supplier Management, and Retirement

原文內容 Original Text

Disaster Recovery

  • Is the disaster recovery process defined in SOPs or SLAs?
  • Are key staff identified, available at defined notice, and trained in appropriate procedures?
  • Is access to archives ensured commensurate with recovery lag times?

Performance Monitoring

  • Are procedures or automated controls in place to monitor network performance and capacities including:
    • Speed
    • Bandwidth
    • Disk Performance (e.g., fragmentation, thrashing)
    • Address Clashes
  • Are event logs created and maintained in support of service performance monitoring?

Supplier Management

  • Has the supplier management process been defined in SOPs or SLAs?
  • Have critical suppliers been assessed against quality requirements?
  • Have purchasing lead times for critical components been agreed upon or have provisions for consignment stocks been made?
  • Have channels of communication been established?

Retirement

  • Have decommissioning plans been made? Including provisions for:
    • Data/Information Archiving
    • Transfer of Processes and Data

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 災難復原條款深度解析

「access to archives commensurate with recovery lag times」的實務含義：

這句話的意思是：在系統災難發生後，必須能在符合復原目標時間（RTO）的時間內取得所需的封存資料。

實務上，這代表：

  • 若您的 RTO 是 4 小時，封存資料必須能在 4 小時內被取回並可讀取
  • 異地封存媒體的物理運輸時間必須納入 RTO 計算
  • 若使用雲端封存，需確認在網路中斷時的替代取存方案
  • 「on request」基礎的實體媒體取回流程必須有 SLA 定義回應時間

重點提示 Key Notes

災難復原關鍵人員的「availability at defined notice」：不能只列人名，必須定義通知後多少時間內必須到位（如：15 分鐘內電話可聯絡，2 小時內可到現場）。且這些人員必須定期接受 DR 演練訓練，並有訓練記錄。

Consignment stocks（寄售庫存）：對關鍵硬體元件（如特定型號的網路設備、伺服器），若採購前置期（lead time）過長，可與供應商協議維持庫存在供應商倉庫，但視同您的可用庫存。這是降低單點失效風險的採購策略。

實務應用 CDMO Annual IT Periodic Review Program

建議年度 IT 基礎設施定期審查計畫架構：

  • Q1：安全管理審查（帳號審查、密碼政策、存取控制、防毒更新記錄）
  • Q2：備份與復原測試（執行年度 restore drill，審查備份日誌，確認異地存放）
  • Q3：變更管理與設定管理審查（審查全年變更記錄、確認設定清單最新）
  • Q4：供應商管理、災難復原演練、整體 QMS 有效性審查、次年計畫制定

每次審查完成後出具正式報告，由 QA 核准，存入 QMS 系統。

比喻說明 Analogy

系統退役（Retirement）就像工廠設備汰換——不能只是「拔掉插頭」就算完成。必須先確保所有相關資料已轉移或封存，所有使用該系統的流程已移轉，並有正式的停用記錄。就像設備除役需要除役確效報告，IT 系統退役需要退役計畫和執行記錄。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的 CDMO 要淘汰使用了 15 年的 LIMS 系統，換新平台。從 Periodic Review 的角度，退役計畫必須涵蓋哪些最關鍵的項目？
  2. 若災難復原演練（DR drill）失敗——例如備援系統無法在 RTO 內啟動——您應如何在 GxP 框架下記錄、調查和解決此問題？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • Periodic Review 的目的是確認 IT 基礎設施持續維持在受控、合規狀態，涵蓋 SOP 有效性、確效記錄完整性，以及法規變化的應對。
  • 資安管理（Security Management）的 Logical Access Controls 直接對應 21 CFR Part 11 要求，重點查核項目包括：唯一帳號、角色型存取、休眠帳號清查、離職帳號停用、密碼規則、未授權存取嘗試的記錄與調查。
  • 備份（Backup）必須搭配定期的復原測試（Restoration Testing）才算完整合規——「有備份但從未測試還原」在 GxP 環境中等同於沒有備份。
  • 「access to archives commensurate with recovery lag times」要求：封存資料的取回時間必須符合災難復原目標時間（RTO），異地儲存的物理取回時間必須納入評估。
  • 建議 CDMO 以季度為單位規劃年度 IT Periodic Review：Q1 資安、Q2 備份復原測試、Q3 變更設定管理、Q4 供應商與 DR 演練，每次出具 QA 核准報告。
6

Chapter 6: Appendices 6–9: Security, Patches, Outsourcing & Servers

附錄6-9：安全管理、補丁管理、委外與伺服器管理 | App 6-9

ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guide: IT Infrastructure Control and Compliance | App. 6–9 (p84–p105)

本章學習目標

  • 掌握 CIA 三角（機密性／完整性／可用性）在 GxP 資料系統中的實際意涵
  • 識別三種資安補丁緊急程度分類，並說明為何緊急修補仍需形式化變更控制
  • 比較平台升級後四種應用程式測試層級的適用時機與選擇標準
  • 解釋委外合規監督責任不可轉移的原則，及 SLA 必要元素對 CDMO 的啟示
  • 說明伺服器備份策略（全量 + 增量）、異地儲存理由，以及備份測試的合規要求
Appendix 6 — Infrastructure Security (p84–p90)

原文內容 Original Text

1. Introduction

A defined level of infrastructure security is required to meet business purposes and to satisfy external regulations. Lack of security may compromise availability of applications and services, record integrity and confidentiality, reputation with stakeholders, and may lead to unauthorized use of systems that would impact on product quality.

A company should take cultural and practical aspects into consideration when defining the rigor of its approach. Companies may adopt different approaches for specific infrastructure elements, based, e.g., on criticality and risk.

2. Infrastructure Security Management

Infrastructure security management includes all the policies, procedures, requirements, training and audit programs, etc. that a company may define appropriate to safeguard the infrastructure, including information assets.

As a minimum, regulated companies need to satisfy the applicable GxP requirements. Relevant documents include the PIC/S Guide, which builds on ISO/IEC 17799:2000 Information Technology – Code of Practice for Information Security Management. The 21 CFR Part 11 contains security requirements focused on electronic records and signatures. RFC 2196, "Site Security Handbook," is another useful source.

Security controls, in general, are considerably cheaper and more effective if incorporated at the requirements specification and design stages.

2.1 ISO/IEC 17799 — Code of Practice for Information Security Management

Information security is characterized in the standard as the preservation of:

  • Confidentiality: ensuring that information is accessible only to those authorized to have access
  • Integrity: safeguarding the accuracy and completeness of information and processing methods
  • Availability: ensuring that authorized users have access to information and associated assets when required

The ISO/IEC 17799:2000 is a risk-based method for assessing, evaluating, and managing risks. It provides a framework for developing a security program with 10 sections:

  1. Security Policy
  2. Organizational Security
  3. Asset Classification and Control
  4. Personnel Security
  5. Physical and Environmental Security
  6. Communications and Operations Management
  7. Access Control
  8. System Development and Maintenance
  9. Business Continuity Management
  10. Compliance

Not all controls will be relevant to all infrastructures. The use of ISO/IEC 17799 as a guide should be adapted to the circumstances of each organization.

2.2 ISO/IEC 17799 and Regulations

Regulatory guidance recommends consideration of these standards, but does not require organizations to be formally accredited. Companies should define a list of ISO/IEC 17799 issues relevant to their infrastructure and map existing policies against applicable sections, using internal audits to demonstrate control to regulatory authorities.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：CIA 三角 The CIA Triad

Confidentiality（機密性）：資料只有授權人員可存取。GxP 系統中，批次紀錄不得被未授權人員讀取或下載。

Integrity（完整性）：資料必須準確且完整，任何修改都要留下稽核軌跡。這直接對應 21 CFR Part 11 的電子記錄要求。

Availability（可用性）：授權使用者在需要時必須能存取系統。若生產線因 IT 系統停機無法取得批次記錄，即構成可用性失效。

比喻說明 Analogy

把 CIA 三角想像成醫院的病歷管理系統。機密性 = 只有主治醫生能看完整病歷；完整性 = 任何人修改病歷都留記錄；可用性 = 急診時隨時能調出病歷。三者缺一不可，就像無菌製造中的環境控制——少了任何一環，產品安全就有風險。

重點提示 Key Notes

ISO/IEC 17799 是推薦框架，法規不要求正式認證，但稽查時需要能展示「公司已將此框架映射至自身政策並完成內稽」。這是合規證明的基礎，不是選擇題。

「安全控制在需求規格設計階段納入，成本最低、效果最好」——這條原則與 GAMP 的 V-model 一致：後期補救的代價遠高於前期設計。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若 CDMO 的 MES 系統每天凌晨備份視窗期間無法登入，這違反 CIA 三角的哪個面向？該如何設計備援？
  2. 公司不需要取得 ISO/IEC 17799 認證，那稽查員要求什麼文件才能「證明公司在控制中」？

原文內容 Original Text

2.3 Technical versus Procedural Issues

Management should establish an administration obligated to define and monitor an infrastructure security program. Controls include:

  • Administrative controls: policies, standards, procedures, guidelines, security awareness training, incident management
  • Technical controls: access control mechanisms, password and resource management, identification and authentication methods, security devices
  • Physical controls: controlling individual access into facilities, locking systems, removing unnecessary floppy disk or CD-ROM drives, protecting facility perimeter, monitoring for intrusion

2.4 Security Incident Management

An incident management procedure should be established as effective communication channels are essential in the quick identification and mitigation of a specific threat. Seemingly isolated incidents may not receive an appropriate level of attention unless they are centrally reported. For instance, an account being locked due to a forgotten password may become more suspicious if the same event occurs repeatedly.

2.5 Intrusion Detection

Intrusion Detection Systems (IDSs) in the form of hardware or software enhance the security of the perimeter of internal networks. Determined intruders may penetrate firewalls, and attacks do not come only from external sources. By monitoring suspicious activity, alarms can be sounded earlier. A well-maintained pattern database and regular review of IDS summary reports ensure efficacy.

2.6 Vulnerability Management

Vulnerability scanners or adequate manual procedures should be applied to determine weaknesses and gaps in security configurations. Corrective actions include: application of patches, changes to security settings, harnessing the network topology.

A practical approach is to start with a complete inventory of systems, identify a small number of reliable sources of security alerts, assess and prioritize each threat. With numerous new threats identified each day, it is often more appropriate to patch during scheduled maintenance (weekly or monthly) rather than daily.

2.7 Anti-Virus Shield Update

Most anti-virus applications can initiate totally automatic updates, but some companies prefer controlled daily updates. Configuration Management practices are required, recording which updates were applied to which systems, and at what date and time.

Two options for remote/off-site clients: (1) controlled distribution from internal IT — allows testing but inhibits rapid response; (2) automatic updates from anti-virus supplier — poses challenges for Configuration Management. A Risk Assessment comparing untested updates vs. leaving clients unprotected may be warranted.

2.8 Public Key Infrastructure

Where a company needs features such as digital signatures, it may implement a Public Key Infrastructure (PKI), or use PKI services from external organizations. Digital signatures secure authenticity, non-repudiation, integrity, and confidentiality of external messaging. Users need certificates from a trusted third party or the company's own Certification Authority (CA).

2.9 Origin of Software

The origin of all software related to qualified infrastructure platforms should be known. If open source software is used, ensure a reputable supplier supports the product and accepts responsibility for maintaining it. Software from non-reputable or unknown sources should be avoided.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：三層安全控制架構

行政控制（政策/培訓）→ 技術控制（存取權限/認證）→ 實體控制（門禁/設備），三層相互補強。GxP 稽查中，三層都要有對應的文件證據，不能只靠技術工具。

比喻說明 Analogy

IDS（入侵偵測系統）就像無塵室的粒子計數器——防護網（防火牆）擋住大部分威脅，但計數器在背景持續監控，一旦異常立即發警報。計數器本身不阻擋污染，但讓你有時間在污染擴散前採取行動。

重點提示 Key Notes

帳號重複鎖定是資安事件，不是 IT 小問題。單次鎖定可能是忘記密碼，但重複發生可能是暴力破解攻擊。集中通報機制讓孤立事件變成可見的模式——這與 GMP 的品質趨勢分析原理相同。

防毒軟體更新的兩難：受控更新可測試但反應慢；自動更新反應快但 Configuration Management 難追蹤。GxP 系統優先選受控更新，需以風險評估文件化決策理由。

開源軟體不等於免費風險：若軟體來源不明或無供應商維護承諾，在 GxP 環境中等同於使用未驗證的原材料——合規風險極高。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. CDMO 的 LIMS 使用開源資料庫，供應商無正式支援合約。稽查時查到這個狀況，你如何答覆稽查員？
  2. 若要在 GxP 系統上採用自動防毒更新，風險評估應涵蓋哪些考量點？

原文內容 Original Text

3. Upgrades and Patches — Balancing Qualification and Security

Changes to IT Infrastructure platforms require formal change control processes, documentation, and testing. These processes take time, especially where individual application tests are required, and particularly for GxP applications.

Where changes are required to address security vulnerabilities, applying the full change control and testing processes prospectively may present an unacceptable risk to the business in terms of security. However, direct application of any upgrades/patches without change control and testing may compromise the qualified status of the IT Infrastructure and present compliance issues.

First, the scope of the change should be understood (Network Operations, Clients, Servers, Firmware/Hardware, Data Management Software, Operating System, Infrastructure Utility Systems). Second, the urgency of the change should be established.

3.1 Urgency of Security Update

Generally, the urgency of application of a change falls into one of three criticality categories:

  1. Emergency Fix: should be applied as soon as possible, where the security vulnerability presents immediate and real threats to the business
  2. Urgent Update: probable threat, fix should be applied within a specified time scale
  3. Update: no immediate threat, consider including within next scheduled platform upgrade

3.2 Compatibility of Security Updates

Security patches are usually available only for a limited number of product versions; suppliers of interacting software may not provide compatible versions, creating a dilemma for system owners. Where critical security patches cannot be installed, system managers may have to resort to procedural controls or even isolate the system from other systems or from the corporate network.

Further guidance on managing security upgrades and patches is given in Appendix 7.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

三種補丁緊急程度分類表

緊急程度     | 定義              | GxP 要求
-------------|-------------------|---------------------------
Emergency    | 即時、真實威脅    | 事後補做變更控制文件
Fix          |                   | (retroactive change control)
             |                   | 強化事件監控
-------------|-------------------|---------------------------
Urgent       | 可能威脅          | 在指定時間內完成
Update       |                   | 正常變更控制流程
-------------|-------------------|---------------------------
Update       | 無即時威脅        | 納入下次定期升級
             |                   | 完整變更控制與測試

重點提示：緊急補丁仍需變更控制

Emergency Fix 可以「先做後補文件」，但不是「做了就算」。事後補做的變更控制文件必須說明：為何緊急、評估了什麼風險、誰授權、做了什麼事後監控。這是 GxP 系統「qualified status」維護的底線。

CDMO 現場常見錯誤：在 21:00 緊急打了補丁，隔天沒有任何文件記錄，直到稽查才被發現——這是偏差，不是緊急程序。

比喻說明 Analogy

緊急補丁就像醫院的緊急手術——不能等標準排程，但手術後仍要寫完整手術記錄、填偏差報告、追蹤恢復狀況。「緊急」改變的是時序，不是文件化的義務。

補丁相容性困境 Compatibility Dilemma

當關鍵安全補丁無法安裝（因系統版本太舊或應用程式不相容），選項包括：

  • 程序性控制（Procedural Controls）：限制網路存取、加強監控、限制使用者操作
  • 網路隔離（Isolation）：將系統從企業網路斷開，降低攻擊面

這兩個選項都必須透過風險評估文件化，並在 CAPA 中追蹤長期解決方案。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. Microsoft 宣布一個嚴重漏洞，影響你 CDMO 所有 Windows Server，但補丁與現有 LIMS 版本不相容。你會如何分類此補丁的緊急程度，並採取什麼臨時措施？
  2. Emergency Fix 的「事後變更控制」最晚應在幾天內完成？請討論合理的期限設定原則。
Appendix 7 — Upgrade and Patch Management (p91–p94)

原文內容 Original Text

1. Fundamental Principles

Regardless of the criticality of an upgrade, the following aspects should be considered:

  • Change Control: Change control documentation should be raised to cover application of the upgrade/fix. For emergency changes, this may be retrospective (but within a minimum period of time following application).
  • Configuration Management: Records should be maintained; documentation recording versions and patch levels of platforms should be accurately maintained. For emergency changes, documentation may be retrospectively updated.
  • Communication: All owners of critical applications should be made aware of the requirement for an upgrade prior to its application.
  • Incident Monitoring: An incident monitoring process should be in place. Where emergency changes are applied with minimal or no specific application testing, particular attention should be given to incident monitoring and reporting.

2. Upgrade Strategy

The upgrade strategy should be based on a technical assessment and an impact assessment:

  • The IT group should perform a technical assessment: whether the upgrade is minor, medium, or major based on complexity and possible impact on applications.
  • All owners of critical applications should perform an impact assessment on their systems.

Issues can arise when implementing patches to platforms where the base application and/or operating system have not been upgraded for an extended period and lag behind the current version. Installation of an emergency upgrade may be compromised — resulting in either the application being unable to run or the patch being unable to be applied.

Systems that have been removed from operational use but retained as read-only systems for record/data retrieval (partially decommissioned) may present issues, particularly where product support is no longer available. Consideration should be given to isolating or segregating such systems.

3. Level of Application Testing

Four general levels of testing that may be applied to applications following a platform upgrade:

  1. No Testing
  2. Confirmation Testing: A minimal level of documented testing to verify that an application runs on an updated platform.
  3. Confidence Testing: Documented testing against pre-defined specifications that consist of a representative subset of functional tests on the updated platform.
  4. Full Testing: Full regression testing of the application on the updated platform.

For emergency changes (e.g., critical security update), it is likely that no prospective testing will be applied. For business critical and GxP applications, enhanced incident monitoring should be applied, and a documented justification made until retrospective testing or final impact evaluation is completed.

Where the update is not an emergency: minor updates → Confirmation Testing only may be appropriate; significant updates or highly critical GxP systems → Confidence Testing as minimum; major updates with likely application impact → Full regression testing.

The two-stage Risk Assessment process from GAMP 4 (assessing impact of failure, likelihood of failure, probability of detection) is a good tool for determining appropriate testing level.

4. Global/Multi-Site Systems

For systems used at multiple locations with worldwide standardization of platforms, an efficient approach is to perform testing at a single location and use this as the basis of reduced or no testing at other locations.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：四級應用程式測試層級

Level 1 — No Testing（無測試）：僅限緊急情況，必須搭配強化事件監控和事後測試計畫。絕非「永久免測」。

Level 2 — Confirmation Testing（確認測試）：最低限度文件化測試，驗證應用程式在更新後平台仍能執行。適用：技術評估為「輕微」的升級。

Level 3 — Confidence Testing（信心測試）：以預定規格執行代表性功能子集測試。適用：顯著升級，或高度關鍵 GxP 系統。

Level 4 — Full Testing（完整回歸測試）：全面回歸測試。適用：主要升級且對應用程式有可能造成影響。

測試層級選擇決策矩陣

升級性質     | GxP/關鍵系統？ | 建議測試層級
-------------|----------------|------------------
緊急補丁     | 是/否          | Level 1 + 強化監控
輕微升級     | 否             | Level 2
輕微升級     | 是             | Level 2~3
顯著升級     | 是/否          | Level 3 (最低)
主要升級     | 是             | Level 4

比喻說明 Analogy

四級測試就像汽車出廠前的品質查驗等級：緊急出廠（Level 1）= 只看引擎能不能發動就交車；確認測試（Level 2）= 還會試踩煞車；信心測試（Level 3）= 在測試跑道跑幾圈；完整測試（Level 4）= 全面安全認證測試。交的車越貴、乘客越重要，測試等級越不能省。

重點提示 Key Notes

版本落差陷阱：若系統長期未升級，緊急補丁反而可能無法安裝，或安裝後造成應用程式崩潰。這是 CDMO 常見的技術債——省下的升級維護費用，最終在緊急時刻加倍奉還。

部分退役系統（partially decommissioned）：仍需保留查閱能力的唯讀系統，若原廠已停止支援，網路隔離是必要的風險降低措施，不是可選項。

多廠區系統：在一個廠址完整測試後，其他廠址可以減少測試——但這需要在策略文件中明確規定，並有標準化平台作為前提。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的 CDMO 有三個廠區共用同一 ERP 系統，IT 在總部測試了一個 OS 升級。其他兩個廠區應該做哪個層級的測試？需要什麼文件支持這個決策？
  2. 若 MES 系統供應商宣布某版本將於 6 個月後停止安全補丁支援，你會如何制定升級策略？按本附錄的邏輯寫出行動步驟。
Appendix 8 — Outsourcing (p95–p99)

原文內容 Original Text

1. Definition of Responsibilities

Outsourcing involves the transfer of management and operations of a company's IT Infrastructure to an external company. Scope includes: operation of a data center and/or networks; operation of systems and/or processes (e.g., Help Desk); hardware/software component build (e.g., workstation).

The contracted service provider may have staff located on the regulated company's premises or provide services from a remote location (if on a different continent, 'offshoring' is sometimes used).

"The regulated company remains responsible for the regulatory compliance of their IT operations regardless of whether they choose to outsource/offshore some or their entire IT Infrastructure processes to external service provider(s). Compliance oversight and approvals cannot be delegated to the outsource partner."

The external service provider should focus on: regulatory education (all staff understand compliance impact); creation and maintenance of SOPs and work instructions; creation and maintenance of quality records; QA and QC of their IT processes.

2. Special Considerations

The location from which the outsourcing company provides services should be assessed. Services on-site should be managed per the company's standard security processes. Services from outside the regulated company's boundaries may require additional controls (e.g., for remote management of a data centre or a Help Desk).

3. Contracts

The regulated company is responsible for interpreting GxP regulations and defining appropriate requirements for the IT Infrastructure, provided to the external service provider in IT industry best practice terminology.

Key Performance Indicators (KPIs) and acceptance criteria should be defined by the regulated company. Contracts should handle ownership and retention of documents and records — if a contract is ended, the regulated company needs access to those documents or records at a later date.

Contracts should clearly state conditions under which the regulated company or regulators can undertake on-site audits to verify conformance. Expert support required on site to facilitate inspections, agreed notifications, and alert levels also should be specified.

4. Service Level Agreements

Where services are requested by one organization and provided by another, a formal SLA should be established. An SLA will usually be included as part of a contract and clearly state KPIs and associated fees.

A typical SLA will specify:

  • contacts on either side
  • duration of validity and circumstances triggering reviews
  • pre-requisites and customer deliverables or involvement
  • scope and nature of required services
  • metrics in the form of KPIs
  • records demonstrating fulfillment of specified service levels
  • pricing arrangements, including penalties for shortcomings
  • reports, scope, frequency, distribution
  • audit provisions, including readiness to facilitate inspections from regulatory authorities

5. Audits

Before entering into an outsourcing arrangement, a supplier audit should be considered. Staff from the regulated company's QA should be allowed to repeat initial audits at suitable intervals or if conditions warrant investigation.

The regulated company is responsible for authorizing appropriate resolution or mitigation of non-compliance areas arising from audits. The regulated company should include tracking of these within its CAPA program.

A non-disclosure agreement should be entered with the supplier to specify what information may and may not be shared.

6. Training Requirements

Regulations require that personnel have the appropriate combination of education, training, and experience. This applies to external supplier personnel as well. The service provider should ensure their staff is trained in regulatory compliance. Such training should be documented.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

重點提示：合規監督責任不可委外

這是本附錄最關鍵的原則。無論 IT 系統由哪家供應商管理，法規責任永遠在受管制公司身上。就像藥廠委外生產，受託方（CMO）執行製造，但合規責任仍在委託方（MAH）。

對 CDMO 的實際意涵：即便 IT 基礎設施完全委外給 AWS 或本地資服公司，FDA/EMA 稽查時，你仍需要能展示對供應商的有效監督——包括稽查紀錄、KPI 追蹤、CAPA 執行。「供應商說他們做了」不是合格答案。

比喻說明 Analogy

委外 IT 就像餐廳外包食材供應。廚師（受管制公司）對菜品安全負責，即使食材是供應商送來的。合約定義食材規格（KPI），定期稽查供應商的廚房（Supplier Audit），食材抵達時要驗貨（入廠查核）。若食材出問題，顧客告的是餐廳，不是供應商。

SLA 必要元素清單 SLA Essential Elements

合規相關必要項目（稽查重點）：
1. KPIs 與接受標準（量化績效指標）
2. 稽查權利條款（含法規機關現場稽查）
3. 記錄保存所有權（合約結束後仍可取得）
4. 事故通報等級與時效（Alert Levels）
5. 培訓要求（供應商人員需受 GxP 訓練）
6. 不合規時的處理程序與罰則

核心概念：記錄保存所有權

合約必須明確規定：若終止合約，受管制公司仍可存取所有 GxP 相關記錄。這在實務中常被忽略，直到供應商倒閉或合約到期才發現記錄被「鎖住」，無法配合稽查——這是嚴重的合規風險。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 委外雲端基礎設施給 AWS / Azure 時，必須在合約中明確：

  • FDA 稽查人員能否要求現場查核雲端服務商的資料中心？（需寫入合約）
  • CDMO 離開雲端平台時，所有 GxP 記錄如何移轉？格式？時限？
  • 雲端供應商的安全事件通報義務（多少小時內必須告知客戶）？

這些都是合約談判時必須確認的項目，不是上線後再想。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的 IT 供應商系統發生資料外洩事件，稽查員問你「你如何驗證供應商的合規性？」你能拿出哪些文件？
  2. SLA 中的 KPI 應包含哪些具體指標？請為 CDMO 的 MES 雲端服務設計至少三個 GxP 相關 KPI。
Appendix 9 — Server Management (p99–p105)

原文內容 Original Text

1. Introduction

The objective of the Server Management process is to ensure that specified requirements for operational availability, performance, and security are consistently fulfilled by the server. An important part of the process is to manage server configuration and changes needed to meet the objectives.

All quantitative measures provided in this Appendix are derived from actual situations and are meant to assist companies, not to prescribe absolutes.

2. Backup and Restore

Failures of computer systems may result in a loss of data. The backup of electronic data is consequently essential to preserve the integrity and availability of the data.

2.1 Backup

There are two main types of backup:

  • Full backup: a copy of all data on a given system
  • Incremental/differential backup: a copy of data that has changed since the last backup cycle

The following minimum requirements are recommended:

  • Full backup: once per week, one day per week
  • Incremental or differential: all other days

Backups should be monitored to ensure successful completion:

  • review of backup logs to ensure successful completion
  • proactive assessments conducted regularly to ensure all required systems are included
  • backup media management

2.2 Verification

An extensive verification of the backup should be made when data is considered critical for the business, although the quantity of data may prevent full verification from being performed.

2.3 Schedules

The type of data should largely dictate backup schedules. Enterprise-level data actively in use can be considered to be changing each working day, with backup normally taking place overnight. Defining the schedule for global systems requires careful consideration, as access by users from other locations may create conflicts. Certain application data files cannot usually be backed up while in use — backup schedules may require augmented processes coordinating with deactivation of applications.

2.4 Restore

When a restore request is received, consideration should be given to whether the person requesting the restore is authorized, and that they are authorized to view the data being restored. When restoring data, checks should be made to ensure that more recent versions of files being restored are not overwritten, unless specifically requested. Consideration should be given to enable recovery to the point of failure.

Restoration beyond clearly defined single records or files may pose a challenge in assuring that all related records are brought back to the same state or point in time to retain overall integrity. This can be achieved only through carefully planned interactions with the system/data owner representatives.

2.5 Storage

A process for protecting backup data should be established to prevent loss, damage, and unauthorized access. Controls include:

  • secure storage facilities with proper access controls and environmental conditions
  • indexing and labeling capabilities and means to timely retrieval during inspections
  • detecting the end of retention requirements and notifying data owner
  • ensuring changes are carried out under change control
  • securely destroying data given necessary authorization

Although manufacturers give an expected lifetime for media, the expected lifetime when containing data is considerably less. Provisions should be made to refresh data after a defined period.

To ensure ability to recover data in a disaster, backup media should be stored at a secure 'off-site' facility — geographically diverse from the location where the system is housed.

2.6 Testing

The requirement to test the backup process should encompass any off-site storage solutions. The test should aim to restore data from historical backups, which may require handling of off-site backups. Restoring actual backups and comparing against the unchanged original file, where possible, gives the opportunity to check that the whole data path maintains data integrity. This periodic activity may certify both the backup and restore procedures.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：全量 vs. 增量備份策略

Full Backup（全量備份）：每週一次，備份所有資料。優點：還原簡單。缺點：時間長、佔空間。

Incremental Backup（增量備份）：每日，只備份自上次備份後變更的資料。優點：快速、省空間。缺點：還原需要依序合併多個備份。

GxP 最低要求：全量每週一次 + 增量每日。這不是建議，是底線。

比喻說明 Analogy

備份策略就像工廠的照片記錄：每個月拍一次全廠大合照（全量備份），每天記錄今天哪裡有什麼變化（增量備份）。出事時，先找最近那張大合照，再依序套上之後每天的變化，就能還原到事故當天的狀態。

異地儲存就像把大合照的副本存在另一棟建築——同棟著火時，備份還能倖存。

重點提示 Key Notes

備份記錄的查核不等於測試還原：光看 backup log 顯示「成功」不夠。GxP 要求定期實際執行還原測試，並驗證還原後的資料與原始資料一致。「能備份」和「能還原」是兩件事。

還原授權管控：資料還原操作必須驗證申請人身份及其查看資料的授權。在 21 CFR Part 11 系統中，未授權還原等同於未授權資料存取。

媒體壽命陷阱：廠商標示的媒體壽命是空白媒體壽命，含資料的實際壽命遠較短。必須建立定期資料刷新（data refresh）計畫，避免長期備份資料自然損壞。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. CDMO 的批次記錄系統週五晚上崩潰。使用週一全量備份 + 週二至週四增量備份，能否完整還原週四所有資料？還原順序是什麼？
  2. 稽查員詢問：「你如何確認備份的 GxP 記錄在異地儲存設施中仍可讀取？」你的標準作業程序應包含哪些驗證步驟？

原文內容 Original Text

3. Technical Performance and Capacity Monitoring

The performance of devices and services need to be monitored to ensure that stated or implied expectations can be achieved. Review results or alarms will trigger maintenance, update, support, or disaster recovery activities.

Surveillance procedures should be developed and alert and action limits defined. For time-critical systems, the platform manager should ensure enough reserve resources to meet surges in demand.

Table A9.1 lists sample performance metrics for a process control server, as an aid in deciding metrics and limits in the context of all relevant deciding factors.

Table A9.1: Example Server Performance Limits
Server Metrics Unit Alert Limit (Real-time system) Action Limit
CPU load % >60 * >80 *
Server Work Queue # >2 >4
Available primary memory MB <50 * <10 *
Memory swaps Pages/sec >15 >20
Physical memory (disk space) % disk access time >60 >80
Physical memory queue length # >2 ** >4 **
Network interface kB total/sec >50 *** >80 ***

* Very much dependent on actual system set-up
** Depends on disk array configuration
*** Depends on application and network topology

Monitoring should take place on a daily basis using applicable software tools. A baseline should be created at the time of installation, and actual values should be considered based on those readings.

When using complex Process/System Management Applications, monitoring and event reaction could be automated.

4. Remote Management

When servers are remotely managed, e.g., via outsourcing or offshoring arrangements, it is important to maintain the required level of security. Consideration should be given to the use of secure communication channels.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：Alert Limit vs. Action Limit

Alert Limit（警戒限）：系統開始發出警報，但尚未到達必須立即行動的程度。對應製造環境的環境監控警戒限——需要調查，評估是否趨近行動限。

Action Limit（行動限）：必須立即採取糾正措施，如重啟服務、擴充資源、啟動災難恢復程序。對應環境監控的行動限——超過即觸發 CAPA。

這個雙層限制結構（Alert → Action）與 GxP 製造中的 OOT / OOS 處理邏輯完全一致，對 CDMO 人員來說是熟悉的概念框架。

重點提示 Table A9.1 解讀

表中數值僅供參考（非絕對規定），應在系統安裝時建立基準線（Baseline），再依實際環境調整限制值。

對即時系統（Real-time system，如製程控制伺服器）而言，CPU >80% 或可用記憶體 <10 MB 是必須立即行動的警號——因為延遲回應直接影響製程控制，進而影響產品品質。

每日監控 + 自動化警報是合規要求，不是選擇。監控記錄本身就是 GxP 文件。

比喻說明 Analogy

伺服器效能監控就像無塵室的環境監控系統：設定警戒限和行動限，持續即時記錄，超標自動發警報，必須有 SOP 規定超標時的應對程序，且所有記錄都要保存以供稽查。兩者邏輯完全相同，只是監控對象從粒子計數換成了 CPU 使用率。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 遠端管理伺服器（例如總部 IT 管理分散在各廠的系統）時，安全要求包括：

  • 使用加密通訊通道（如 VPN、SSH）——非加密的遠端存取是重大安全漏洞
  • 遠端存取本身也需要存取控制記錄（WHO、WHEN、WHAT）
  • 若透過委外供應商遠端管理，合約中必須明確規定安全通訊標準

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 稽查員要求查看過去 6 個月的伺服器效能監控記錄，以確認 MES 系統在批次生產期間的可用性。你的 IT 部門應提供哪些文件？記錄格式應如何設計才符合 GxP？
  2. 若 IT 供應商透過網際網路遠端管理你的 GxP 伺服器，你需要在合約和技術層面做哪些確認才能符合本附錄的安全要求？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • 附錄六 CIA 三角：機密性／完整性／可用性是 GxP IT 資安的三大支柱，ISO/IEC 17799 是框架基礎，不需正式認證但需映射至內部政策並完成內稽。
  • 附錄六 補丁分類：三種緊急程度（Emergency Fix / Urgent Update / Update）決定行動時序；緊急補丁可事後補做變更控制，但不能省略文件化義務。
  • 附錄七 測試四級：No Testing（僅緊急）→ Confirmation（輕微升級）→ Confidence（顯著升級/GxP系統）→ Full Regression（主要升級）；多廠區可集中測試後減少其他廠區測試量。
  • 附錄八 委外原則：合規監督責任永遠在受管制公司，不可委派給供應商；SLA 必須包含 KPI、稽查權利、記錄保存所有權三大合規要素。
  • 附錄九 備份策略：全量（每週）＋增量（每日）是最低要求；異地儲存確保災難恢復；定期實際執行還原測試才能真正驗證備份有效性；效能監控採 Alert/Action 雙層限制，每日記錄並自動警報。
7

Chapter 7: Appendices 10–13: Networks, Glossary & References

附錄10-13：網路管理、術語表與參考資料 | App 10-13

ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guide: IT Infrastructure Control and Compliance | App. 10–13 (p106–p126)

本章學習目標

  • 區分三種用戶端類型（非限制／限制／受控），理解 GxP 環境為何需要「受控 PC」
  • 了解標準化映像檔部署如何降低資格確認負擔，同時確保一致性
  • 掌握網路運作中心（NOC）的職責與 SLA 監控機制
  • 認識 SNMP、Syslog、RMON 三種網路協議的功能及 GxP 合規應用
  • 熟悉 App. 12 術語表中的關鍵概念區分：評估 vs. 稽核、資格確認 vs. 驗證
  • 了解本指南核心參考文獻的層次：GAMP 4 為基礎，PIC/S 與 ISO 17799 為安全基準
Appendix 10 — Client Management（用戶端管理）

原文內容 Original Text — App. 10 §1 Client Types

Personal Computers (PCs) in the form of stationary PC units, laptops, or 'hand-helds' are used by companies in a variety of roles with distinctly different risk profiles depending upon their use. Those that are connected to the company's network may be prepared and maintained according to a set of client types, e.g., unrestricted, restricted, or controlled as described in Section 5 of this Guide.

As part of the client preparation process, companies may choose to prepare and verify installation scripts, or use an image-generating tool, which mirrors an image of a released software configuration onto PCs.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：三種用戶端類型

Unrestricted PC（非限制型）：使用者可自由安裝軟體、修改設定。適用於一般行政辦公場景，風險較低。

Restricted PC（限制型）：限制部分操作，例如不允許安裝未核准軟體。適用於非直接 GxP 環境。

Controlled PC（受控型）：完全鎖定——使用者無法修改設定、安裝任何軟體。GxP 應用通常要求此類型，因為必須保證資料完整性，符合 21 CFR Part 11 的電子記錄要求。

重點提示 — 為何 GxP 要求受控 PC？

21 CFR Part 11 要求電子記錄不能被未授權方式修改。若使用者能自行更改 PC 設定或安裝非核准軟體，就無法保證資料的準確性與可追溯性。「受控 PC」等同於在電子記錄鏈中插入了一道防火牆。

比喻說明

想像醫院手術室（受控）vs. 護理站（限制）vs. 行政辦公室（非限制）。進入手術室的設備必須完全符合規範，任何未經授權的器械都不得帶入——GxP PC 也一樣。

原文內容 Original Text — App. 10 §2 Client Management

The Client Management group or designated individual maintains the expertise and resources required to provide adequate client management services to the company. Some of the main responsibilities of the unit are:

  • to acquire formal approval by QA and management representatives of significant changes
  • to apply change controls in conformance with procedures (see Section 6 and Appendix 7 of this Guide)
  • to maintain controlled standards for approved hardware and software components, and settings in conformance with security requirements and IT Code of Conduct
  • to test PC platforms and corporate office packages to ensure an effective and stable client user environment
  • to test or qualify clients against all corporate applications
  • to provide and verify installation images or scripts conforming to standards to enable cloning of clients
  • to detect and correct errors in both hardware and software
  • to assemble documents and installation manuals
  • to advise and instruct client supporters and others
  • to install security patches on clients
  • to scan all standard clients for virus
  • to ensure timely update of anti-virus software and signature files
  • to administrate centralized maintenance processes
  • receipt and registration of all IT equipment
  • to manage system time (if not managed by servers)
  • installation and set-up of standard clients
  • before delivery of the PC or other equipment, to conduct prescribed tests to ensure that all installation and configuration matters are in order
  • to implement handling of used hardware for recycling
  • to provide User support
  • to provide a general contact to suppliers

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：用戶端管理群組的雙重職責

Client Management Group 同時扮演兩個角色：

  • 技術維運角色：安裝、測試、修補漏洞、防毒掃描
  • 合規角色：取得 QA 核准、執行變更控制、維護文件

這兩個職責的結合，使其成為 IT GxP 合規架構中的關鍵節點。

重點提示 — 系統時間管理

列表中看似平凡的一項——「管理系統時間」——在 GxP 環境極為重要。電子記錄的時間戳記必須準確，否則批次記錄的時序無法被稽核員信任。若 PC 時鐘偏移，可能使整批次記錄受質疑。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若一台受控 PC 上的使用者自行安裝了未核准的辦公軟體，哪些 GxP 風險會被觸發？
  2. Client Management Group 在執行安全性修補程式前，為何需要先取得 QA 核准？

原文內容 Original Text — App. 10 §3–5 Platforms & User Modifications

3 PC Platforms

PCs should possess enough computing power and connectivity to run the client software and other software that is required by the applications. The company will usually have some basic requirements for specific hardware as a result of long term commercial agreements with specific suppliers. Care should be taken to ensure that the chosen PC brands conform to standards for protection against Radio Frequency Interference (RFI) and Electromagnetic Compatibility (EMC) and other applicable codes.

4 Operating System Platform

Client modifications may be managed centrally by the Client Management Group or locally by the user or a local administrator. Modifications to a set of clients have a greater risk level than modifications to a single instance. All modifications should be managed carefully according to SOPs.

As is the case for servers, the configuration of critical items of the client operating system can be grouped into three categories:

  • manufacturer supplied default parameters that remain unchanged
  • Manufacturer supplied default parameters that will be altered to address specific company requirements for the client; these may be changed later during the client life time to optimize performance
  • parameters that are supplied blank, and should be populated by the company, and without which the client may not work

5 User Modifications

Company policies may dictate whether clients should be restricted from user modification (see Section 5 of this Guide). Many applications, especially those that are GxP regulated, will require that PCs running thick client software be restricted, or even controlled in order to obtain the necessary confidence that data is not lost or modified in an unauthorized way.

PCs running thin client software are less prone to causing data modifications or availability problems, e.g., when using Web-based client technology.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：OS 組態的三類參數

這三類劃分也適用於伺服器，是 Configuration Management（組態管理）的基礎框架：

  • 預設不變參數：廠商設定，維持原狀
  • 調整型參數：為公司需求修改，需記錄原始值與修改原因
  • 空白待填參數：公司必須主動填入，否則系統無法運作

每次變更任何一類，都必須透過正式變更控制流程。

比喻說明 — Thick vs. Thin Client

Thick Client（厚用戶端）像是自帶廚房的餐廳包廂——食材、烹調都在現場，改動容易影響整體。Thin Client（薄用戶端）像是只有桌椅的外賣取餐點——核心處理全在廚房（伺服器端），本地端幾乎沒有可動手腳的地方，GxP 風險自然較低。

重點提示 — EMC/RFI 在製藥廠的重要性

製藥廠的生產環境中往往有大型馬達、高頻設備，會產生電磁干擾。未符合 EMC 標準的 PC 可能出現資料錯誤或系統當機，直接影響批次記錄完整性。

原文內容 Original Text — App. 10 §6–7 Images & Patch Management

6 Images or Installation Scripts

Client management often includes the creation and maintenance of images or standard installation scripts or both. This ensures easier management of client preparation processes and demonstration of control.

Besides the operating system and standard office packages, an image could include the company's most used client software rendering subsequent requests for installations unnecessary. This approach would improve reinstallation time, but require more time supporting the image, and although user accounts would not be created on a default basis, security policies could be violated.

Before an image can be released for use, it should be tested against the relevant applications and hardware used in the company.

7 Patch Management

Security patches to be installed on clients should be tested for compatibility with the operating system, office software packages, and client software. A test lab with instances of the hardware and software used in the company should be available, and pilot installations in a no-impact live environment should be made as part of the qualification plan. This should discover potential problems with the patch in the live environment before general rollout.

Besides test requirements, security patch information from the supplier should be made available to the organization. This will ensure awareness of the process and allow owners of critical business applications outside the scope of the PC management group to conduct tests before rollout (see Appendix 6 of this Guide).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：映像檔部署的合規優勢

映像檔（Image）是一個已經通過測試的完整系統快照。部署到新 PC 時，每台電腦的起始狀態完全一致，大幅降低「每台 PC 都需要個別資格確認」的工作量。這就是「資格確認重用（Qualification Reuse）」的概念——同一份 IQ/OQ 記錄，可以涵蓋所有由同一映像檔建立的 PC。

重點提示 — 修補程式管理的 GxP 風險

安全修補程式有時會改變系統行為，導致已驗證的 GxP 應用程式出現問題。正確的流程是：
測試實驗室驗證 → 試點部署 → 全面推送
跳過任何步驟都可能讓已驗證系統的狀態失效（out of validated state），需要啟動重新驗證程序。

比喻說明 — 映像檔 vs. 逐台安裝

映像檔部署就像連鎖餐廳的中央廚房出品——所有分店的醬汁配方完全一致，品質可預期。逐台手動安裝則像每家分店各自熬製醬汁——難以保證一致性，稽核時也說不清楚「哪台 PC 安裝了什麼」。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個已核准的映像檔，如果加入了新軟體，需要經過哪些步驟才能再次發布使用？
  2. 為什麼安全修補程式需要在「不影響生產的環境」中先行試點，而不能直接推送？
Appendix 11 — Network Management（網路管理）

原文內容 Original Text — App. 11 §1–3 Introduction & Goal

1 Introduction

The current dominating network technology is based on internet standards, including the protocols: Internet Protocol (IP) and Transmission Control Protocol (TCP). Consequently, this Appendix focuses on providing recommendations based on those standards.

All quantitative measures provided in this Appendix are derived from actual situations and are meant to assist companies, and not to prescribe certain absolutes.

2 Goal

The goal of network management is to identify and employ a variety of tools, applications, and devices to assist managers in monitoring and maintaining network performance in support of other platforms and services.

3 Network Management

When establishing the infrastructure network management process, the network administrator should break down the work process into logically separated steps:

Provisioning and Installation:

  • Planning
  • Design
  • Analysis
  • Facilities Installation and Maintenance
  • Network Installation
  • Data Gathering and Analysis

Operations and Maintenance (Network Operations Center / NOC):

  • Upgrades
  • Event/Log Management
  • Fault Management/Service Restoration
  • Change Management
  • Configuration Management
  • Performance Management
  • Security Management
  • Account Management
  • Report Management

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：網路管理的兩大階段

本節將網路管理活動清楚分為兩個階段：

  • 佈建與安裝（Provisioning）：一次性的規劃、設計、安裝工作
  • 運維（Operations）：持續性的日常管理，由 NOC 主導

從 GxP 合規角度，「運維」階段是最關鍵的——因為它關係到系統是否持續處於受控狀態（maintained in a controlled state）。

重點提示 — 量化指標僅供參考

本附錄特別聲明：所提供的數值來自實際案例，僅作指導，並非強制標準。公司應依據自身業務規模、網路架構與 GxP 風險評估，制定適合自己的 SLA 指標。

比喻說明 — NOC 的角色

NOC（網路運作中心）就像機場的塔台管制中心——所有飛機（資料封包）的起降（傳輸）都在監控範圍內，任何異常立即通報，確保飛行安全（系統可用性）不中斷。

原文內容 Original Text — App. 11 §4–5 Provisioning & NOC

4 Network Provisioning and Installation

Network provisioning involves the following tasks:

  • Network planning and design is the responsibility of the network engineering group which keeps track of new technologies and introduces them as needed in conformance with applicable standards and company requirements.
  • Identification of bottlenecks through analysis of traffic and performance data provided by the Network Operation Center (NOC) and introduction of modifications to the network to optimize the use of the equipment.
  • Keeping track of new network management tools and introducing them where they would be efficient for gathering statistics and showing trends of traffic patterns for tuning and planning purposes.

5 Network Operation Center (NOC)

The function of the NOC, typically headed by the overall network administrator, is to assume responsibility for the daily operation of the network. The responsibility of the NOC is to provide network services in conformance with SLAs and other applicable requirements and standards, this includes:

  • establishing a network management system, e.g., based on SNMP
  • ensuring that the gathering of data for performance, tuning, and accounting purposes is functioning and kept current
  • restoration of faulty services
  • analyzing logs and assuring that all manageable network devices respond as required, e.g., via Syslog
  • assuring that there are current and easily available configuration backups of all network equipment as well as a documented trace of all configuration changes
  • providing management with reports and statistics (KPIs) to ensure that the network is performing optimally and the SLAs are within the agreed limits
  • ensuring that approved security procedures are followed by tracking all network accesses and by securing that only permitted access to the network is allowed
  • applying tools and procedures to ensure that the availability (defined by different parameters such as latency, bandwidth, and availability) is maintained by analyzing trends, planning upgrades, performing preventive maintenance, and fault correction

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：NOC 的六大核心職能

  • 監控（Monitoring）：即時掌握網路狀態
  • 記錄分析（Log Analysis）：Syslog 匯集，追蹤異常
  • 組態備份（Config Backup）：所有設備設定均有備份與變更紀錄
  • KPI 報告（Reporting）：定期提供 SLA 達成率給管理層
  • 安全存取控制（Access Control）：追蹤所有網路存取
  • 故障恢復（Fault Recovery）：快速復原服務，降低停機時間

重點提示 — GxP 角度下的組態備份

「具備所有網路設備的最新組態備份，以及所有組態變更的文件化追蹤」——這句話直接對應 GxP 的組態管理要求。稽核員可能會要求查看：某台路由器去年何時做了什麼設定變更、由誰核准、備份在哪裡。NOC 若無法回答，即視為合規缺陷。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. NOC 的 SLA 報告應包含哪些關鍵指標才能讓 QA 滿意？
  2. 若一台核心網路交換機的組態遭到未授權修改，NOC 應如何察覺並回應？

原文內容 Original Text — App. 11 §6 Common Network Protocols

6.1 Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP/RFC1157)

Network management system contains two primary elements:

  1. Manager
  2. Agents

The manager is the console through which the network administrator performs network management functions, often accompanied by data management systems to store configuration information, logs of alarms/alerts ('traps' in SNMP context), and performance data history.

Agents are the entities that interface to the actual device being managed. Bridges, hubs, routers, or network servers are examples of managed devices that contain managed objects.

SNMP allows managers and agents to communicate for the purpose of accessing these objects. The SNMP has become the de facto standard for internet work management. Because it is a simple solution, requiring little code to implement, suppliers can easily build SNMP agents into their products. SNMP also separates the management architecture from the architecture of the hardware devices, which broadens the base of multi-supplier support.

6.2 Syslog (RFC3164)

This protocol has been used for the transmission of event notification messages across networks for many years. Its value to operations and management has led it to be ported to many other operating systems as well as being embedded into many other networked devices.

In its most simplistic terms, the Syslog protocol provides a transport to allow a machine to send event notification messages across IP networks to event message collectors, also known as Syslog servers.

One of the fundamental tenets of the Syslog protocol and process is its simplicity. No stringent coordination is required between the transmitters and the receivers. There are usually many devices sending messages to relatively fewer collectors. This compilation process allows an administrator to aggregate messages into relatively few repositories.

6.3 Remote Monitoring (RMON) (RFC 1757)

Remote network monitoring devices, often called monitors or probes, are instruments that exist for the purpose of managing and/or monitoring a network. A company may employ many of these devices, up to one per network segment, to manage its networks.

RMON also appears as a software capability that is added to the software of certain network equipment, as well as software applications that could run on servers or clients. Despite the variety of these approaches, the RMON capability serves as a dedicated network management resource available for activities ranging from long-term data collection and analysis or for ad-hoc fire fighting.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：三大網路協議速覽

SNMP（簡單網路管理協議）：主動查詢設備狀態。Manager 向 Agents 發出查詢，取得路由器、交換機等設備的運行參數（CPU 使用率、錯誤計數等）。設備異常時，Agent 主動發出「Trap（警報）」通知 Manager。

Syslog（系統日誌協議）：被動收集事件訊息。各設備將自身的事件日誌傳送至中央 Syslog 伺服器，管理員可一站式查閱所有設備的異常記錄。

RMON（遠端監控）：針對網路流量本身的深度分析。可部署至每個網路區段，長期收集封包層級的統計資料，用於趨勢分析與問題排查。

三種協議的功能比較

SNMP   → 設備狀態管理（Manager ↔ Agent）
         主動查詢 + Trap 警報
         RFC 1157

Syslog → 事件日誌傳輸（設備 → Syslog Server）
         被動彙集，集中儲存
         RFC 3164

RMON   → 網路流量分析（Probe → 分析平台）
         每段網路一個探針
         RFC 1757

重點提示 — GxP 合規中的協議選擇

在 GxP 網路環境中，Syslog 最直接支援審計追蹤（Audit Trail）需求——所有網路事件均有時間戳記並集中儲存，供稽核員查閱。SNMP 則支援 SLA 監控所需的即時效能資料。RMON 適合在懷疑有網路效能問題時進行深度調查。

比喻說明

SNMP 像是護士定時量血壓（主動檢查設備）；Syslog 像是病房的事件記錄本（任何異常自動寫入）；RMON 像是心電圖機（持續記錄細部波形，供需要時回放分析）。

原文內容 Original Text — App. 11 §7 Network Performance Metrics

Table A11.1 represents actual settings for a network segment and may be used as guidance for a company to decide on its own metrics and limits.

Table A11.1: Example Network Performance Limits
Network Metrics Unit Alert Limit Action Limit
Average load over 24 hrs % >10 >20
Peak load % >40 >80
Collision rate % of net time >0.1 >1.0
Discards (lost packages) % of net time >0.1 >0.5
BCast/MCast (simultaneous transmission to many receivers) % of net time >2 >5
Switch CPU-load % of max >50 >70

A monitoring frequency of one to four times a month should be considered; in larger organizations, monitoring would be automated and run almost continuously.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：Alert vs. Action 雙層門檻

表格採用兩層門檻設計：

  • Alert Limit（警示限）：超過此值需記錄並持續觀察，但不一定立即介入
  • Action Limit（行動限）：超過此值必須立即採取矯正措施

這與 GxP 製程監控中的「警戒限／行動限」概念完全一致，是品質管理思維在 IT 基礎設施層面的延伸。

重點提示 — 遺失封包（Discards）在 GxP 的意涵

網路封包遺失不只是效能問題——在 GxP 環境中，若資料傳輸過程中有封包遺失，可能導致電子記錄不完整或時序錯亂。行動限 >0.5% 看起來很小，但在高頻資料採集的場景（如批次製程監控）中，0.5% 的遺失率已可能導致資料缺口。

監控頻率建議

小型組織：每月 1–4 次人工檢查
大型組織：自動化持續監控（接近即時）

建議配置：
  SNMP polling  → 每 5 分鐘
  Syslog        → 即時收集
  RMON 報告     → 每日/每週彙總
  SLA 報告      → 每月提交管理層

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若 Switch CPU-load 連續三天超過 Alert Limit（>50%），你應採取哪些步驟？
  2. 如何向非技術背景的 QA 主管解釋「封包遺失率」與資料完整性的關聯？
Appendix 12 — Glossary（術語表）

原文內容 Original Text — App. 12 §1 Definitions

Term Definition
Assessment Investigation of processes, systems, or platforms by a subject matter expert or by IT Quality and Compliance. An assessment does not need to be independent in contrast to audit.
Audit (ISO/GAMP) Systematic, independent, and documented process for obtaining evidence and evaluating it objectively to determine the extent to which agreed criteria are fulfilled.
Building Block Group of components defined, installed, and controlled by a set of specifications defined by the company to maximize opportunity for re-use.
Certification The process of confirming that a system or component complies with a specific standard (e.g., ISO/IEC 11801). Does not imply involvement of an authoritative body.
Certification Authority (CA) A trusted third-party organization or company that creates and manages digital certificates to distribute public keys and other information.
Change Control (GAMP) A formal process by which qualified representatives from appropriate disciplines review proposed or actual changes to an object. The main objective is to document the changes and ensure that the object is maintained in a state of control.
Client The networked computing device enabling the user to access a client/server system; encompasses desktops, laptops, palmtops. A thick client performs the bulk of data processing locally; a thin client has greater reliance on the server.
Compliance The practice of obeying rules or requests made by people in authority, e.g., adherence to specified standards such as regulations, good practices, SOPs, SLAs, or specified user requirements.
Computerized System All of the computers with their associated hardware, software, and documentation needed to satisfy specific user requirements. Standardized components such as routers and switches are NOT considered computerized systems.
Configuration Management Those activities necessary to precisely define an object at any point during its life cycle.
Disaster Recovery Plan A plan to resume a specific essential operation, function, or process of an enterprise.
Firmware Software (firmly) embedded in hardware components. Despite its name, current technology often permits firmware to be updated post installation.
GxP Application Software entities which have a specific user defined business purpose that must meet the requirements of a GxP regulation.
GxP Regulation The underlying international life science requirements such as the US FD&C Act, US PHS Act, FDA regulations, EU Directives, Japanese MHLW regulations.
Infrastructure Platform The hardware and software which must be present and functioning for an application program to run as intended (e.g., RDBM platforms, network platforms, server hardware platforms).
Logical Access Controls Features embedded in software programs combined with specific settings (Access Control Lists) that are used to authenticate a user requesting access to computerized resources.
Periodic Review (GAMP/PDA) A documented assessment of the documentation, procedures, records, and performance of a computer system to determine whether it is still in a validated state and what actions, if any, are necessary to restore its validated state. Frequency is dependent upon the system's complexity, criticality, and rate of change.
Privileged Access Access to resources or data with the capability of performing administrative tasks (e.g., create, modify, or delete user profiles) in contrast to ordinary end-user access levels.
Qualification Process of demonstrating whether an entity is capable of fulfilling specified requirements. In the context of meeting regulatory requirements, implies adherence to strict documentation requirements, reviews, and approvals.
Quality Assurance (QA) The planned systematic activities necessary to ensure that a component, module, or system conforms to established technical requirements (ISO). The activity of, or group responsible for, ensuring that the facility and systems meet GxP requirements (ISPE).
Risk Assessment Overall process comprising risk analysis (systematic use of available information to identify hazards and estimate risk) and risk evaluation (judgment of whether an acceptable risk level has been achieved). (ISO 14971, modified by GAMP)
Security The protection of computer hardware and software from accidental or malicious access, use, modification, destruction, or disclosure. Also pertains to personnel, data, communications, and physical protection of computer installations.
Testing (IEEE) The process of exercising or evaluating a system or system component by manual or automated means to verify that it satisfies specified requirements or to identify differences between expected and actual results.
Validation (FDA) Establishing documented evidence which provides a high degree of assurance that a specific process will consistently produce a product meeting its pre-determined specifications and quality attributes.
Virus Generic term for all the various types of malicious code that have been designed to breach a company's security measures.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：三組容易混淆的術語

Assessment（評估）vs. Audit（稽核）
最關鍵的差異在於「獨立性」：評估可由內部主題專家執行（不要求獨立）；稽核必須是系統性、獨立且有文件的。一個部門不能稽核自己——但可以自我評估。

Qualification（資格確認）vs. Validation（驗證）
資格確認針對「設備/系統能否達到預期功能」；驗證針對「製程能否持續生產符合規格的產品」。資格確認（IQ/OQ/PQ）通常是驗證的前提條件。

Building Block（建構組件）vs. Computerized System（電腦化系統）
Building Block 是以「最大化重用」為目的設計的標準化組件群；Computerized System 是滿足特定使用者需求的整體系統。路由器、交換機等標準基礎設施組件不被視為 Computerized System，因此其合規要求較輕。

重點提示 — Periodic Review（定期審查）

定期審查的頻率取決於三個因素：複雜性、關鍵性、變更率。GxP 應用系統通常每年執行一次；基礎設施系統可能每兩年一次。審查的目的是確認系統仍處於「已驗證狀態（validated state）」，若發現偏離，必須啟動再驗證。

重點提示 — Privileged Access（特權存取）

特權存取（系統管理員帳號）在 GxP 系統中屬於高風險控制點。任何特權存取操作都應被記錄、核准，並納入定期審查。21 CFR Part 11 要求審計追蹤包括「誰」在「何時」做了「什麼」——特權帳號的操作記錄尤為重要。

比喻說明 — Assessment vs. Audit

評估（Assessment）就像主廚試吃自己餐廳的菜色後記錄改善點；稽核（Audit）就像米其林評審匿名前來，依據標準作客觀評判——前者可以自己做，後者必須來自外部或獨立的人。

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：縮寫背後的重要性分層

這份縮寫表反映了本指南所涉及的多個合規層面，幾個值得特別注意的縮寫：

  • CSV（電腦化系統驗證）：整份指南存在的根本原因，確保電腦化系統符合 GxP 要求
  • IQ / OQ / PQ：資格確認三階段，任何 GxP 系統上線前的必經程序
  • CAPA：矯正預防措施，偏差發生後的正式回應機制
  • IDS：入侵偵測系統，資安控制的重要組件
  • UPS：不斷電系統，GxP 系統可用性保障的硬體基礎

重點提示 — GxP 中的 x

GxP 中的「x」代表 Clinical（臨床）、Distribution（配銷）、Laboratory（實驗室）、Manufacturing（製造）四個領域。作為 CDMO，你的作業橫跨 GMP（製造）與 GLP（實驗室），因此 IT 系統必須同時符合兩者的要求。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個 LIMS 系統同時屬於哪幾個縮寫所代表的範疇（CSV、GxP Application、Computerized System）？
  2. UPS 在 GxP 資料完整性框架中扮演什麼角色？

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：文獻層次架構

這17份參考文獻可以依重要性分為三層：

第一層：製藥行業 GxP 核心文件

  • GAMP 4（文獻1）：整份 ISPE GAMP IT 指南的基礎。所有 IT 系統驗證策略均源於此。即使 GAMP 5 已發布，GAMP 4 仍是本指南寫作時的規範性引用。
  • PIC/S PI011-2（文獻4）：製藥監管機構（如 FDA、EU、TGA）接受的電腦化系統 GxP 最佳實務指引，對 CDMO 出口客戶市場的合規尤為重要。
  • GAMP 電子記錄指南（文獻2）：21 CFR Part 11 合規的具體操作指引。

第二層：資安與組態管理標準

  • ISO/IEC 17799:2000（文獻6）：資訊安全管理的國際基準（現已升版為 ISO/IEC 27002）。GxP 系統的資安控制措施通常參照此標準。
  • ISO 10007:2003（文獻5）：組態管理指引，本指南多次提及的 Configuration Management 實踐依據。
  • NIST SP 800-30（文獻12）：IT 風險管理的量化框架，提供風險評估方法論。

第三層：基礎設施技術標準

  • ISO/IEC 11801（文獻9）：網路佈線標準，附錄10提到的網路認證依據。
  • ITIL（文獻13）：IT 服務管理的最佳實務框架，NOC 運作模式的參考。

重點提示 — GAMP 4 vs. GAMP 5

本指南（ISPE GAMP IT Infrastructure）出版時引用 GAMP 4。GAMP 5 於 2008 年發布，引入了更強的風險評估導向。若今日在 CDMO 執行 IT 系統驗證，應同時參考 GAMP 5 的方法論，但本指南的框架仍然適用——兩者並不衝突。

比喻說明 — 參考文獻的層次

GAMP 4 就像無菌製造的基礎法規（Annex 1）；PIC/S PI011-2 就像官方查廠指引；ISO 17799 就像資安版的 ISO 9000——它們共同構成一個互相支撐的合規框架，缺少任一層都會讓整體架構不完整。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若你的 CDMO 正接受 FDA 查廠，稽核員問及電腦化系統的安全控制依據，你應引用哪幾份文獻？
  2. ISO/IEC 17799 與 NIST SP 800-30 在 IT 風險管理中各負責哪個面向？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • 附錄 10：三種 PC 類型（非限制／限制／受控）決定合規控制程度；GxP 應用需要受控 PC；映像檔部署是降低資格確認負擔的關鍵策略；修補程式必須先在測試環境驗證再推送。
  • 附錄 11：NOC 是網路 GxP 合規的運維核心，負責 SLA 監控、安全存取控制、組態備份與故障恢復；SNMP 管理設備狀態、Syslog 彙集事件日誌、RMON 分析流量深度資料。
  • 附錄 12：關鍵術語區分——評估（可由內部執行）vs. 稽核（必須獨立）；資格確認（IQ/OQ/PQ，針對設備能力）vs. 驗證（針對製程一致性）；Building Block 的設計目標是最大化重用。
  • 附錄 13：GAMP 4 是整份指南的基礎性文件；PIC/S PI011-2 是監管機構認可的電腦化系統 GxP 指引；ISO/IEC 17799 是資訊安全管理基準；NIST SP 800-30 提供 IT 風險評估方法論。
